First Page

॥ Shri Hari ॥

The Fragrant Blossoms of Life

 

tvameva mata cha pita tvameva

tvameva bandhushcha sakha tvameva

tvameva vidya dravidam tvameva

tvameva sarvam mam devadeva

 

Prof. Ramcharan Mahendra

Gita Seva Trust

 

Preface

May our life remain like the fragrant flowers, may our fragrant life be the source of the fragrance of other lives and by the fondling love and the motivation of courage let them stimulate to progress onward. Man has been blessed with the opportunity of a limited and unknown span of life. The fragrance exists in this life only for a very short period; so this life should be spent in the most decent manner. It is not humanity to pass this life in complication, unrest and troubles. If everyone lives one’s own life dedicately and fragrantly by helping others to live a healthy life, then only the goal of human life will be achieved and the divine motive for the creation of the world will be fulfilled; otherwise not.

The human personality is more profound, still and serene than even ocean. It contains genius, sharpness and radiance like the Sun. Its depth and talent are unmeasurable, self-confidence and skill and art. Human being is the highest envolved creature. If his entire potency comes out abruptly, it can create up heaval in the whole world. If so desires, he can enlighten the whole world with enlightenment. The possibility of all around prosperity and progress is present in the human body, mind and soul, but he achieves them by the constant prowess and efforts. We are blessed with the human life so because we may make allround development of our personality and spread our fragrance in all the corners of the whole garden (universe).

Life is struggle, only those who are able to prove the excellence of their prowess and valour get victory. A river succeeds in reaching the sea when it maintains its constant competence to make its flow go ahead dashing against rock¦ The river lacks this competence remains limited like any pond or lake. Where is the opportunity materialise the dream of progress in reality?

A man has to climb on the tall tree of the difficulties to pluck the nectar fruit of success. He has to move on the high peaks of the troubles and miseries of various kinds. Those who lose their patience and courage to see the height, have to return empty-handed. But the heros who challenge the dangers and go on proceeding onward tumbling down the hardships, sufferings and antagonism, obtain a lot of on this very earth. The golden part of the successful eminent persons of the world has bloomed on account of their guts only.

This is the God’s will that we should adopt the various virtues what the Lord, Himself possesses. We should develop in ourselves the divine property what we call morality and humanity. The huge structure of religion and culture has been built so because we may create the faith in our mind impressed by them to live a restrained life of noble conduct. The main motive of theism and divine justice is that ‘man should realize the control of invisible power over him and may not dare to think of doing ill and immoral work even secretly, not only with body but even in thought also.’ Self-restrain is the root of nobility. The self-restrain and self-refinement are necessary so because the man should learn gentility and generosity towards his kins as well as others. This is the royal path to become a social animal in true sense. To follow the rules of sociability is the only way to safeguard the individual and Cosmic prosperity and peace—to maintain to remain progressive only. Self-control is the root of nobility.

Man has formed the society only to enrich his life with pleasures, comforts and means; and not to make his life thorny. When he first started to live having formed a society, he remained constantly prompt for the mutual co-operation. Mostly he used to be unselfish and detached. The feeling of sympathy, compassion and co-existence prevailed in his heart. This was the basic cause of his happy life. It was so when man was not civilized and well educated as today.

Then, what is the reason today when the man is so advanced in his social thought, he is leading his life in such a pitiable and frightened condition? Why has he become so that he is finding out the shortcomings in the humanenss and righteousness? Why are the people of the same society engaged in exploiting and torturing one another?

There is its reason—‘Man’s attitude today has become selfish hoarding.’ Today the man wants to a amass all the objects of the world for himself only. If in the society, the general delight, means prosperity and pleasant circumstances are to be brought, the man today boasting of being cultured, will have to be free from the lust of selfish motive. The allround prosperity and pleasure of all in the whole society is possible only on giving up this lust. It is the selfishness of mankind that has led to the doom of the world.

Man is the architect of his own fate

The Lord has constituted the body, mind and spirit of the mankind very skillfully. Each and every nerve, organ and pulse has been fitted very carefully. He has blessed every organ of this body with unlimited immence power secretly. Well! Our duty is only to know it and develop it patiently. In my opinion, abundance of objects are lying hidden in us to prosper and glorify the life. The wonderful power of courage, vigour, industry, labour, effort, patience and struggle are created by our positive and creative thoughts and we take its advantage in the practical field of our active life. If we don’t pay attention to our hidden talent and spiritual power, we will remain poor, weak being and distressed.

The braves only deserve the enjoyment of earthly enjoyable objects, but the question is to make our life deligent. Nothing will come to our hands if there is no prowess.

Veda has said—

कृतं मे दक्षिणे हस्ते जयो मे सव्य आहित:।

गोजिद् भूयासमश्वजिद् धनंजयो हिरण्यजित्॥

(Atharva. 7/ 50/8)

‘Mankind! Do the valorous acts with your right hand and the success lies in the left hand.’ Amass the wealth of cows, horses, gold and all the other kinds of wealth by your self-efforts and labour.’

It is true that only the lion-hearted men of firm determination and constant striver have brought unique revolutions in the world. The circumstances could not overpower them by any way.

Hardships are the test of your prowess

A valorous man should greet the difficulties instead of giving in before them. They should consider them the honourable chapter of the school of their life. All the progressive minded persons of the world have been educated by the teachings of difficulties. Their minds having been developed by themselves, have been able to expand the knowledge and science to this high limit. If the life remains empty of difficulties, troubles, calamities, hardships and hard labour, man’s life will become completely inactive and full of disappointment.

Well! What is charm of utter disappointed, inactive, and disillusioned life?

Whatever the hue and cry, hustle and bustle in the world, whatever the motion and progress is, whatever the life is that is all due to the protection of the life from the difficulties and to beat them and to fight them.

Greet the difficulties considering them inevitable part and parcel of the progress of life—accept their challenge and overcome them even suffering hundreds of hardships to any kind of calamity. This is your prowess, this is the only way of your success and progress. Difficulties are not your opponents only but they are your friends too; they are the cause to advance you to go ahead on the path of progress. The single blow of disaster changes and improves even the most damaged and spoiled men. The experiences of those men who have been trained in the school of hardships and who have passed through, are invaluable and useful.

Live the life with great zeal

Grow like seed and remain progressing constantly like creeper going higher and higher. Mind it, human life is meant to live the life of exhilaration and enthusiasm.

Generally, everyone lives the life, but is there anyone to say confidently that really he is leading his life properly? I mean by living a life is to lead the life full of elation.

A life in real sense is an enthusiastic life, an optimistic life, lively life. Let us live a life which is not only dear to self rather than it should be fondling and darling to others also, it should be invaluable, ideal and motivational to all and sundry.

But what is the secret art that may make us to live such an exhilarated life? That art is very simple. Neither it requires any penance nor the practice of Yoga. Even in the usual course of life, the art of the life of exhilaration will be proved itself.

That art is to live for others, to live for the poors, downtrodden and weak, to live for the interest of the human beings and the prosperity of humanity, to live for the world sake. When we live for others, our life will be the life of others, all will begin to love him and all the doors of self-contentment will be opened.

The successful life means to live for any goal with a definite strategy. Do the works for others more than you do for yourself. Keep yourself away from the worthless disasterous doings. The more deeply the life is pondered over, the more complicated it will become. Really, the matter of consideration should be why the certain work was done by me? Talk less, do more. This is the best means for success.

Prof. Ramcharan Mahendra

 

Bravo!

When some tread on their way, by the staggering motion of their steps, the earth feels burdensome. When some proceed on their way, due to the seismic inspiration, the path runs calling—‘O the wayfarer! I have extended a red carpet reception in your wait.’

Prof. Ramcharan Mahendra is the wayfarer of the same type. He moved ahead on the path of literature and the success ran after him giving call; because the wonder-box of his literature is not the scent of the sky-blossom or the woman dance of the fancy-copious enjoyment. He has the infallible sight of the judgement of life. His literature is imbued with the throbbing of life, which is not such as the show-piece of book-shelf as whosoever reads it may keep it there in the shelf after reading but the reader remains tempted to assimilate it as many times he reads his literature. Be pleased to read his book ‘Jeevan Ke Mahakate Phul’ (The fragrant blossoms of life) after his books ‘Swarn-Path’; ‘Anandmay Jiwan’, ‘Amrit Ke Ghunt’ ‘Akash Ki Nai Kiran’ ‘Jiwan Me Naya Prakash’ etc., published by ‘Gita Press’ Gorakhpur. Prof. Mahendra’s Pen, which has painted such bright paintings on the canvas of life that create the forceful thrill in the heart and uncontrolled fluttering of lips just to see it, is felicitating—‘Well done!’

From Monthly ‘Naya Jivana’

II Shri Hari II

Peace, prosperity and happiness by spiritual outlook

A saint was enjoying the beauty of nature and flowers sitting in a very cheerful posture in the royal garden of a king. The royal garden had been decorated expensively. Green creeping plants and laughing flowers of different colours, fascinating fragrance, the greenery of grass, cool breezing, and the natural beauty of the water-flow nearby were overwhelming the saint with bliss. Being unconscious of his body and mind in the state of intoxication, he was enjoying the charming beauty of Nature.

This carefree state of bliss of the saint displeased the king. Why should a common man sit without any permission in his garden? He approached the saint in anger and said—‘Do you know whose garden is this?’

The saint remained sitting in the same posture being carefree. The glow of the peace and delight was still glowing on his face as before. He answered—

‘This garden is mine and it is I who am enjoying it.’ Uttering so, expanding and making himself easier, he sat down and went on gazing the pleasant and soothing Nature. The king—‘Don’t you know that this is the royal garden? I am the king, the lord of this state. This is my garden. I have the right over this. Its flowers, creepers, plants, trees and all the other beautiful objects of nature here are mine. Special investment has been made from the royal treasury to enhance my delight. Each and every tree of this garden is invaluable. They have been caused to bring from far and wide. Unlimited royal expenditure has been made to plant and flourish them. Even then, the half naked in ochre coloured clothes and skeleton bodied destitute orphan like you claim of your right on it. The man who is unable to fulfil the common needs of his body and stomach, can ever be the master of this garden?’

The saint remained listening to the arrogant intoxicative speech of the king. Then, defusing his sweet smile he said—

‘O the king! You are failing to enjoy the charming beauty of the green creepers, flowers, plants trees and other objects of this garden so much as much I am enjoying in spite of your abundance of royal means and sources. Even after so much expenditure and lookafter and protection by a number of servants your honour being, unable to equal me in the enjoyment, is the open evidence of the fact that this garden does not belong to you. Here, the beautiful form of Nature is lying open. He, whose sense organs are capable to enjoy its pleasure, whose sensitivity is minute to assimilate the Nature, who can establish identity with Nature with rapt attention, is the lord of this garden. Beauty and delight are the matter of heart. Only the tender-hearted man can enjoy its taste, otherones, who may spend huge money on it, can never be its lord. Beautiful and pleasant objects are really the property of those compassionate persons who get pleasure and delight from them. I am enjoying the charms of this beautiful garden. So, it is mine.

Hearing this the king became thoughtful. The profound truth was hidden in the words of the saint. It was true that he had spent uncountable money in the decoration and nurturing of the garden, In the nursing and collection of the plants he spent lavishly. But he had no immune heart to enjoy the art of the Nature. He used to remain entangled with the numberless worries of the royal affairs even while walking in the garden. In such a beautiful atmosphere of the Nature, the political and diplomatic complications always kept him restless. To walk in the garden was for him just like to settle the problems of royal affairs sitting in the royal assembly. A number of persons presented before him in the royal assembly, and in the garden, all of them used to be seen before his mind. It was equal for him whether the garden was there or not.

Actually, there is hidden a great secret of delight and pleasure in the above mentioned instance. The sentimental feelings of pleasure and beauty are related to our heart. A flower of rose or coloured clouds, rising sun or melodious music, a pleasant painting, which we consider charming, it may be possible that the otherone’s sight may get no charm there and he may not feel pleasant to see it. But if eyes of beauty, the ears worthy of the taste of melodious music and flooded heart with love and compassion belong to you, then, take it granted that you will feel more pleasure in the objects belonging to others than they.

Pleasure and beauty are personal emotions. The subtleness of the feeling of sympathy and enjoying the bliss are individually different. To remain close to any beautiful object does not mean that he is getting pleasure and inspiration from the object in the same proportion as a compassionate man can get.

Contrary to it, a sensitive person can enjoy many objects of others only by the minute observation of his philosophy, the depth of feelings and liberal out look. You may go and enjoy the objects of Nature in the garden of those who plant it. You can enter the splendid state of art and painting by testing the art of paintings, painted in the houses of the men of riches. You can enjoy the melodious music being played on in their houses. You can broaden the scope of your spirit by sharing the joys and sorrows of others. The others children are your own children. Everyone who is related to you is your friend and well-wisher.

In reality the beauty and pleasure are not in the objects. It is in the mind of the person who scans it. The measurement of our pleasure and beauty depends on the height and broadness of our mind. The more refined the taste is, the more compassionate and open the heart is, the more pleasure and beauty he enjoys. It is the outlook of man that gives him pleasure. The worldly and materialistic enjoyments for which, the world beings are restless, have not the least reality of pleasure at all. The real pleasure is in our own inner spirit.

Don’t be distressed to think that you are not owner of big gardens, grand palaces or huge buildings. Just imagine that if these things belonged to you, certainly, you could not shift them anywhere else. Even if you were its master, these things would have been far from you. Only in your mind a self possessive sense would have prevailed that you are the master of these materials and others have no right on them. Considering them as your own only in your imagination, you can be free of the sense of mineness which makes the heart of the owners of these objects narrow.

Considering all the worldly objects as if your own, enjoy them. The Supreme Lord has created each and every object for you only, to absorb your spirit in the pleasure and peace and for your help. The gardens full of greenery, the banks of the rivers flowing with sweet and gentle sound with unlimited exhilaration, the soothing shadow of the trees, flowers, pleasant and cool breezing, public places, temples, Monastery—all belong to you. Consider your own temple where you enter for worship, meditation, devotional songs etc. Suppose you were its lord, how would you maintain its cleanness and beauty, how seriously would you have looked after it and remained careful, you can do so even now. You go to any public inn or any library. Maintain the cleanness of the room of every public inn in which you stay, considering it your own. Read the book or newspaper in a public library so carefully as if your own. Just as you use your own objects very carefully, adopt the same attitude while using them also.

As much identification you have with the public objects, so much pleasure you will feel. By extending the sense of oneness, you will feel the juice of oneness in most of the lifeless objects, animals-birds, flowers-plants, gardens and at public places. Everything is meant for you only. The God has created each and every object only for your sake, you can feel jocund with them—keep this attitude in your mind. Move one step ahead and think that unreal even higher than these enjoyments of unreal world more refined and superior there is an other source of bliss also. That infinite eternal ocean of happiness and pleasure is the bliss of your self-spirit. After entering that universe of soul, one feels the eternal joy and supreme peace. That is such a divine bliss where the death has got no approach. By the dalliance of this supreme enjoyment, we become free from the fear of death and we become immersed in the eternal supreme powerful divinity. On attaining this immutable state, the adverse occurences and circumstances cannot make us ruffled.

Never think that you are destitute, poor and helpless or you are not the owner of so many objects. The want of any object should not be the cause of your worry. There is no question of scarcity in this well-affluent extensive creation of the God. Everywhere there is the abundance of prosperity for you. It may not be today but tomorrow these objects of riches are available to you, it is certain. The victory of abundance over scarcity, nobility over evil the truth over untruth is inevitable. There is no room for narrowness in the creation, it is in your mental outlook itself. In its place, we should contemplate about one’s own colossal expansive soul.

In your soul there is no lack. Expanse is everywhere there. The soul which God has blessed you, whose illumination is observed in the entire creation, that is your soul itself residing within you until a man is conscious of his own soul or has got self-realization, he remains ignorant of his spiritual lustre and his potency. After adopting the spiritual outlook in life there comes a great change in man’s life. He starts realizing the presence of an aspect of his divine soul everywhere. He sees the glimpse of affinity in every man, animal, bird, insect, lifeless objects. He becomes free from narrowness and nobility enters his mind. By adopting the spiritual outlook, it seems to him as if he has come in the celestial light from the darkness or he has awaken from the dream and come in the state of reality. The scarcity of petty objects due to which the worldly men suffer sorrow and pain to the realized soul these very objects appear quite mean, trivial and unsubstantial. The reason is that because of the evolution of his eternal conscious blissful, he remains calm and free from passion, distraction and he abides in the environment of divinity.

There is a very common and short way to attain the spiritual outlook and to remain endowed with the constant happiness to recognise and realize one’s soul and see its shadow in the entire world. We all are in the possession of these divine accomplishments, which are in the Supreme God. Everyone is fully competent to develop his divine spiritual powers having given up the worldliness, sensuousness, jealousy, greed and petty selfishness. I am in reality, the eternal soul, and immortal one. My sense organs are restrained by my mind. I move in the world freely and fearlessly. My soul remains unaffected at all by any external struggle, miseries and oppositions or against references, my soul is not going to be hurt the least. I have surrendered the reign of my mind to the hands of my mind. Selfishness, narrowness, poverty, scarcity—cannot revolt in the state of my spirit. My mind has realized the greatness of the soul. If such thoughts prevail in our mind, we start realizing that the Lord has not kept His sons deprived of any object, which are actually useful for them.

You have endless capabilites. As to the proportion you reveal your capability, abiding in the innersense and you practise the identification of the self with the self of others, you start getting rid of self-created narrowness, to the same proportion your defiled life will be far away from you and your sense organs will start enjoying the happiness of higher rank. Believe in that all the scarcities, all the sins, sorrows, miseries, fear and worldly worries are created by you yourself. Your soul is not in bondage of these. Keep yourself aloof from these, being released from them. Be one with the soul which blesses you with full happiness, supreme bliss and supreme peace.

Your power of love, powers of benevolence, sympathy and pity, kindness and pathos, divine powers of God-devotion in numbers are lying hidden inactive in your innerself. Due to your ignorance you have not developed them. It is only needed to make them active by constant practice and unshakable faith. By virtue of meditation and reflection, there can be reinforced. The meditation of the supreme Lord, the full concentration in Him and remembering Him again and again by muttering, we can increase the powers of our spirit.

Due to their ignorance many people have come to the conclusion that they can never attain, happiness, peace and divinity. Talent, accomplishments and powers are God-gifted oblations. Are you also of the same opinion? If it is so, remove this delusion of your mind at once today itself. The Nature has provided you enough means and capacity. As your spiritual realization and your spiritual attitude develops, so will expand the light of the lamp of knowledge, divine capacity and moral strength also. The momentary worldly pleasures and the darkness of deformatory attachments are destroyed. The fierce disturbance of mind, its constant unstability and dreadful blow of mental tendencies are cooled down. Having got rid of the false worldly creations, false attachments the man attains unobtainable divine capacity.

Realize your self-consciousness. That is your true form of Bliss and Consciousness. That is such a state where there is Supreme Bliss, perfect happiness and Supreme Peace. The spiritual truth is the only means to make you get rid of delusions, ignorance and decisions taken in ignorance. Peace is attained by introverting the traits of mind into it.

On attaining the spiritual sight the diseases, distress, sorrows, scarcity, victory, defeat, repute, humiliation, greed, hunger, joy, sorrow cannot disturb us. They cannot bind the soul in bondage. After realizing Atma nothing else remains to be known.

That what is eternal pleasure, which is present in the entire world in the manifisted form, which spreads the illumination everywhere without any restrain, which blesses us with the sight of foremost supreme sprirt by pulling us from the deep well of darkness, to attain that mental condition is the only spiritual outlook. This is only the supreme stable eternal truth. Merging in the soul the eyes of wisdom get opened and all bondages and lacks get extinct.

आत्मानॸरथिनं विद्धि शरीरॸरथमेव तु।

बुद्धिं तु सारथिं विद्धि मनः प्रग्रहमेव च॥

(Kathopanishad)

‘You! Consider the spirit, the master of chariot, consider this body as the chariot and intellect as the charioteer and considering the mind as rein, live life accordingly.

The same God is hidden in all the beings, is All-pervasive, is the inner soul of all beings, dispenser of fruits of their deeds, the abode of all beings, the witness of all good and evil deeds, All-consciousness, alone and attributeless.

 

Modern life of tension and mental sickness

A clerk gentleman of a very common status somewhat perturbed, came upright to me and begged for Rupees five hundred to borrow. I asked him in amazement—‘Have you settled the marriage of your daughter and managing for it or are you sending your son somewhere else outside in connection with his higher education? What will you do with the money?

Browing beat he said in a loud pitch of voice—‘Oh! What to tell! I have been passing a very perturbed life for three months. My mind is restless and burdensome. My mind remains always heavy with tension?

‘Why? what is the matter?’ I asked him in a soothing voice.

‘The matter is nothing but a triffling and it has become a mountain of mole hill. My neighbouring drunkard dwelling in front of my house clashed with me on a triffling matter. First, he used hot words in passion and then came to blows. It turned to fighting. He has filed a criminal suit against me; but his case is weak. I have engaged a famous lawyer and have been winning the case till now. Enough! How can I eat humble pie before such a below standard man? My prestige is at stake. Now, a little sum of amount will be spent undoubtedly but I will teach him a lesson of humiliation. Well! Please, manage for me by anyway for Rupees five hundred only. Money can be earned, it is earned and spent but it is necessary to teach that wicked a lesson by giving him a blow of defeat.’ While conversing he got excited. His brows got curved and eyes became red.

It was clear that he was bent upon taking the revenge. Even after three months of the event, his agitated and fiery mind had not been cooled down. His mind was full of tension. His mind seemed to be tired and burdened. This tensionised mind is the root of mental ill.

This incidence is of recent past when a man became so mad in wrath that he cut down the nose of his wife, though the cause of his wrath was very simple. His wife used to insist on going to her maternal house off and on. The husband used to remain overpowered with anger. This tension went on increasing and taking root in his mind. UItimately it ended in a terrible result. The husband would have suffered the punishment and the wife became disfigured forever.

Ò Ò Ò Ò

I have a friend. He is a Hindi poet of high rank. He is a professor. There is magic in his pen. He suffers from the problem of sound sleeplessness in the night. He remains changing the sides on the bed. Several times he takes the sleeping drug while going to retire on bed; but the doctor always alerts him of the danger of the intoxicating medicines. The regular dose of the intoxicating medicines should be avoided. Now, without that medicine he does not get sleep for continuously even two nights. He is now disturbed with the disease of sleeplessness. Once, he had written to me informing me about his mental disease—‘My teacher Prof. Broganwakar had been suffering from this very disease for thirty years and at last, he died of the internal mental tension.’ I have observed many patients, suffering from the disease of sleeplessness who remain ready to sacrifice a lot for a little sleep. In Delhi, a young girl of eighteen years could not sleep for the whole year. A sixty years old woman being afflicted with her son’s death didn’t sleep completely for twelve years. This insomnia is the result of the long tensionised life and useless worry and hidden fear permanently abiding in our mind.

This is a news from Ranchi—

‘It has come to the notice that a Uranva youth, belonging to the village Duraganva under Police station, Lohardaga district Ranchi murdered his father by beating with bamboo-stick. The father had scolded his young son with abusive words only. He took it ill and agitated so extremely that he murdered his father.’

Due to such a small reason, such a great sinful deed occured. It was the result only of the hidden tension secretly settled in his mind.

Ò Ò Ò Ò

A young student fled away to Bombay in the attraction of the cinema world. He remained wandering there as a half mad. He remained knocking about from door to door of movies producing companies, He had intense desire in his mind to become a filmy star. Unfortunately nowadays, the cheap films, which are being made are full of sexuality, wantonness and immoral deeds. To see them the youths become addicted of moving in the dreamland. They remain overpowered with the tension created by passion and sexuality. When this student found nothing, he committed suicide. It was written in his suicide note found in his pocket—‘I wanted to become the hero of the cinema. I don’t want to remain alive in such a world of deformation; where there is none to value my art-skill. Thus the mental tension became the cause of his death.

Ò Ò Ò Ò

A young bride committed suicide being fed up with the piercing satirical remarks of her mother-in-law. The last letter she wrote, it had been made clear there that she was fed up with the discard and suffocation and thus, she was ending her life. The women mostly suffer from excess of tension which compels them to live in the hell of mind.

Ò Ò Ò Ò

It is just recently an old pensioner fell down and died in the bank while withdrawing his pension. A teacher died sitting in the chair while teaching in the class. The teachers and students had to perform his funeral rites.

Such men always remain in the condition of worry and tension. They remain always disturbed with imaginary fear and mental diseases. The family—worries either small or big, run after them in their mind every moment. These long lived worries become mental diseases increasing day by day and at last they become the cause of death.

What are the causes of tension?

The question arises, why is mental tension created?

The people in general today lose their temper on worthless matters. The bad tendency to take it ill and the feeling of jealousy and hostility has become so common and so sharp and violent that they become agitated by the mild hurt of their egotism. Their heartily instincts become uncontrolled. When the hostility is created with otherone, the worry and anxiety is natural and then it creates mental tension. Their condition becomes like a monster of human body.

It is the nature of animals to become furiated or dissatisfied without any reason, to hurt with horn or legs and bite with teeth.

If anyone just touches the snake even by mistake or unknowingly, it will become so fierce in anger even by a mild hurt on account of its wicked nature that it will take the life of the facing person.

It is said that the lions, tigers and panthers are so ill-tempered that they are annoyed merely as why he looked on face. Casting the eyes down one may pass on, it may be possible but they consider it their insult to be faced by others. This is heard through the people that the demons, devils, monsters and ghosts are also heartless in the same way. To hear a little against them, they lose their sense in passion.

The serpent, lion and goblin-devil are not considered to belong to the human class of birth but many of them are found in the shape of men also. Those who have not learnt to restrain their voilent instincts, their anger and agitation, insanity and passion, are voilent animals truely.

The modern law does not permit to take revenge at once. So the fury to others, agitation and passion remain hidden in our mind. Today the court cases are increasing very fast and the advocates are earning unfairly. Its main reason is that the people want to cool down their tension through the court cases.

He used abusive words against me, he damaged my prestige, he damaged my reputation, he defeated me and he usurped my wealth—when such thoughts are stored in the mind hidden, the mind is filled with tensions. Man starts plotting against them to take revenge by anyway. The hostility goes on increasing. Hatred begets hatred; it cannot subside it. Love, kindness, pity, compassion, affection, sympathy etc., are such tender instincts that can pacify the instinct of hostility and the tension is minimised—

It has been said also—

अक्रोशदवधीन्यां स ह्यजयदहरच्च मे।

ये च तन्नोपनह्यन्ति वैरं तेषूपशाम्यति॥

He abused me, insulted me, beat me, defeated me and forcibly took my wealth—those who don’t provide room to such thoughts in their mind, are free from hostility and tension.

न हि वैरेण वैराणि शाम्यन्तीह कदाचन।

अवैरेण हि शाम्यन्ति एष धर्मः सनातनः॥

So keep in mind—‘The hostility can never be subdued by hostility, it is love, forgiveness and friendship that bring peace and this is the eternal morality.’

Meaningless disputes and agitation are not the solution of the problem, on the other hand, they intensify the hatred and struggle. Court cases result is utter failure rather than the hostility continues longer. Even the party in opposition also claims his case justified. So, whether they win or lose the case but they leave after them repentence, remorse and a long chain of tragic helplessness.

The tensionised condition is dreadful. The passion and agitation should not be given place in the sub-conscious mind. Be aware of the passionate thoughts. There should be self-control, patience and peace at the time emotional agitation, perturbness, impetuosity, anger and imbalance. At such a moment the work should be done with cool mind and patience.

If you are able to maintain the mental balance, there can never be any adverse situation where the way is not possible to be found out. You should only maintain the balance of your mind. Find out the solution with a considerable understanding, intelligently with farsightedness.

How can we live happily?

In our Vedas the unfailing ways and means have been given to remain free from mental tensions, Just see—

सहृदयं सांमनस्यमविद्वेषं कृणोमि वः।

अन्यो अन्यमभि हर्यत वत्सं जातमिवाघ्या॥

(Atharvaved 3/30/1)

It means—‘May we prove to be contemplative, humane and of noble conduct and have the mutual love and affection for one another always having given up the hostility to one another! Only then, we can be happy.’

ज्यायस्वन्तश्चित्तिनो मा वि योष्ट

संराधयन्तः सधुराश्चरन्तः।

अन्यो अन्यस्मै वल्गु वदन्त एत

सधीचीनान् वः संमनसस्कृणोमि॥

(Atharvaved 3/30/5)

It means—‘By reforming the life, enhancing our knowledge, helping and serving one another, speaking sweetly and modestly always, we should give friendly treatment to one another. All the minds should be the same. (Love, compassion, sympathy and divine bliss may be blessed to us!)

अनमित्रं नो अधरादनमित्रं न उत्तरात्।

इन्द्रानमित्रं नः पश्चादनमित्रं पुरस्कृधि॥

(Atharvaved 6/40/3)

It means—‘O God! Bless me to face only such persons face to face or back to face, over head or downward who are free from the disposition of hostility and embelished with fraternity and friendship. You should always cherish this ambition—

यद् वदामि मधुमत् तद् वदामि यदीक्षे तद् वनन्ति मा।

त्विषीमानस्मि जूतिमानवान्यान् हन्मि दोधतः॥

(Atharvaved 12/1/58)

It means—‘Always may I utter only sweet words from my mouth! (Possessing the divine virtues in mind). May all love me! May my heart always remain illuminated with divine light! May I remain protected from the bad elements if they come near me!’

बलविज्ञायः स्थविरः प्रवीरः

सहस्वान् वाजी सहमान उग्रः।

अभिवीरो अभिषत्वा सहोजि-

ज्जैत्रमिन्द्र रथमा तिष्ठ गोविदन्॥

(Atharvaved 19/13/5)

Brothers! To make this life perfectly useful and successful and to attain the permanent mental satisfaction and joy, embrace your divine (Divine Property) and be aware of the demonish tendencies. Uncountable hurdles and disturbances are natural to be created in life always. You will never be free from them, but to accept their challenges and get rid of them, you must develop confidence and faith in the divine form and your bright future. Sing always the divine songs in praise of the Lord. Study the religious books and listen to them to be free from mental tension. The sport with the children makes our mind delighted. The music leaves a healthful impact on us. Better you hear and sing the devotional songs. By singing the religious songs and devotional songs, reading the stanza written by Tulsidas and the devotional songs of the foremost devotee Sur and Mirabai being concentrated we become free from our mental tension. To the best possible capacity never create in your mind ill will, the feeling of hostility to anyone and secret fear and worry. Worship the Lord daily.

 

Premature-death by perplexity

It has come to the notice through a reporter that in America, the patients of blood pressure and heart, the number of suicide commiters and the patients of insomnia have increased by leaps and bounds in comparison to the past several years. Eight lakh and eighty eight thousand people died of high blood pressure, Nine lakh of people died of insomnia and about three lakhs of people died of cancer. This number of death is just the double in comparison to the past few years. All these persons have died terribly because of the perplexity of mind.

Such types of uncountable deaths are common in every country every year and none is paying serious attention towards it and mostly are not even published in the news papers. Most of the cases of premature death are of such persons as have fallen ill due to the loss of the life giving energy by addiction of intoxication, sexual enjoyments, triffling worries of business, immoral love-relations, worthless disappointments and mental agitation. Their mental balance derailed so much that they could never be cured.

What is the disturbed life?

If you ever felt mental agony or disturbance and felt annoyed and your desires remained unfulfilled, you become forgetting and fuming. In the situation of anger you feel tension in your mind and inwardly you remain perturbed, restless and desultory and become worried again and again and your mind is bent upon to vent one’s spleen. By these symptoms it can be marked that your mind is perturbed. This disturbance of mind may be the cause of untimely death or heart-ailment.

The disturbance of mind is very harmful for our health. The psychic of man’s mind going beyond limit, may create perturbation and mental disease.

The perturbed man does not feel sleep in the night. He passes the whole night changing the sides on his bed. The insult made by anyone always pinches his mind in the night, sometimes remains frightened by public slander, pungent criticism in the society or his opposition. He remains fearful from false reproach. He becomes turbulent just hearing a little reproach against him and he fails to tolerate it.

Generally, the family conflicts are the causes of the turbulence. Among the women the triffling matters become the cause of pungency wordy altercation and critical remarks. They turn the moles to mountain even the triffling problems and spoil by allowing too much indulgence including the entire family. This tumult noise on triffling matters always go on disturbing the tender-hearted men. The loafing of the children, the worry of daughter’s marriage, the difference of opinion between the husband-wife, the scarcity of money, intoxication, rising prices and humiliation caused by the officers or torture by them etc., hundreds of reasons may be responsible to cause mental perplexity. Perplexity is the fruit of suffocation and humiliation.

The strain of nervous system

In this connection, the opinion of the greatest psychologist, William James is valuable—

‘The imaginary and useless worries of the present and future, the hidden fears of the mind and needless strain of nervous system decreases our working capacity certainly and creates hindrance on his path of progress. The main cause of untimely death or heart-attack is the strain on the nervous system.’

The man entangled in so many complications and entanglements, remains afflicted with tension. Constant mental tension creates deformations in the nervous system and the face becomes faded for emotional expression. This is one of the reasons of American’s emotionalessness. If you remain always worried or you are suffering from any hidden fear; if there is any restlessness regarding future, then note it that there is strain on your mind. Your nerves and muscles will always remain stretched.

Suppose, you are sitting in a simple chair and you are taking your breath at the rate of 18-19 per minute in place of 16 per minute and you start breathing before taking every breath out, there will be unnecessary pressure on your nervous system. You will be panting always, you will remain disturbed with the future worries.

On the other hand, if your forehead is shrink free lines of worries, you take your breath slowly and slowly mentaly free peacefully, your muscles remain loose, the worries can never even touch your mind.

The internal turbulent condition of modern mankind

The so-called gentle and cultured mankind today is badly turbulent by his mind. His mental tension remains constant. He remains always sunk in the ocean of economic and social problems mentally. He remains distressed by the imaginary feelings of inferiority complex and the weakness of nervous system having been tired of the social gaps like mountain. These troubles are generally artificial and imaginary.

The poor health of the modern men is also one of the vital causes of the weakness of his nervous system. Nutritive edibles, ghee, milk or pure fresh items of food are not available to them. He pulls on the machine of his body depending on the aridity creating objects in the mind like wine, tea, coffee, biri (a form of crude cigarette) cigarette, intoxicating objects. On these artificial intoxicating elements the machine of the body does work for some time but ultimately it is broken to pieces and the untimely death occurs. So the physical treatment of the nervous system is a must. For a sound health, natural food and natural treatment should be practised.

The seed of sound health is planted in the very womb of the mother. So long as the mother and father are not fully cautious of their physical and mental health, the coming generation cannot be safe from the mental diseases.

Nowadays it has become very common to critcize bitterly to one another, to find out others fault, to blame others, complains and show of jealousy. The dirty habit of finding fault at others is specially found in the politicians but it should not perturb us.

Maintain the mental balance at the time of hardships

In the moments of difficulties, first of all, let the mental peace be protected from the polluted impact on our minds. Keep your mind cool and pondering over by cool mind and heart, find out any means to get rid of and implement it. Be aware of mental disturbance. If your mind got influenced then think that your all weapons were snatched away and all the means to face were ended.

The easiest way to save the mind is neutrality. But what is meant by neutrality?

Any hardships be fallen on you, contemplate and study it in such a way as if you are not concerned with that calamity at all, as if no problem arose before you and if any mishappening has happened, you are mere a spectator.

Remain firm like rock before the protest and criticism

Treading on the path of truth, never be perturbed at all by the meaningless critical remarks of others. All the greatmen have to face opposition and they have faced it boldly and successfully with cool and peaceful mind.

Once, the great sage Daya Nandji Sarswati was opposed in a very dirty way knowingly by some people. This relates to Pune. By making his cut-out, which was garlanded with shoes; seated on a donkey in the form of procession it was demonstrated in the whole market. The face of the statue had been painted with black colour. When this news was conveyed to Swamiji, he uttered—

‘The duplicate Dayanand faces such situation. If that is the duplicate Dayanand, he deserves to be treated so miserably. I am the real Dayanand sitting before you steady in calm mood. This criticism is nothing to affect me in the least.

Even hearing his opposition, he remained steady and peaceful as usual. He was not perturbed the least. There was no trace of any disturbance at all on his face.

In the same way, an agitated Pandit of karnawas (U.P.) used to abuse Swamiji daily, but he paid no heed. By chance one day, he fell ill and did not come to abuse him. On this account, Panditji sent fruits for him. On this compassionate treatment, he was very much ashamed and his habit of abusing was given up.

A certain man used bitter words and abusive language for Mahatma Buddha daily and scorned him. He went on disturbing him by abusing for four days continuously; but the Mahatma always remained steady and peaceful they are never disturbed. He was very much amazed at the mental peace of Mahatma Buddha.

He said—‘My piercing words have no effect on you at all.’

Mahatma Buddha answered—‘If anyone does not accept any gift, whom does this gift belong to?’

He said—‘That belongs to the giver.’

Buddha said—‘You abused me which I did not accept. So, all your bitter words, abusive language and scorn remained with you.’

He had no answer. Actually this is the condition of fully steady and peaceful mind the practice of which washes away the worries and disturbance of mind.

The new method to escape from perturbation

A specialised doctor of mental diseases of England Dr. Hanery Rollin’s experience is that music, devotional songs, repeatedly singing of divine names loudly and the recitation of the verses of literature play a very important role in removing the perturbation of mind, tension and mental problems. Dr. Hanery Rollin has a very big hospital of mental diseases.

He has disclosed that about ten years back when the patients of mental problem were brought for treatment, it was not proved much beneficial. Later on, when some such patients who had interest in music were motivated and other patients who did not know music were also encouraged to join them; it proved very useful in curing them. This experiment proved successful to a great extent.

Dr. Hanery’s opinion is that for the treatment through music it is necessary that the patients should be kept in groups. A patient of mental problem remains always eager of the assurance that he is needed for the society. To encourage him to sing has proved to be an assurance. This experiment has proved beneficial to most of the mental patients.

By hearing or singing music, they become free from tension and they get a healthy flow of oblation to wash away jealousy, hostility, anger and worries.

All kinds of tension and disturbance are originated in mind. In your life mind plays the principal role.

Your all instincts are connected with mind. If a man behaves with contented and balanced mind, pleasure and success follow him in such a way as shadow follows the man.

अक्रोशदवधीन्मां स हजयदहरच्च मे।

ये च तन्नोपनह्यन्ति वैरं तेषूपशाम्यति॥

It means ‘He used ill words for me, he beat me, he defeated me, he robbed my wealth—Men who don’t mind such thoughts, get rid of hostility. They become free from tension.’

न हि वैरेण वैराणि शाम्यन्तीह कदाचन।

अवैरेण हि शाम्यन्ति एष धर्म: सनातन:॥

Mind it—‘Enmity cannot be rooted out by enmity. Fraternity (Love, affection, kindness, compassion) cools the mind, this is the eternal Dharma.

Spirituality gives peace to the mind and balance of mind prevails. When the medical treatment fails, the spiritual medicine cures the mind. By the spiritual means the mental diseases of man are cured. Riddance from sorrow, disease, anguish and disappointment can be possible.

Where the medical treatment of knowledge and science fails, wonderful benefits can be taken on the strength of divine power. You may be suffering from the miseries of any degree, your mind may be tensionised, you might be feeling depression, please watch and test the effect of spiritual treatment also. You can be benefitted in all respects.

A spiritual method

Prayer is such a spiritual method which unites the man to God directly and provides the direct divine aid. Those who call the Lord piteously, get the help certainly. The faith in God is encouraging to mankind.

Internal agitation and external problems are created only when a man is turned away from the Supreme Lord. The Lord is the source of immense joy. Why will anyone staying just near soft and cool water of fountain remain thirsty? The more distance from God means the more internal disturbances of mind and the more affliction of sorrow, poverty, suffering, strife and dissatisfaction. By the true devotional prayer and connecting himself to the presence of the Supreme Lord directly, a man can attain the spiritual power.

An occurence of war period

It was a bullet-shot on the face of a soldier and he began to writhe in pain. The doctor advised to take the bullet out with operation. People assumed that he would die during the operation.

But the soldier had full faith in the dispensation of God. He began to draw the power from the source of that immensely powerful Supreme Lord by prayer. He made the prayer of God with full devotion—

‘O the source of energy! Make me capable to bear the pain of this critical operation successfully. Bless me with full self-confidence to ignore the pain! I am surrendering myself to your hands.’

He felt that any secret spiritual power was strengthening him with supernatural energy for the pain and suffering. The energy was being transmitted in his body. The power of Almighty has been supporting him. Having faith in the divine power he slept by and by.

When in the next morning he got up, he was feeling fresh energy. People thought that he was dead, but he told happily, ‘Doctor! I am ready for operation.’

All were amazed at his bravery. Only because of his self-confidence, the operation was successful and that soldier survived. He narrated that it is the fruit of secret godly help. He had prayed with true devotion that is why his body affliction were removed and came out safely from the jaws of the death.

Believe in God, the theism means to think that I am permeated by a single Supreme element. That eternal supreme element is present in every object.

By the true prayer of the Lord, singing hymn in His praise, worship and congregational singing (hymn) and true devotion, our anguish and grief, scarcity and suffering are washed away. A man having faith in God suffers neither from any internal woe nor has he to suffer in his active external life. In all the circumstances considering it a frolic, he maintain his life blissful by virtue of his divine virtues and divine traits.

Practice to remain free from mental tension

Make such effort that tension and perturbation may not get room in your mind. By the mercy of God, all the worldly affairs are accomplished without any effort. Without any reason you remain restless about them and become unhealthy because of keeping your mind filled with agitation. Your all the problems are being solved one by one themselves. It is better you do your duty only and have faith in God for fruit.

The man disturbed by mental tension, goes on proceeding towards untimely death. Form such habits as your needs may be minimum possible. The unfulfilled needs create mental tension. The man having the minimum needs, can enjoy the state of peaceful life easily. Those who have formed the dirty habits of sensuous enjoyments, comfortable life, the palate-taste or longing for the sense objects, intoxication, remain always perturbed with mental tension due to their unfulfilled artificial and false needs; better you don’t do so. It is mentioned in our Shastras—

वियात विश्वमत्रिणम्!

(Rigved. 1/86/10)

The gluttons face untimely death. Have control over your tongue. Eat to live healthy and not to enjoy taste.

By eating of unwholesome edibles, there is stimulation of passion and then mental tension upsets us.

If you want to live happily cool minded, peaceful and stable, give up the thoughts that cause pain to the spirit.

Immorality, doing unrighteous deeds, the evil thoughts of worry deserve to be entirely abandoned.

 

Protect yourself from this green-eyed monster

Seeing a hunch-backed old woman the sage Narad became graceful. He said—‘O the old woman! Come to me I will cure your hunch-backness by the power of my Yoga.

The old woman said with folded hands—‘Naradbaba! If you are graceful to me, let me remain hunch-backed.’ Kindly make my neighbour also hunch-backed.

Being amazed Naradmuni asked—‘O the old woman! What will be your gain by the other being hunch-backed?’

The old woman said—‘I will feel pleasure to see other walking in the hunch-backed posture.’

This is the case of an old hunch-backed woman overpowered by the feelings of jealousy, who is interested in the grief of others, forgetting her own pleasure. It means that if the feeling of jealousy prevails dominantly in the world, it is not the heaven of pleasure but it may turn to the dark pit of ‘Raurav Hell’.

What is jealousy?

Jealousy is a wicked feeling that creates pain and jealousy in the mind to see others virtues, pleasure, progress and prosperity. It is an inner feeling that burns us internally to see others prosperity and progress.

Why is it so wicked? It is so because it does not inspire us for our own progress and prosperty, but contrary to it, it stimulates for the downfall of others to see them grieved.

Jealousy is a blended mental disorder which is generated and grows up with the association of laziness, arrogance and disappointment. This is the sentiment of superiorty complex. In other words it strengthens the egotism of man.

The jealousy is connected to the inferiority complex. Due to the inferiority complex we are unable to use our full competence in making the effort to reach our goal, we only have the burning desire. First, we think—Would that I had the particular object! Then, again we think—‘Oh! he has the object but I don’t. Then, we think—If it does not belong to me, it should not belong to him as well.’

Envy is the healthy state of jealousy. In envy, to see anyone endowed with comforts, prosperity, attributes or to see anyone well off, we feel sorrow for our own shortcomings and then an ardent longing is created in our mind to achieve it. The envy is that forceful intense desire or excitement, which inspires us to compete others. Envy is not a bad sentiment of mind. Here, we feel sorry for our weaknesses. Here, we want to correct our mistakes moving forward.

In the envy, we feel sorrow as why we did not make progress and in jealousy the matter of sorrow is—‘How and why did he progress?’ The motive behind the envy is to increase the number of virtuous, qualitative, reputed and happy persons and on the other hand the motive behind jealousy to make downfalll.

Envy is concerned with a particular person while jealousy is created against all those who are distinguished among the people or who are deserving of others attention. In jealousy the feeling of anger lies blended in anyway. About a jealous person it is said also that the man is burning in jealousy. In the literature jealousy is expressed in the form of auxiliary sentiment from time to time, but the anger is completely inanimate sentiment. The man against whom we react anger, we never care for the goal of his mind. A poor jealous man remains always excited and restless only to escape himself from being considered inferior. The rich man wants to see the other as down fallen. The jealousy is born as a result of unfulfilled desire to see others inferior and poor. It creates arrogance, it strenghthen egotism and it remains weaving the warp and woof of malice. Being afflicted by igotism we cannot bear to see the welfare of others and being entangled with arrogance we fail to notice our own weaknesses. The cause of arrogance is superiority complex. Jealousy is its associate—whatever is available should come to me.

We become used of feeling sorrow in mind because of seeing others progress as the man of my neighbour is growing higher. I am continuing in the same condition without any progress. Then, why should he prosper in this way? There must be something bad to him also? He must also suffer from some kind of agony, disease, grief, difficulties. I must cause some trouble to him. It will hurt him any way by doing so. By such thoughts our mind is hurt. All thoughts cause our noble and virtuous instincts and vital breath to deteriorate by and by.

Being mad in jealousy, man abandons the path of righteousness, morality and reason. His common condition even becomes the condition of intoxicated mind and others general condition seems to him exception. The disorder caused by jealousy in mind creates different types of deformations in the mental condition. Fear, nervousness, delusion, all these are originated by the depreciation of reasoning due to jealousy.

Every action has its reaction. The exposed reaction of the jealous actions in the outer sphere of mind is poisonous. The impure feelings of man pollute the surrounding atmosphere. The poisonous atmosphere becomes the cause of everyone’s harm. The feelings of jealousy that we have for others, probably its reaction among them also may be similar against us.

Those who consider that they can hide their jealous sentiments in their mind, commit a blunder. It is certain that it will be exposed by any means. From the psychological point of view, other misconduct and the thinking to hide it, is the mother of several mental diseases. In so many persons, the behaviour like senselessness and madness is the outcome of mental complex born of jealousy. The jealousy remains active inside the mind and continues doing undesirable acts. The human life is not the result of only those sentiments, thoughts, emotional feelings, resolves, which exists on the surface of memory rather than the hidden characters and feeligs of our mind which are not in our memory even openly also influence our personality. The secret jealousy lying in our secret mind is always active in our life. Jealousy, anger, sexual feeling, hostility, worry, fear and every experience of misbehaviour done, leaves a print on our inner mind certainly to some extent. These traits and experience are the constant growing germs. The formation of new life or the creation of new life continues going on the basis of these germs.

The defilements of jealousy after making their roots in our mind, don’t go away easily. When the feeling of selfishness and egotism become formidable, there are conflicts and struggle between the dead and living sentiments loss of sleep, nervousness, revengeful attitude wait for opportunity to assail harm, indifference etc., mental worries are the indication of jealous mental condition. If this disorder becomes violent an unexpressed worry and anxiety always continues to be present in our mind. Mind forgets the care of water, food, exercise and rest. While retiring on the bed the mental conflicts and unexpressed inner passionate feeling, don’t allow us to take rest. So, all the five organs of knowledge of man are disordered; the blood circulation is interrupted. The physical diseases also become dominant. Due to the disorder in the whole body, the mind is not nourished properly.

To give place to jealousy and anger in the mind is to invite the number of mental agonies and diseases. So, always remain cautious and escape yourself from jealousy. This feeling has been named as ‘Greeneyed monster’ exactly right.

 

Even the devils of mind may be the cause of death

अपेहि मनसस्पतेऽपक्राम परश्चर।

(Atharvaved 20/96/23)

It means—‘Be free from mental weakness. The weakness of mind is fatal.’

Laughed so much to death

A news of Jodhpur, 23 October 65,—According to the news, a worker of Jansangh was so much overjoyed by the victory in an election that he had to be relieved of life.

It is reported that on the victory of his party in the election he cheered so much that he happened to dance. From all the roots of his hair joy was bursting out, From molecule to molecule elation was reflecting; his all the parts of the body were dancing. His gladness crossed the limit. By and by increasing, it reached the climax. Just as a driver fails to stop the motor car, running with very fast speed by using the sudden brake, similarily he could not check the speed of his profound joy. Enough, he went on laughing. He remained laughing and cheering. His laughter slowly and slowly reached such a stage that he came to feel heart attack. In twinkling of eye he fell down there and died.

There was no deformation in his body at all, he was looking healthy and strong as usual, but his laughter had disbalanced his mind and by its assault he had lost his life.

Like the similar case, it was a report in the Newspapers—

Manila, 22nd November 1965. Forty-two years old Bentura Karwelis, on winning a bet in the phlipines elections similarily due to laughter beyond the limit died. As the matter was reported, he was narrating before his family members laughing cheerfully in the loud voice how he had won a bet of ten bags of rice. He felt pain is the chest. He felt some strain and tightness in his body and at once, he died of brain stroke.

Hear the third news—

It is concerning to Shivhar, Muzaffarpur, on 2nd July 1965. In the assemblage of a marriage party of this village, the music and dance was at climax. In the whole assembly the stream of enjoyment and pleasure was flowing all around. It was the world of wantonness there. All were in the jocund mood of joking and jesting. He began to laugh at any matter and while laughing excessively, he died.

It is said that this man was watching the dance in the mood of intoxication standing on the support of the bamboo of the tent. He was so much engrossed that he had forgotten everything. Abruptly, by a joke of the dance he burst into such a laughter, which he could not check. That laughter went on increasing slowly and slowly and later on it transgressed the limit of endurance. He laughed so much that he fell down there and died the very moment. This mournful event interrupted the whole pleasant atmosphere. The people were so much surprised that they were unable to imagine that anybody might die of laughter.

Any instinct of mind if goes beyond limit and our mind becomes uncontrolled, that becomes the cause of death.

What will be now?

A news of Bulandshahar 3rd July 1965—

What will be now? What will be now? It was the voice of a weak farmer; which stopped his heart-beating and led him to death.

The whole occurence is as such six miles away from there a farmer of the village—Sikhaura, Malkhan Sing’s entire crop got damaged on account of heavy rain and flood and the weak-hearted farmer’s mind was hurt as—‘Oh what will be now? How will be sustenance? Who will help? how will the food and clothes be available? His mind was distressed with such a hidden fear that his inner instincts could not bear this percussion. This dreadful worry as if, had made his future perfectly dark. It resulted so that he could not have his inner conflict under control. He lost his courage and patience. The disappointment surrounded him. Thus, being unable to control his inner mental conflict and by sudden heart-attack, he passed away.

Having such men in view in the Vedas it has been said here—

अपवक्ता हृदयाविधश्चित्।

(Rigved. 1/24/8)

It means—‘A wise and reasonable man should give up those thoughts that cause pain to the heart. A man should bear the pain of calamity, danger, loss, death with strong heart. They should have the complete patience and maintain balance of mind.

The fatal result of the excessive of wrath

This news is related to—

Modi Nagar—1 June 1965. Four miles away from here, near the village, Bhojpur on a brick furnace a dispute ensued between contractor and brick-making labourer for wages. On one side, the summer season and on the other side demonical frenzy of wrath led to a brick-maker fainting and instant spot death. Having The police noted the case and sent the dead body for post-mortem. This dreadful result had come out because of the excess of wrath and lack of tolerance.

The second news report is as such—

Kanpur, 5th July 1965. A resident of the village—Nigoh under the Shivali Police Station, was arrested on the charge of committing murder of his six months old daughter. It is reported that due to the constant weeping of the infant, being wrathful, that angry man threw down the child forcibly on the ground, as a result she died.

Being perturbed by this, the man himself also ran to jump into a well to commit suicide but acosting him the people handed him over to the police.

Death in dispute

A news report of Kanpur. ‘Whether the ‘Kumbh-bath’ is beneficent or not?’ On this a fierce dispute broke out in Bighapur station, in the district, Unnao. Both the groups became furious in anger. In the frenzy of wrath the provocation started and became violent. One of them died and another was injured.

Such a news reveals the fact that when the emotions of man goes out of control and then, they become the cause of great violence and crisis.

A Calamity

Lisban! 31st July 1965. The Portugal news Society, Lucy Tania has reported that two men of Portutgali populated area, Goa, India jumped down from Lorry being frightened and one of them died.

The story is such—Two men were provided seat in a Lorry on their request. When they saw the covering of the coffin, lying near them rising up slowly, they were frightened and remained gazing it, but when from the coffin the drowsy voice was heard, ‘Has the rain stopped?; they were extremely frightened and out of fear they jumped down from the Lorry. One of them died and the another one was badly injured. Later on, it came to the notice that their fear was baseless. The sound that frightened them was of the man who was going to the city Ponda with the empty coffin. That man had entered the coffin to protect himself from the rain and had slept insidce the coffin.

There is a news of Barmer—

A man went for the first time to the funeral ground with the dead body for funeral rites. To see the dead man’s body for the first time, he was frightened so much that he passed many sleepless nights continued dreaming dreadful dreams. He got suspicious of fear. At last, that fear proved to be the cause of his suicide.

Only due to fear

A man named Jaun became disappointed from his life due to several failures. He had suffered many big mental shocks one after another in his life. He created several doubts in his mind being disturbed with the worry and perturbation. His mind was in a fix. He himself thought—

‘Now, what is left in this life? The whole day passed in disappointment. What will I do to live the life of helplessness? I have no longing to live this life. It hardly matters whether God calls me from this world, I will bring the poison from the chemist just today to end this pinching pain of worry. I find only suicide the sole way to get rid over the worldly miseries.’

In such a contemplation of mind being monotonous looking in a mourning apperance he went to a chemist to purchase poison.

Man’s face is the index of his mind. The inner feelings cannot be hidden, they come to appear on the face. The intelligent persons read the mind of the man by his facial appearance. As regards, the shop-keeper he reads the faces of the consumers throughout the day. The doubt was created in the chemist’s mind that—‘There is something black in the bottom. This man wants to end his life by taking poison.’

I have to purchase the poison phial to kill the bed-bug’,—he said to the chemist.

‘What will you do? You never purchase any poisonous medicine; said the chemist.

‘Hello What to tell? The bed bugs disturb me the whole night. I am tired of them. I will get rid of them by this poison. I will take a peaceful sleep.’

‘Mind, brother! This phial is full of poison, use it very cautiously. Be careful that it may not go to the hands of any child, otherwise he may die.’

Having uttered so the chemist went inside the shop and in the phial of poison he filled the harmless medicine and gave it to Jaun.

The chemist’s assumption proved quite true. Jaun was coward. His plan of suicide was fully planned. He was flying away from life.

He wrote the last letter to his wife and drank the poisonous medicine. He began to conceive death—Just to die,......Just to die.

Then he disclosed it also that he had taken the poison, and after a while he will be dying.

Then, not to wait, it created hue and cry all around.

‘Jaun has taken poison. Jaun is committing suicide. Make haste, save him anyhow. Call the doctor. Cause him vomiting any how, save Jaun.’ The patient’s condition was going on deteriorating.’

Due to unbalanced and perturbed mind his hands and feet were growing weak. His heart was throbbing badly. Just to die—just to die.’’

All were watching his exhausting and deterioriating condition every moment and expressing their feelings of grief.

At once, Jaun was taken away to the hospital to an expert doctor for the treatment and his treatment was started.

The doctor tested his pulse and heart very carefully, he made the urine, stool and vomiting etc., chemical test, All were expectant for his death news.

But astonishing! He did not die. He was waiting for the last breath lying on the bed. He was not losing his life.

The doctor tested the red liquid of the phial and at last said disclosing the secret—

‘The medicine, Jaun had taken, was not any poison. That was any harmless medicine. There was no deformation in his body.’

The chemist was called in. He also supported this fact. Making his view clear he said—‘I had given the harmless medicine to save Jaun’s life, that was not poison.’

Later on a great effort was made to convince Jaun but he was not ready to agree. Still he was the victim of mental disbalance. The fear of death had made him worried.’

He repeated the same again and again, ‘I have taken poison. I will not be saved to remain alive.’

The worry of fear and death had rooted in his mind. impatiently, It was perturbing him. This poisonous feeling had made his mind exhausted. This fear had polluted his all the nerves. The fear of death was not being washed away from the core of his mind. Due to wrong imagination and mental perturbation he was waiting for the death.

It resulted so that he remained in the hospital for many months in the suspicion and confusion. It took long for the patient to recover.

Without taking the poison only the false dread of death and mental disbalance had created these disturbances.

This was the opinion of the doctors that only the fear of taking poison had made him reach near death. It is not known how many persons are mentaly sick in the confusion and suspicion of such type of worries.

This example clears that the fear, worry, perturbation, blind faith, mental pressure, all these have a great effect in our mind.

The same idea has been expressed by Dr. William Edler in these words—

‘Mental feelings react verily our physical actions. If our mind is sick, it is certain that body will also suffer from sickness. If the patient is mentaly worried, fearful, doubtful about death, then the doctor has to face great difficulty in his treatment.

Take it granted that not only one but a number of persons looking physically healthy outwardly, are suffering from mental disease bearing in their mind hidden suspicion, whim, worries, tension, sudden emotions.

Death due to mental weakness

There is a news of London—A peon of a college of Everdin University lost his life only by the sounds of shrieking in anger and slanders of the streets. The matter was that he used to make true and false complaints of the students misbehaviour to the higher officials. Due to this mental weakness of back-biting, he became piercing spike in the eyes of the students.

Conquer the ill motives and remain cool and peaceful

A man should remain always cautious from such mental emotions and provocations. Whenever there is attack of these enemies of mind, let the mind be cool and composed and overpower the reverse circumstance and control patiently.

In our mind demonical propensities, morbid feelings and divine traits, modesty and virtues are talent, modest and nobility are lying asleep. If the demons wake up, they should be controlled by self restraint and self discipline.

पिपेश नाकं स्तृभिर्दमूना:।

(Rigved 1/68/10)

‘Remember it—‘The self restraint persons can win even the paradise. The path that leads to the happy and peaceful life, goes to have the vices and misconducts under control.’

अपवक्ता हृदयाविधश्चित्।

(Rigved 1/24/8)

It means—‘Give up the sensuousness and sin of mind that cause pain to the soul. Evil thoughts of Sexuality, anger, fear, worry etc., are always worth abandoning.’

In your secret mind, whatever the unnecessary worries are gathered, they create the situation of misery. The ill wills are the origin of mental disbalance and the source of mental diseases. Never give place to the bitter experiences in your mind. The lustful desires are the mother of all the vices.

Maintain the balance of mind

Remember it that mental disbalance may be the cause of horrible problems. Worry, fear, anger and perturbation are the greatest enemy of the mankind. Always keep your mind cool and at the time of hardships set the example of fortitude and tolerance.

To keep the mind cool, righteousness can support you. The theistic view in life gives us the power of Supreme Lord, which always maintains the balance of mind.

मर्त्या हवाअग्ने देवा आसु:।

(Shat. Bra. 11/1/2/12)

‘A man becomes Deva (god) by auspicious deeds. By the noble and auspicious thoughts, balanced and peaceful mind and virtuous deeds attain the position of Deva (god) through this body on this earth.’

आर्या व्रता विसृजन्तो अधि क्षमि।

(Rigved 10/65/11)

Those who follow righteousness and duty, are alone the gods. They are the apparently gods who remain balanced and calm even in hardships and troubles, misery even in the biggest adverse situations and in the perils.

 

Don’t lose patience in odd situation

When a man dies, the mind trembles with fear, the tragic news of death is painful to hear. When we return from the funeral ground after funeral rite, our mind remains restless for many days.

Not one-two, ten-twenty or one and two thousand persons but if twenty thousand persons commit suicide per year, it should be considered a serious situation.

Such an odd situation is there throughout the world.

The famous newspapaer of America—‘New York Times’ has published a survey report recently which reveals the fact that every year, about twenty thousand Americans commit suicide. This survey report has become the cause of worry in America.

The report says that there are several cases of death that cannot be called suicide whereas they are the cases of only suicide and nothing else.

According to the report in America suicide is one of the first ten causes of death and as far as the youths are concerned, it is one of the five causes.

A glimpse on the causes

In which month the highest number of deaths occur?

The American survey department has found out that the highest number of suicides are committed in the month of December and specially in the days of the Christmas.

It seems to be a matter of great astonishment? The Christmas is the festival of joy and happiness for the English people. Well! Why these deaths in the month of happiness? Listen to the reasons—

The Americans make the retrospection of their activities of the whole year in this month. What was done in the whole year? In how many matters were they successful and in how many matters they got failures? What were the facilities or the financial problems? In business, what was the loss or gain? They retrospect all the accounts of their work. They are materialists. They live the life on the principle of ‘Eat, drink and be merry lest we may die anytime. Most of them become depressed getting failure in their material purposes. Most of them are left alone by the false friends and even by their wives. They begin to hang around them who are endowed with the materialistic comforts and objects. Mostly, the Americans being afflicted by this disappointment and lonliness commit suicide.

Some more reasons as follows—

1. Want of self-confidence—

The mental patients of suicide consider this life short-lived, purposeless and meaningless. They think that the materialistic circumstances can dash them to dust easily. They don’t have their own identity. Man is a toy of fate. This lack of confidence creates cowardiceness in them.

2. The loss of enthusiasm—

The minor adverse situations disturb the enthusiasm of their lives. First their efforts are half-heartedly performed, and then next they don’t have patience. They connect their failures with meaningless reasons whereas the want of their sincere effort is the chief cause of their failure.

3. Domestic problems—

The quarrels among the women, the disputes between the mother-in-law and the daughter-in-law the difference of opinion between the father and son, habit of intoxication, the sexual lust, and to deviate soon from the mental disorders. Mental and ligamentary defilements unable to marry the children properly, unemployment of the son, more children and the social conventions are the reason of suicides.

4. Economic problems—

The enhanced expenditures of the modern time, showy life, modern fashions for the false show, so much money is needed which cannot be met out. Because of the unfulfilled false needs, the troublesome problems are created and the life becomes a burden.

5. The passion of strife—

Nowadays, in the Western countries, the people are intoxicated with the madness of war and strife. They try to solve the problems by strife and quarrel and by the violent methods instead of adopting the peaceful means. As a result they always remain in tension.

6. The racial discrimination—
