The feelings of high and low between the whites and black and the complex of superior and inferior, poor and rich fill the mind with jealousy and hostility.

7. Mental tension—

The tension of mind, to remain absorbed in meaningless thinking and inner mental conflict and struggle in brain makes the life quite unstable and restless.

8. The addiction of intoxicating medicines and wine—

The people have started using mostly the intoxicating medicines now-a-days to win over worries and mental troubles. It keeps mind hot and the man happens to do something otherwise in excitement.

9. The chiefest cause—

Disbelief in Almighty and the other world, the desire of the materialistic joys and comforts and discontentment in all the circumstances.

You are the centre of energy

If anyone of the reasons mentioned above is created in your mind, you should be careful at once. Nobody knows when being dominant this poisonous situation, may assume the form of suicide.

In the early morning sitting peacefully, ponder over calmly again and again on the following thought and instil it in your secret mind—

‘अहमिन्द्रो न परा जिग्ये।’

(Rigved 10/48/5)

It means—‘I am the centre of energy. I can never be defeated in life.’

‘I am not to be deviated from my path due to minor botherations. I am never to be overpowered by the horrible situations. The hardships come and pass away like storm. I am the unmoved, steady and stable rock in the storms. The dreadful circumstances or any misery cannot assail any harm to me. They come to test me but I am never defeated by them.

‘My self-confidence is great. It is never disordered by the common wants and a little miseries. I have unwavering faith in the eternal power of the Lord. God’s potency is always with me. It protects me always like armour. I am never nervous due to my troubles; I think of means to solve them one by one. I find out the reasonable solutions of the problems.

‘My life is secure. The great energy of the Lord is being exposed in me. I will face all the adversities like a hero.’

Daily, roar this resolve like a lion. By this nectareal thought daily morning and evening while going to sleep on bed, your self-confidence will become strong and firm. Keep on your self-confidence growing. Your self-confidence is to save you from all kinds of miseries, fear and grief. It is expected from a wiseman to contemplate about his own abilities, moral virtues, prosperity and courage always.

The dark clouds cannot stay long in the sky, similarly, the problems of life are also momentary. The man who has faith in the benedictory Lord, his life is protected from different kinds of calamities, ignorance, attachment. aversion and worries.

Who is spared from troubles? Who is free from disease? Who is safe from being harassed by the botherations? Who is free from death, disease, sorrow? If you minutely mark, every one is suffering from the worries.

But the brave, never care for them. They continue always making the right effort for the raising up their fortitude and progress.

To remain fixing your eyes towards bright future and continuing practice to make it practical, is the way to get rid of the odd situations.

Whenever the undesirable thought of fear, cowardiceness, defeat comes to our mind by creating the contrary thought of courage, spirit, vitality and being victorious in struggle, we should be free from the unfavourable situation.

ॐ भद्रं कर्णेभिः शृणुयाम देवा भद्रं पश्येमाक्षभिर्यजत्राः।

स्थिरैरङ्गैस्तुष्टुवार सस्तनूभिर्व्यशेम देवहितं यदायुः॥

स्वस्ति न इन्द्रो वृद्धश्रवाः स्वस्ति नः पूषा विश्ववेदाः।

स्वस्ति नस्तायो अरिष्टनेमिः स्वस्ति नो बृहस्पतिर्दधातु॥

(Rigved 1/89/8, 6)

ॐ शान्तिः शान्तिः शान्तिः

‘O gods May we hear the auspicious words with our ears. May we have always the auspicious sight with our eyes. May our body and limbs be strong and resolute so that we may be fulfilling the Lord’s work

Gods! May Indra whose glory is spreading all around, do the highest good to us. May the evil Shanishcher. Garuda and Vrihaspati be benefactor to us. May we be peaceful. May peace pervade all around us. May we be healthy-minded and engaged ourselves in solving our problems peacefully.

Enjoy the life till the end

This life is valuable. It is meant for constant struggle and progress. The coward and fearful thoughts don’t become you. It has been said—

उत्क्रामातः पुरुष माव पत्थः।

(Atharvaved 1/4)

It means—‘Always talk of rising high. Never think of downfall nor fall down.

Friends! Hold on the feelings of hope and success always and never of disappointment and defeat in this struggle of life. We are sure to win this time. In the future our success is must—keep this nectareal feeling always in your mind.’

उद्यानं ते पुरुष नावयानम्।

(Atharvaved 8/1/6)

It means—‘Brothers! Always make progress. Don’t allow downfall at any cost even by mistake. Adopt the strong thoughts of raising up the life and not even by mistake think of downfall and embrace virtuous deeds.

मात्र तिष्ठ: पराङ‍्मना:।

(Atharvaved 8/1/9)

It means—‘In any sphere of life tardiness and discouragement is not right. Mind it, To be indolent and disappointed is a kind of atheism.’

वीरयध्वं प्र तरता।

(Atharvaved 12/2/26)

It means—‘Only the industrious persons cross over the ocean of this world. The boat of the persons devoid of prowess, sinks in the middle.

Think for the life sake. So long as you are alive always cherish the fanciful thoughts of healthy and perfect joy in your mind.

अमृतं विवासत।

(Rigved)

‘Make the company of only the optimists and courageous. Keep the cowards away who make you coward and make your future disappointing and dark.

Have full faith in righteousness. Your noble deeds of this life are to improve your next life. The God is always present with you.’

शुचिं पावकं ध्रुवम्।

(Rigved)

It means—‘Praise those who are firm in righteousness. May you also achieve courage like them! May you live a long life and remain healthy, may you attain the self esteem.’

 

Don’t be perturbed worthlessly

You have to travel by train. It is still one hour for the train to arrive but why is this palpitation in your mind? Worry and nervousness have upset you. You have the fear in your mind for the train to depart one hour earlier. You are not free from this worry till you step in the compartment of the train; your mind remains filled with different kinds of worry for example—the worry to buy the ticket, the worry of pick-pocketting or the theft of your luggage, the fear of not getting the accomodation in the train; the fear of the arrival of the train before time, the fear of your watch being slow, the doubt of the collie’s non-availbility, the worry of missing the connecting train.

Such types of many worries make you off the rails. You hurriedly proceed and forget a few things even on the way, you lose the money or sometimes you forget to give necessary information to someone. When you reach the station, you came to know that the train is still late to arrive. Again the nervousness starts! Whether the suitable berth will be available or not? Will I be able to load all my luggage in the compartment? Is the weight of the luggage under the limit of the ticket or more? The worry of the ticket of your small child worries you that he might be arrested by the ticket-checker as you think that you have not purchased his ticket considering him under age.

The train arrives at the platform and you find that your all the worries were meaningless. All the feelings of your nervousness were useless. Due to false imaginary fears you were upset in your mind.

You will be astonished to know that there are some such persons also who have no care of catching the train at all. They have already taken the information about the train by which they have to travel but when the moment of catching the train comes close, they remain sitting silently and so carelessly as if they have not to go to the station. It seems that if they are even in sleep, they can catch the train. Such men are mentaly so strong that their daily routine and their different activities are not disturbed at all by anyway, this is simply an example.

There are different spots of nervousness. For the examinees, in the examination hall most of the examinees forget half of the question paper due to the hidden fear. As soon as; they enter the examination hall the heart beating starts. They forget half of the portions they have learnt. In the palpitation, they write wrong even what they know. For a doctor nervousness is very dangerous. At the time of operation if he becomes nervous seeing the deteriorating condition of the patient, the patient’s death is certain. If the drivers of train, motor car or motorcycles, the Rikshaw-pullers become mentaly disturbed, it is not known how many accidents will take place. When an orator stands to give a speech or an actor starts playing his role and just before he becomes nervous, he will fail badly.

In every sphere of life, the nervousness is harmful and dangerous. Becoming nervous is also a kind of mental weakness. So, a man should understand its characteristics well and make effort for its remedy.

In the society and world the dreadful situations arise. The root of nervousness is not there but it lies hidden in the mind of the man. Unstability, dissatisfaction, disease, fickleness are dependent on unhealthy atmosphere and they are not dependent on the outer world.

A man becomes nervous to see a dreadful situation but the other one faces it boldly and bravely due to his mental balance and to the best of his capacity. According to the doctrines of Western psychologists, the root of all the outer actions of man lies in his ulterior mind. This ulterior mind is very active, swift, powerful and very strong and capable. It guides the Supreme mind and body from inside. If any fear has occupied its place in the interior of mind (Generally in childhood) as a result, evil thoughts and evil instincts remain creating fear. The most secret dangerous effect of fear is there on body. Very harmful changes come in us. We usually have the adverse imaginations of the dangerous fruits. To see others being nervous, we also become the victim of nervousness like contagious diseases. Nervousness is the polluted reaction of the mental complex of the intricate fear. The root of this habit is found in the man’s initial life, family circumstances and emotional feelings and experiences.

Minutely observe and think how the cowardly habit of nervousness was formed? What were fears that frightened you in the childhood? Who were to tease you, to frighten you, to threaten you and to cause you trouble? How many times did your teachers rebuke you and reproach you? How did the step-mother misbehave with you? What were the deeds where you got failures?

If you get your psycho analysis performed by any learned psycho analyst, he will tell you the cause of the complex of your mind. He will tell what are the reasons of disappointing and entangled complex of your mental feelings. The child whom you always rebuke and reproach, threaten or discourage and torture, his entire potential productivity becomes crippled. From the very childhood he becomes pessimistic and indolent. He suffers from the inferiority complex and shyness badly from the very childhood. He feels shameful in triffling matters even and he hesitates to express his true words even before others. The ill-treatment with him spoils his self-confidence. It is here, he develops the habit of nervousness. He becomes devoid of the strength to fight against the odd and adverse circumstances.

So, this is the duty of the parents, teachers and guardians that they should never make the undue harassment of the children. They should make them realize their mistakes with love and affection. They should not rebuke them so badly, that they may lose their ambitions of life and become worthless forever, they may not be deprived of the instinct to fight the adverse circumstances.

Contrary to it, the sense of leadership should be developed and encouraged among the children. The old fables of strengthening their self confidence, the secret reasons of their small victories, their grand successes, the full appreciation of the courageous deeds even in the odd situations and whole-hearted appreciation and praise should be made with open heart.

The famous scholar of psychology Shri Lalji Ram Shukla has written that to humiliate the small children for anything is just like to create the feeling of nervousness in them. Such a child remains always afraid of being humiliated by other. So, he dares not meet the strangers or do any new work. It is common that sometimes the elders laugh at the child on any matter. If the child asks any question in the class, the teachers neglect them. Thus, the child feels ashamed of. Then, he loses his courage to open his mouth before others. Sometimes the child feels shy before all for his any mistake. His experiences also prove very unpleasant. He tries to forget his bitter experiences and forgets also. But such experiences make him weak forever. At the time of examination he becomes so nervous that he fails to write the answers of the questions. This is the bad result of the nervousness of his mind. So, it is clear by this instance that we should never rebuke or reproach the students and give contrary indication. We should not give a long speech of criticism for their mistakes. Bitter experiences should not be expressed before them again and again.

Know the real cause of your nervousness by the analysis of your mind. Fresh the old memories again and again. Having come to know the cause of nervousness, it can be removed wisely and intelligently.

If you go through these causes seriously, you will find that it was all your imaginary feeling and there was the least truth in it.

The reasons that make you to think uselessly and make you nervous in reality have not to happened ever, though you have become very old.

The present wise thoughts, the healthy indications or suggestions given to the hidden mind and the behaviour full of self-confidence are the three infallible weapons that can make us to get rid of our habit of nervousness. By these three means our self-confidence can be promoted and strengthened. As our self-confidence increases so the habit of nervousness decreases.

We become nervous so because we don’t make the preperation of the work to the best of our capacity and strength. The world requires the full preperation and in depth. The work done half-heartedly, being unsuccessful, damages our confidence. The nervousness starts. Whatever the work taken in your hands needs prior full mental and intellectual preperation for it and ready for all the circumstances whether adverse or favourable, whatever is possible. The full preperation will never leave any room for nervousness. Why will the man who is ready to face all the situations good or bad, feel palpitation? They are the thieves who feel heart-beating, fear, escape and feel shame. When you are well prepared, most of the weaknesses are over. Make full preperation before you take any work in your hands to accomplish. The contrary feeling of nervousness is ‘calm and peaceful emotion.’ Those who assume the peaceful and steady mental disposition root out the nervousness. We should form the mental habit of growth in the calm and steady condition of the mind. While doing any work we should be cool minded. The hidden self instructions of peace should be conveyed to the hidden mind. Go on contemplating so always.

‘I accomplish every work peacefully. I never do any work in hurry being overcome by imaginary useless fears, I am at peace, in supreme peace and steady, my mental balance is always right. I know that I can make progress only when I am free from fickleness. I never feel nervous; because I am healthy, happy and carefree in the potency of the Lord. By the power and initiation of God whatever is auspicious and stable for me, it will be so. Any storm or hardship cannot affect my peace of mind.

Continue inspiring your hidden mind in this way again and again. Day and night by rooting this sentiment in your mind your mental condition will be balanced. Visualize in your mind such peaceful persons, sages, learned men, thinkers as if you want to be peaceful yourself. The images of such great men inspire and encourage you in the state of nervousness.

Use your fancy in right direction; it means sketch such an auspicious and valorous painting of mind by imagination that you may see your that successful form in that painting. The picture of successful and peaceful life that you see on the canvas of your imagination will be certainly practical in your life. Suppose! You feel nervous while giving a speech. Now sketch the picture of a big meeting in your mind and imagine yourself giving a speech fluently before that big gathering. By the mental practice of success and peace, you will be able to accomplish it in your practical life certainly.

Do the work with peaceful, steady and cheerful mind. Don’t think yourself unfit for any work beforehand. Speak slowly and slowly. Do only one work at a time. It may be possible for you that you may be nervous to see many works before you; and you may feel tired due to a hidden fear. If the works are completed slowly and slowly, the mind does not feel too much burdened and disturbed.

Have confidence and firm resolve in your mind for the successful completion of the work. The work you are taking in your hand will be certainly, completed successfully, This bent of mind awakens your potency to get the success in the work. Have the constant thought of your characteristics, energy, capacity and your divine qualities. Even by mistake, don’t think of your weakness and shortcomings in your mind; otherwise you will feel nervous more and more. By thinking of the weaknesses, the worthless thought of self-remorse comes to our mind and it causes weakness. First, take small works in your hands where you can be successful. Then taking the hard and difficult work in hand, you should complete it successfully. It will develop confidence in yourself.

The root cause of your nervousness is the imaginary accumulated fear of your hidden mind. So you must do what you think you cannot do, you must meet those whom you fear, hesitate or feel shy to meet. By its practice, the hidden fear of mind is washed away. So, gladly and fearlessly greet the difficulties and hardships.

 

The golden clues of the protection at the terrible time of miseries

The life faces big earthquakes of hard time sometimes in the life. Unexpected sudden storm of calamity and miseries, death, tragic news make most of the persons extremely restless. Sometimes the ghost of fear appears before our mind. The life seems to be badly tangled in dangers. It seems that the life will be shattered forever.

At the time of such dangerous situation man is struck with amazement. The intelligence does not work. He becomes at a wit’s end. He becomes disappointed or being agitated, he speaks such words for which he repents later on.

Sometimes, we commit such actions in the excitement that we did not want to do actually or we did not mean so. Once an officer used some bitter words for the clerk. The clerk was enraged so much that he threw the files upon the officer’s face. It resulted that he was relieved from the service and he remained repenting for the whole life.

William Leyan Pheleps is quite true in version—

To keep the mind peaceful and cool in the adverse days is very useful for man. It saves us from many bad fruits. Let us see the most successful and affluent men around us and change our life afflicted with distress and perturbation accordingly.

Some men have struggled the sufferings very patiently. They have found out their own ways. Some ways are being given here for example—

Rules—(1) Mark the experiment of Field Marshal Bycount Smith to remove the tension of mental agony. Once, he had to face a big defeat in the war. He was trying to find out any such a way as he might inspire courage and zeal among his soldiers so he began his speech in the following way—

‘The result might be more horrible,’ he said.

‘How?’ a soldier asked the question.

‘It was possible that it might rain even!’ just laughing he said. All came to laugh hearing his smiling answer. The tension was minimised.

When you are also ever in hardship minimise your mental tension smiling. ‘Laugh’ itself is a nectarial remedy, which makes the body light spreading in the whole body. It makes the life lively.

You, too, should use ‘Laugh’ and ‘smile’.

Rule—2. A professor was giving his lecture in a higher class. He was mentaly nervous. He was speaking very fast saying the matters hurriedly. In hurry, he forgot the writer’s name of the drama on which, he was giving coments. He tried his best but could not recollect the name. A clever student of the class comprehended the mistake. Abruptly it came to his mind that hurry should be avoided in troubles, so without any fear, he went on arguing and discussing. As he got the interval of mind, his mind pacified and he was able to recollect the writer’s name—the name was Sir James Verry. Now, what was there? With a courage he told the name of the writer. His shyness was removed. He was escaped scarcely from a great disrespect.

So, stop for a little while. Make your mind cool and balanced. In hurry it is possible, you may commit such an error which may not be corrected later on. Suppress your mentality of doing anything in excitement in hurry. You will be saved from foolishness certainly.

So, let some time pass. Let the matter be pacified.

Rule—3 While conversing with others we want to cling to our thought with our own point of view only and stick to our view badly in discussion. We should not deviate the least. On the other side the other one also does not want to deviate from his obstinacy and his logic. It results so, that the tension continues.

The shop-keeper wants to bring round the customer but the customer does not want to give up his obstinacy. Nobody wants to be humiliated by withdrawing his words. But if you do so you will make the otherone your enemy.

A successful merchant told me,—‘The secret of my success is that I allow my customers to express their views to their best. I never dominate them. I satisfy their egotism. I only hint and allow them full opportunity to think over. By doing so I don’t lose my customer.’

Don’t try to dominate others. Never hurt their ego.

Rule—4 Hearing our bitter criticism and ill our temper goes out of control. Some are so much excited that they lose the balance of their mind.

Recently I met a psycho-expert doctor. I asked—‘You have to meet several lunatics and men of disbalanced mind. What do you do?’

He said—‘It is possible only to hear our own criticism. If we take it in our mind that it has not been uttered for me. By this way, the psycho patient is annoyed with some one else on some other issue from his friend, from any member of his family or from any official. He makes me merely the scapegoat to vent his spleen on me.

You should also keep in mind that half of the population of the world and specially the women are either mad or immature. They seem to us strange and we are strange to them. Then, why should we be disturbed uselessly considering their utterence ill?

Rule—5 Gordon Kuper was flying by an aeroplane in the sky when his plane developed some problem. He writes that he did his best possible; used automatic control but the plane could not be controlled. First, I made my mind balanced peacefully. Then, I used the outer manual control. We do all this always usually in the beginning. I found that the plane was controlled. I got down safely. Since then, I realised that by the simple and common things and means the grand result can be achieved.

In the hours of peril, you should bear firmness in your mind and think over the way with cool mind to get rid of the hardships. Take it granted, if you are free from perturbation, it is undisputed fact the solution of the problem will come out.

There is no such difficulty, which may not be overcome. In life, never accept defeat. Disentangle knots of entangled difficulties. Don’t talk of your inferiorty or defeat—

अनुहूत: ..........

आरोहणमाक्रमणं जीवतो जीवतोऽयनम्।

(Atharvaved 5/30/7)

‘You (Going towards death?) I am calling you back. Turn back. Recognise the path of life. Know the path of progress and prosperity.’

 

The downfall of the society can be checked by this way

The sorrow is being expressed from place to place in the country regarding the moral decline. The new methods of cheating or deceit, fraud, theft, false advertisements somewhere adulteration in food materials somewhere bribery somewhere black marketing somewhere partiality are coming to our notice.

It is practically impossible to get pure milk, ghee, flour, curd and medicine etc., in the market. Everywhere there is adulteration of the spurious objects. In our country, the businessmen don’t realise that the business flourishes by honesty and by selling the pure materials. Black-marketing, not to pay the sales-tax, illegal business with the foreign countries like Pakistan etc., less weighing, by telling more price and after high haggling to charge less, showing the superior quality of sample and then giving the object of inferior quality, corrupting the originality by mixing the spurious object, the attempt to cheat the customers, are the different shapes of the downfall of the business.

Generally in the newspapers off and on the news of moral decline are published. In one year, only in Bombay the Anti-corruption Bureo lodged 243 cases of corruption and ignoble conduct including against 67 Govt. officials also. Out of them in 26 cases, 35 Govt. officials were arrested on the charge of taking bribe, embezzlement or grabbing money by illegal means.

The news report of the last 11th December 58 of Saharanpur says that 14 grain merchants, one Railway booking clerk and four brokers of Saharanpur were arrested in so called charge of sending the rice valuing rupees two Lakh out of the state. The illegal business of intoxicating objects has come in practice openly. It is published generally in the newspapers, several news of making illegal wine, or bringing opium by stealth selling drugs prepared from hemp plants and its leaves are in practice openly.

Just cast your sight on the monthly crime report of the Bombay Police. In the last of the month 103 cases came to light. Out of them 29 cases were related to the crime of drugs, 3 cases were related to gambling, 61 cases of driving the car without license and rest 10 were different cases of crime; for example the black marketing of cinema tickets, cheating, personal use of the Govt. property, the theft of building materials, pressing the women for prostitution and selling them.

All these immoral deeds are done due to the lust and greed of earning money easily without any labour. A number of persons have the desire of a prosperous and wealthy life and they want all the worldly objects of comforts and enjoyment, but they don’t want to earn honestly and with labour. As a result, they always think of any new method of cheating and deceit.

Why do the people become depraved?

The addiction of making money without any labour is very bad. When a man is demoralised once and forms the bad habit of parasitic living, shirkering, cheating he never takes interest in permanent work.

Some people feel proud of their dignity in showing themselves more than their status or showing their higher social status, Despite being internally hollow, they want to show their position superior outwardly to keep the society in dark. There are some who are unrestraint in the addiction of taking wine, in the satisfaction of their sexual desires, fashion and the habit of luxurious comforts. The moral earning is always limited. Their mind remains always restless to meet their extra additional expenditures. They always think of the sources to increase their income so that they may fulfil their lustful desires and maintain ostentatious life.

In the modern age of unemployment it is hard nut to crack to increase the income honestly. In addiction; the man shirks from labour and wants to enjoy the pleasures without labour. He uses his wit in finding out the way that he may increase his income just double without taking trouble of doing any work or doing the minimum possible labour. In this matter he goes beyond the limit of propriety or justification. Momentry enjoyment and greed deludes his discrimination.

The social cause of moral decline is the attitude of false show, spirit of ostentarian false pride, the fulfilment of passionate and sexual desires or the madness after fashion and unnecessary craving or greed. A corrupt person’s mind remains always filled with greed that leads him towards illegal means. Some persons have the natural criminal tendency of theft. There are some of lustful nature who are fond of drinking wine, prostitution and passionate objects of hotels. Some satisfy their ego with extra- vagancy. All of them are the mental patients.

Extravagancy, luxuriousness and comfortability is a big flaw of the showy society. It is not limited only to the rich and capable group but is stretched to the middle and labour class; clerk and the officials also.

As much the false tendency of showing rich is found today, was never found so much in the past. The people are not satisfied with their honest income; they always think of the means to become rich abruptly in a single day (which are usually immoral). They do speculation, gamble, decieve others by so many ways, cheat others and perform corrupt practices and try to take bribe.

In the cities, the tendency to show false splendour and false show is prevalent everywhere. You can mark it on the streets, roads, in the parks, temples and mostly on the occasions of marriage functions. The fashion show and status show is perhaps most popular. The tendency among the young boys and girls to decorate and beautify themselves is growing by leaps and bounds unrestraintly. The people want to impress their grandeur on others to spend more than their income and its bad result is in seen in the form of bankruptcy in business, several court cases of cheatings and different types of crime. Where the culprit is sentenced severe punishment for dishonesty and cheating others.

Our outer show should be better. We should look as rich and capitalist, This variety of make up is now leading the society towards corruption. The cheater have now started impressing on others with their false dignified identity. They want to live in a particular style, reside in grand buildings, organise parties and then there is the sway of betels and cigarattes and to meet these expances to them taking corruption seems the only simple means.

A group of persons which is poor inside but shows that they are rich. This lower middle class tries to cover their poverty by all means. They have already spent their income before earning. They remain always indebted to either of the grocer or of cloth merchant. They fail to pay the electricity bill. The room rent is always due but even then, they organise banquets for their friends and they will never minimise their expenses in giving gifts etc. How long will the friends and relatives remain with them? Only till they are badly entangled with the debt and its payment goes beyond limit. The moment he became helpless under the burden of debt, such opportunistic friends become invisible and start hating the indebted man. None has any regard for him.

We have become slave of fashion. We see through others eyes, we think through others mind. We do what pleases others. We don’t do according to our means, according to our status or according to our income. We are slave to superstitions. We are bent upon acting as is the custom of giving and receiving? When we have no money at all in our pocket and we mortgage our house. We don’t consider independently and never think pros and cons. Without the consideration of the class we belong to, we follow blindly the higher status. The society separates after tumultuous applauding for two days and we remain burdened with the debt throughout the life. It has become our misconception that if we put on such clothes or remain in make up and follow the vogue of the society, only then, we will deserve respect. Being enmeshed in foolishness we desire to live the life of that class, which is of higher status, higher income, wealthier and better welloff.

Thus, a number of wise and educated persons even move towards sorrow, helplessness, suicide, agitation, crime and corruption. By the food adulteration, bribe from others, they cheat the innocent public deceitfully. They cheat by different ways. They get false advertisements published and don’t hesitate in committing robbery and murder. By committing theft repeatedly, they become habitual of doing so. Seeing a corrupt man well-dressed up the others also change themselves in the same colour. They also follow the same immoral means. The one corrupt person makes another one corrupt.

The money earned by dishonest means is like poison. Who earn money by immoral and evil means. Poison is present all around them.

The wealth earned by immoral means stays long only for eight to ten years and the entire wealth is destroyed just when the eleventh year starts.

Saint Tolostoy considered wealth as sin because of several evils are inherent in wealth. His wife preferred the luxurious life of eating, drinking, fondness for delicious dishes and outer show. She always used to put up the new demands of new fashions. Thus, due to the dissimilarity in their nature and view, their life had become sinful. If in his place, there had been any other one of weak self-confidence, he could have become corrupt to please his wife. He could resort to the conspiracy of robbing people by deceit, cheating, fraud, knavery and hypocrisy; Tolostoy had a great hatred for corruption. He did not deviate from the path of truth and morality. In the age of eighty-two, being tired of his wife’s strife, he abandoned his home.

It is true that they are great fortunate who treat the wealth as their servant. They, who are the servant of wealth are very unfortunate.

Out of so many pious objects, the fair means of earning money is the best.

Our society, responsible of moral downfall

Who should be blamed for corruption? Whether the individual or the society? You will say that it is the individual who commits theft, treachery, fraud, cheating, adulteration and takes bribe. So, it is the individual responsible for this, the individual is to be blamed for.

In my opinion, the individual is not so much responsible for the corruption as much as the society. The society always influences the individual. In every society there are some customs and traditions and some definite rules and regulations. The individual is bound by them. Every individual of the society wants to follow the customs and traditions which have due importance in the society and which are considered good or bad in the society in natural way. He feels exalted of following them.

In the society there are some who lead a very simple life, but there are some such arrogants who have nothing in their pockets, but they boast of being well off by living a showy and ostentatious life outwardly. They maintain make up with artificial ornamental objects. They are outwardly something and inwardly something else, When they maintain make up, the society gives them due honour. They move in the society with a social status. The men of common status also imitate them to see their make up and luxuries. They are attracted to their fascinating life. Everything in the society goes on by imitation. One after another, well! Only this fascinating life is causing trouble everywhere.

The luxurious and fashionable life of the big men in the society creates the feeling of jealousy among the men of lower income. He is unable to meet his expenditure with the limited income. So, he always remains mentaly dissatisfied. Anywhere you cast your look, you will find a common complain of low income because he does not want to live under the limit of his income and social status and makes an unsuccessful effort to imitate the lives of rich, landlords, feudal chieftains, kings of higher status.

The suggestions to check the moral downfall

The moral downfall is a social disease. It is only the society that can solve this problem. If the society makes effort, the corruption can be rooted out very soon. Such functions in the society should be banned, which arouse the sense of jealousy and imitation of the rich class of persons in the minds of people of small incomes or that functions that prompt to increase the expenditures of false and unnecessary show. In the marriage functions where irrelevant expenditures are made for sake of only show, dealings the show of dowry, all these encourage others also for undue extra expenses. If anyone spends ten thousand the otherone plans for fifteen thousand to show him down and the third one tries to find out any other plan to show his position better than others. Curse to the social copying and imitation that keep us deprived of the living truth! And keep us restrained from exposing our reality! Or it may be said in other words that while exposing our real position, we may feel ashamed. Either the dowry should not be given at all or if given the transaction should be made through cheque which should be without any show of status-symbol. In the marriage, the daughter’s education, abilities and qualities, her moral conduct and health are on priorty. Money is completely subordinate. If there is no show of dowry then who will feel proud of giving dowry?

Beauty-adornments should not be given importance

Today, when we observe the women life, we find the fault of society there also. Why is a young lady fond of decent royal garments, nylone sarees of quite new colours and attractive prints, and new designed ornaments? Why does she want to look in new fashions? Why does she use creams, powder, lipsticks on her face? Why is she so keen in looking so charming?

The reason behind it is that she thinks that she will get the honour of the society by the use of these adornments. It is her understanding that a wife is auspicious to be in the decorated fashions and in the adorned look. That simpleton lives in such a society where to look fashionable and adorned with jewellery is considered to be good; and to remain in half-naked dress, the Western countries are imitated and followed blindly. The society gives more importance to those beauty adornments and fashions; The society gives respect.

In the craze of the social importance the simpleton woman gives up the use of several objects useful and necessary for life. She uses vegetable ghee in place of pure ghee, tea in place of milk but she spends freely for beauty adornments and fashionable garments. The fault goes to the society that accord states to the person on the basis of wrong measures outward show misleads the people.

The public mind does not think seriously going into the depth of the objects. Their mind is immatured. It is influenced by the only outer show. The individual’s life is valued on the basis of his outer appearance. So, it is the need of the time to ban pretentious show.

Cinema should be abhorred

The young boys and girls see the heros and heroines of cinema being honoured by the society as well as the government. The photos of the well decorated heroines are published with a great elegance. The newspapers attract the public attention towards them by publishing their interesting reports. The youths move with the newspapers decorated with the heroines pictures. In the rooms of the houses and in the offices their photos are pasted on the walls or the calenders of their photos are hung on the walls for decoration and honour. When the youths, whether male or female see this honour given to them by the public, the girls also want themselves to become like them. The crime of misguiding them is done by them who have diverted the immatured minds towards the evil paths by giving undue honour to them.

The society has given more importance to the cinema in the daily public life. Cinema has become a very important part of our daily life. The students of immature mind saw the romance and adventures in the films. They imitated them. As a result this class became voluptuous and romantic. The feelings of indiscipline, fashion, sexuality and hooliganism were aroused in the student’s minds.

Now, there is the need to look down upon the cinema with hatred; the heroines should not be given honour. Only the man of character, knowledge and learning, nobility, hard labour etc., should be honoured. The social sanctity and honour should be awarded to them only who have risen up in life by good conduct, restraint, noble behaviour, sacrifice, penance, simplicity and modesty. Thus, to go in the right direction, to think in the right direction should be encouraged. If the society gives due honour and place, to the truthfulness and modesty, the public will make effort to develop the human virtuous qualities being deviated from the attachment of money. Their thought will be diverted towards the higher moral ideals; We will have to give a new ideal lesson to the society.

The social sanctity should be given to the healthy acts of the society only

The whole aim of the true education is not only to make the society devoted to righteous acts but also to develop its taste in them. The society should become pious.

Out of all the purities, the purity of money is the best because the pure money is that which is earned honestly; He is not pure who makes himself pure with the soil and water only.

A thinker has written, ‘Undoubtedly, there are such men who have become rich by the means of injustice, dishonesty, fraud, torture, cunningness, bribery and corruption and today they have become worthy of honour in the society. Know it truly that they cannot be happy and contented. Can they enjoy the least of this wealth pleasantly?

‘No, Never at all. Their soul rebukes them, pinches them, tortures them and afflicts them day and night.’

The learned men should guide the right direction

The responsibility to change the social atmosphere goes to the learned, thinkers, writers, editors, poets, social reformers, political leaders and saints only who preach and teach them with their thoughts, letters and articles, the new thoughts to the people, the new methods of thoughts and let them know to differenciate right and wrong. By their arguments they reach to the definite decisions. Wisdom is the quality of some distinguished persons, it is the personal property of some intellectuals. If these preachers take trouble to divert the social values towards the morality diverting it from the worldly attachments, it can be very beneficial to the society.

Those editors, who are preaching the feeling of sexuality and romanticism, are the public enemies; those who print the romantic, exciting, passionate and attractive photos of the ladies on the front page and are pushing the youths towards sensuousness, are causing great harm to the society. The others will also become like the persons whom they give more importance. So, they should give honour and due respect to the ideal men who are raising up the moral standard of human life higher and they should honour the crest jewels of women. In their papers they should publish the narratives, occurences, stories of only those ideal men who have the ideal worth raising up others higher. The public has gone astray towards corruption to read the dirty literature, romantic tales and narratives and the literature of low grade.

The downfall of literature is the symbol of the down-fall of the nation. That is the true literature that proves beneficial to human being, it means to make the moral uplift of human life, to stimulate the faculty of discrimination. For the mental health, discernment is as important as the health for the body. By the awakening of discrimination, man will automatically be able to discriminate right and wrong. The editors should publish such literature which may develop the reasoning power in human mind and the public may proceed ahead towards divinity. The writers should write such literature where the man may learn the lesson of self-control, he may learn to lead his life in the limited income and may learn to remain contented; He may not allow the growth of his needs, subtle desires and gross desires. By virtue of prolification of such thoughts the atmosphere will be ‘Sattvic’ residing in such atmosphere, the society will itself renounce corruption.

 

Let them be always away from us

Who should accompany us? What should be away from us? These questions have always put the Indian thinkers in complexity.

What should be kept away from us? Our intellectuals have pondered over this question a lot; they have considered over it from many different angles, they have deeply and critically studied on this matter from all point of views. This answer is useful for the progress and development of the human life.

We should be far away from those things that harm us; those evils that hurt our body, mind and soul should be left afar, we should avoid those persons who generate evil in our mind through their association. Our bad habits, bad nature, anguish, disease, lamentation, worry and hostility should be away from us; because all these are unhealthy and harmful. Our scriptures have mentioned those poisonous objects that should remain quite far away from us. As the scriptures say—

Those people should not come in our contact

There are numberless men of different ideals and motives, of different colours, taste, features, natures, attitudes and mental maturity, they are different in habits and living standard. Outwardly all look similar; but all are quite different from each other in their minds, intellects and nature. There is a vast difference in their behaviours like the difference between earth and sky. Some are the source of new inspirations and spirits of courage and progress in our life; and some others may be the source of poisonous habits and ill motives. So, the understanding of good and bad, superior and inferior, progressive and fallen persons is very necessary. So, you should live in the company of the persons of good and virtuous mentality and thoughts and escape from those—

उत वा य: सहस्य प्रविद्वान् मर्तो मर्तं मर्चयति द्वयेन।

अत: पाहि स्तवमान स्तुवन्तमग्ने माकिर्नोदुरिताय धायी:॥

(Rigved 1/147/5)

It means—‘You should always escape from those persons who are always busy in censuring others and fault finding in others because our disposition may be full of blemishes as of those by their association.

Such men always remain busy in the condemnation of others and finding fault in them. There is no moral, worldly, trading and spiritual benefit from these at all. The mean and evil tendency of fault-finding, develops in their company.

We imbibe in ourselves thoughts and habits of those people in whose company we live day and night. Virtues and vices all are infectious. So, the man should always escape from the persons of the mean mentality of censure.

Maintain distance from the ignorants and fools

दीर्घतमा मामतेयो जुजुर्वान् दशमे युगे।

अपामर्थं यतीनां ब्रह्मा भवति सारथि:॥

(Rigved 1/158/6)

It means—‘The ignorant persons (due to their foolishness, ignorance, narrow mindedness and little knowledge) being tempted by greed, suffer from disease and pain; but the noble persons of righteousness, remain always free from bondage by developing their realization and help others also in their deliverance from the worldly ocean.

Ignorance is the cause of unforesightedness. The ignorant person has the narrow outlook. He gives undue importance to those objects which are not valuable at all in reality. The ingnorant persons measure the superiorty or inferiorty of man on the balance of property earned by his parents and forefathers in place of virtues, actions and nature. They misguide even the reasonable persons by their tendency of imitation of others.

A wise foe is better than a fool friend because we are always watchful to him.

Let us always accompany the nobles

Always live in the association of reasonable, learned, cool-minded and balanced persons; so that you may be benefitted by the noble tendency and true knowledge, avail such a company. Maintain distance from the quarrelsome persons of agitating nature.

मा नो अग्नेऽव सृजो अघायाऽविष्यवे रिपवेदुच्छुनायै।

मा दत्वते दशते मादते नो मा रीषते सहसावन् परा दा:॥

(Rigved 1/189/5)

Mind it, you are surrounded by all good and bad persons in the society. There are gentle men of benedictory and modest nature also here poisonous and violent like lion, serpents, scorpions etc., creatures in a large number are hidden. But the poisonous persons of the second category are more in number and remain always in wait to find out way to trouble you.

So, the clever and wise men should escape from these ignoble persons and have the association of noble persons, Adopt the virtuous deeds and spurn the immoral ones.

Our actions never perish. Virtuous and moral actions, service to others and help to others, the noble deeds are fruitful later or sooner certainly. In this world or in the next world it is only the righteousness is supreme. The wise men never appreciate anything better than righteousness.

धर्म एव कृत: श्रेयानिह लोके परत्र च।

तस्माद्धि परमं नास्ति यथा प्राहुर्मनीषिण:॥

‘Keep the company of the religious-minded people. You will obtain from them the profound secrets of life and the world. You will get inspiration to make progressive life from their conduct, speech and action.’

आयुर्नसुलभं लब्ध्वा नावकर्षेद् विशांपते।

उत्कर्षार्थे प्रयतेत नर: पुण्येन कर्मणा॥

Getting this rarely attainable span of life, man should not do any sinful act. A considerate and reasonable man should remain always active in the performance of noble deeds for the progress of the self as well as of the society.

Let us escape from those of bitter tongue

We must always maintain distance from the uncivilized men of hot speech, using always abusive language for others. They are like the beasts and misuse the tongue, the greatest gift to the mankind.

The man using the abusive or obscene language, remains entangled internaly with animatistic tendencies. The abuse is harmful for the society. It is the vice that stimulates the hidden inner sin and evil latencies.

It is always that those who reproach, are terribly afflicted with anger and use piercing bitter words are sick of mind, they can go to any extent in their action. So, better avoid their shadow even.

मा नो निदे च वक्तवेऽर्योरन्धीरराव्णे।

त्वे अपि क्रतुर्मम॥

(Rigved 7/31/5)

‘O Lord! Those who speak harsh and reproachable words, should be avoided at all. Let us not have any concern with the errors of cruelty, rudeness and harshness etc. May my all the actions remain dedicated to you! It means—May I always fulfil noble deeds!’

The rudeness and harshness are the demonic tendencies. These are the symbol of such cruelity that is found in the men of uncivilised and demonic character.

Be pleased and loving. Let your heart always remain liberal for the distressed and afflicted persons.

यो मा पाकेन मनसा

चरन्तमभिचष्टे अनृतेभिर्वचोभि:।

आप इव काशिना संगृभीता

असन्नस्त्वासत इन्द्र वक्ता॥

(Rigved 7/104/8)

‘It means—The untruthful persons telling lies deserve to be secluded. It is better to be away from them.’

How can a liar be your own if he can deceive others? There are hundreds of works in life, which can be harmful due to telling lies. He tells ten bigger lies to cover one lie. So, after testing twice and thrice, it is useful to give up the company of a liar.’

The behaviour of a liar is deceitful and selfish. He can betray even his friends and relatives for the sake of self-interest. Beaware of the selfish and deceits.

यस्तित्याज सचिविदं सखायं न

तस्य वाच्यपि भागो अस्ति।

यदीं शृणोत्यलकं शृणोति नहि

प्रवेद सुकृतस्य पन्थाम्॥

(Rigved 10/71/6)

‘In your life-journey, you will meet such who make friendship with anyone to serve their own interest and when they get their motive fulfilled and their work is done, they give up the friendship. Being deceived once by such deceits, let us be cautious and never trust them. Such fraudulents have to become the victim of reproof, blame and disgrace.

Let the selfish and deceitful persons be away from us. The heartless and curt persons who only think of the harm to others and fail to give any inspiration for the uplift of life, should be kept away.

The desperadoes must be resisted

Let us be away from the wickeds who are harmful for the nation and who don’t hesitate and miss the chance of deceiving for their own petty interest.

Let us remain escaping from the fools causing ill to their own kith and kin and relatives and committing treachery against the motherland.

Let not the anti-social elements who spread the poison of hostility, dispute, fray and sabotage in the society.

यदि नो गां हंसि यद्यश्वं यदि पूरुषम््।

तं त्वा सीसेन विध्यामो यथा नोऽसो अवीरहा॥

(Atharvaved 1/16/4)

‘He who destroys our animal property as cow etc, is liable to be punished. It means, he who violates the human interest and commit anti social actions, should be protested boldly and bravely.’

In the interest of the society the individual and family interest is inherent. So, anti-social tendency should be checked forever. It is proper. Every individual of the society is entitled of the full and equal opportunity of education, development and progress.

य: सपत्नो योऽसपत्नो यश्च द्विषन् छपाति न:।

देवास्तं सर्वे धूर्वन्तु ब्रह्म वर्म ममान्तरम्॥

(Atharvaved 1/19/4)

It means—‘Let us destroy him who wants to do sabotage in our society and destroy our high moral interests. Self-protection from the wickeds is must. Usually, the main cause of the harm to the people is failing to distinguish the evil-minded persons rightly. So, the discriminative sense of recognising the good and bad must remain in our mind.’

व्याघ्रं दत्वतां वयं प्रथमं जम्भयामसि।

आ दुष्टेनमथो अहिं यातुधानमथो वृकम्॥

(Atharvaved 4/3/4)

It means—‘It is the moral duty to destroy the thieves, scoundrels of demonic character like the violent creatures of wicked nature. We should continue the prevention of such types of lewds, thieves, violence, hostility, the disease of selfish tendency and other evils.’

Numberless violent animals and demons in the form of mankind are present in our society. Their outer appearance is like man but they are internally filled with animal instincts. Just as the scorpion’s nature is to sting and the serpent’s nature is to bite, so are these wicked persons harmful to the society. We must remain beaware of them! Remain escaping from them!

The demoniac sentiment through human beings which is spreading, may not affect us! Let not the spirituality be forgotten in the dazzling of materialism. It is the greatest need of the time to make the righteousness practical. No doubt, the science should flourish but not at the cost of human character.

 

Be aware of the rumours

Rumour is harmful for the both individual as well as the society. Its base is the use of the imaginary power of man in the wrong direction. Fear is a strong mental impulse of man. Usually, the fear perturbs all the living beings, but the man comes to use his imagination in the wrong direction joining his intellect with fear by the rumours. Those who spread rumours, corrupt the public mind and divert them from the right path by making the irresponsible talks among the people of the vicinity and create the polluted atmosphere of terror and perturbance among the uneducated and innocent public. The public starts taking interest in the talks of fear and danger generally without thinking deeply. The innocent people reckon the fear double or four times more through their imaginary power. Sometimes, the rumours have very dangerous effect. The fear gets instilled in the mind of the public very soon and hearing the wrong informations again and again it takes the shape of mental complex.

Impact on the soldiers

The psychologist writer Prof. Laljiramji Shukla writes describing the reaction of the rumours—‘In the war period of hearing the false propoganda and poisonous rumours some soldiers suffer abruptly by the attack of paralysis. There is no deformation in limbs of their bodies, but they cannot be used for duty. After the mental study of such coward persons it has come to notice that they were frightened by their inner heart from the fear of the dreadful sights of the war and butchering; but they did not accept this fear outwardly. Their ambition to show their heroism to the other soldiers did not allow them to accept this fear. Such persons used to boast of their valour before other soldiers. A ball of cannon fell down before such a soldier boasting of his heroism and it burst out. Only its sight made him unconscious.

The cannon-ball had no hurt on his body; but as a result of fear his mouth opened. Then, he continued in the same condition. Due to fear, it was a mental paralysis in his opened mouth. When by the mental treatment the purgation of the fear hidden in his inner mind was made, his mouth could be closed then. Thus, the mental complex of imaginary fear creates extraordinary kinds of great fear in the minds of men.

The rumours are infectious

The mental disorders are created only by the sight, imagination and hearing of certain rumours like the infectious wicked diseases. Suppose, any party or group is interested to serve its purpose or any enemy wants to make any country coward, he starts repeating such wrong rumours again and again through his preachers, secret agents or radio, which has a very bad and poisonous effect on man’s unconscious mind. The majority of the public is innocent and uneducated. If the fear or terror have made their roots deep in the mind, the public begins to turn their imaginations towards the directions of inauspicious imaginations of downfalls, weakness, defeat, sorrow and imaginary pain etc., These inauspicious imaginations spread from individual to individual, family to family, in the streets and Mohallas in schools and then in the whole village and city. The inauspicious imaginations make the soldiers fighting in the war and the citizens worthless and impotent by creating the cowardice feeling. These rumours make even the whole city deserted. Man’s prowess, vigour, patience, courage working capacity is destroyed.

So, it is very necessary to be aware of the rumours in the present difficult times. Neither we should take interest in hearing the rumours nor should we share in spreading it. But it is needed that the rumours originating harmful imaginations should be repudiated at once and such thoughts which are encouraging and strengthening to the faith in the victory should be spread over among the public. By the propoganda of right and courageous thoughts the fear and confusions of the public will be swept away and even in the most horrible circumstances, they will be able to face the enemy without any perturbation.

The reason behind the victory of the Britishers

The burning example of a country going to be defeated in reality, how it can change the defeat into a victory is being quoted here. In the last great war, when in the war of Dankark, the British army could not stay before the Germans and when they had to cross the English channel giving in badly, the atmosphere of disappointment spread all over England. Till then, almost all the European countries hostile to Germany had already surrendered before Germany. No army could stand before Germany. So, in this hour of distress, the Britisher’s condition was miserable. If Britishers mind had not been made free from fear and disappointment and there had not been generated the petals of hopeful imagination in their mind, the Britishers would have been defeated.

At that critical time the public imaginations were stimulated towards the hopeful thoughts of victory. This thought was propogated that the Britisher may lose the small wars but they are always winners in the big wars. By this good thought the thought of hidden fear changed into hope. As a result, the Britishers didn’t give in before Hitler. They remained facing them boldly. The outer circumstances also favoured them. The Russians who were at daggers drawn, having joined them as friend began to fight against Germans. On the otherside, America, too, supported them with man and money. Thus, by the right use of imagination the defeat turned to victory.

Neither accept that of which you have no confirmation of its truth; nor say to anybody. Such matters are the origin of cowardice mind and they are harmful to the nation.

Those who make the mountain of a mole hill with great elation they concoct glories without head and tail. Let us be very careful from them. By spreading rumours and getting others entangled with them, they take nasty enjoyment in becoming leader achieving their objective and diverting the innocent and uneducated public from the right path.

It is just possible that the enemy may be spreading the rumour. So, a minute watch should be kept on those who spread such rumours or describe it in a dramatic way.

In the war period, only the matters of the public welfare are useful. So, the auspicious imaginations of the enemy’s defeat and the victory of our nation should be made. Instead of believing in the rumours of others, find out the truth yourself.

 

Blind faith is the bane for religion

Regarding religion different wrong and illogical concepts are a mental disease. In the primary stage of the mental development, the wild men did not understand the truth of religion. Their understanding, their reasoning, contemplation and their mind all were undeveloped. They measured the religion by illogical means. They used to be fancy of the devils, ghosts, mesmerizing, enchantment and spell and bad customs to be free from that what frightened them. The so called fraudulent Sadhus used to show, deceitful wonderful miracles. Such fraudulents have made the religion very much defamed and caused a great harm to the innocent emotional public. The reasonable and educated persons mostly are acquainted with the ominous result of superstitions and they are in practice of reading such bad occurences in the newspapers but the backwards need to remain very cautious from these knaves. This abominable superstition can never be the part of religion. The forts of heresy will have to be tumbled down. Go through some fresh news; what foolish acts are done by the unwise superstitious persons.

Burnt the hut on fire

In the village Patauli under the Gurugaon area, a woman lit fire to nine huts. It is not known who was that deceitful person who had instilled her mind with the superstition that she would be blessed with son by doing so. She narrated that any one practicising occult art sitting on the roadside, had suggested an issueless lady that if she lit fire at least six huts, she would be able to conceive child. Ignorant and superstitious that foolish lady came to belive this the right way and she burnt the huts to ashes. Later on, this lady was presented before the Panchayat. The Panchayat punished her with the penalty of Rupees one hundred on the charge of burning the huts.

Offered the tongue to Shankarji

It was reported in a news of the district Ramgarh that a man offered his tongue having cut it, to the Lord Shiva in the local temple of Lord Shiva. This man had no issue. At last, he wished the blessing of Lord Shiva to get a son by offering his tongue. It is a false conviction that the god-goddesses are pleased by getting the sacrifices of men and animals or such other offering.

To please the goddess—Mother Kali

A resident of Mohalla—kela of Gaziabad, named, Hari Singh was sentenced to life-imprisonment in connection with the crime of murdering his four years old son—Virendra. According to the crime report, the accused cut the neck of his son with big knife and he went to the goddess-temple to offer his son’s blood to the mother kali. The other devotees there, caught him and handed overt to the police. How many innocent people, it is not known, have to lose their money, morality, religion, life and body by being entangled into the trap of false superstitions to please the gods and goddesses.

The means of getting boon from the goddess

A refugee young man, named, Kartar Chand in Amritsar made up his mind to sacrifice himself to please the mother Kali. The youngone tried to cut his neck with razor before the goddess, but at once, he was got admitted in the hospital, where he could be out of danger by the difficult efforts of the doctors. According to the police report, the young man was suspicious of his wife’s infidelity. He prayed to the goddess to reform her habits and character and desired to offer his own sacrifice. Such fools will be called a sinner only.

The human sacrifice to please God

The Chanda district police had arrested three Gonds on the charge of a human-sacrifice. It was their misconception that the cause of not raining was the displeasure of Indra and there was no possibility of rain without offering him human sacrifices. By leading astray a man, they took him away before the Gond-god in the dense forest and made his methodical worship and then sacrificed him. Some of his blood was offered to the god and the rest remaining was distributed among themselves. It is a matter of great sorrow that what a heinous crime a man comes to commit because of his foolishness!

In the temptation of Lord’s Sight

In Agra, a twenty-two years old man, named Shriniwas, having cut his neck, offered it before the idol in the Parasuram temple, near Renuka village. His desire was to view the sight of the Lord as soon as possible by reaching the heaven. Srinivas died at once. According to an eye-witness, that youth had first sprinkled his blood on the idol having taken it out of his head and chest. What a foolishness!

An unique fire-trance

It sank in the mind of a 60 years old hermit that the salvation is attained by the self through fire trance. In a village, near the village Pilparia, he abandoned his life by fire-trance. It is said that the hermit made pyre himself with his own hands before his hut on the Panchmarhi road at a deserted lonely place two days before and after the performance of different religious rites and after reverential song of hymn and worship, he lit fire to the pyre. When the pyre began to burn in blazing flames, he jumped into the flaming fire. In a little time, his body was burnt to ashes.

Such a delusion in mind regarding salvation is very devastating.

For the temptation of the goddess-Bhawani’s vision

A resident of a village, named Jihadpur, about eight miles away from Khurja, observed fast of nine days on the festive of ‘Navratra’ in the last days and repeated the name of the goddess. He was expecting since long that the goddess would bless him with Her sight apparently. Even after the long prayer, when the goddess did not appear before him, being overpowered in emotion, he pierced dagger in his neck and died. It was a wrong notion in his mind that the goddess having appeared would save her devotee.

The Sacrifice of the Child

The district and Session Judge of Indore, Shri Kale sentenced life imprisonment to a twenty-two year old woman of the village, Chimali. It is said that this woman committed the murder of a ten years old child of the other one for the well-being of her one year old child. Someone had instilled in her mind the superstition that her child would remain alive only then, in case she would drink the water mixed with the ashes of the hair of the child having been murdered and burnt by her. Earlier her two children had already died.

By such superstitions what more except repentence can be attained? These superstitions are the examples of our ignorance and foolishness. Behind the curtain of the religion, hundreds of occurences of such types happen daily. The social sanctity of such wrong, confusing and harmful beliefs should never be given the name of religion. The spells, enchantments, miracles etc., and are generally the selfish means to mislead and cheat the common public. They are harmful, both directly and indirectly and worth abandoning. We should assess every fact with our intelligence, logic and reality and oppose every false, harmful and polluted customs, confused mentality and bad conceptions and condemn them boldly with courage.

 

Elder in age even are you not a child in mentality?

We treat the child-behaviour affectionately and fondly being considerate. They are perplexed in no time in conversation, living way, behaviour and conduct, sorrow and pain. The least problem makes them nervous. They become disturbed by the imaginary fears at once suddenly. Feeling appetite they become restless and start weeping. If their toy is broken, if they happen to see any nightmare, if they have to stay in dark, they are perturbed badly. If they are separated from the brother, sister, mother, father and put alone, they become faded and start weeping and shrieking. They quarrel on triffling matters. They smile elatedly even to get a small toy, a little sweet, a few coins. They take keen interest in the coloured garments.

There is a change every moment in their thinking power and way of thinking in their liking and taste. Today they say something but the next day, they are obstinate for any new item.

They are so emotional that they are influenced by greed, hostility, jealousy, agitation, anger, joy, anxiety on any matter of little importance.

Are these bad tendencies found in the children, present in you also? Your body has advanced in age; the moustaches and beards have already grown on your face, but yet you are mentally a child only.

Isn’t it that you are disappointed with a little difficulty or opposition? Are your emotional feelings of joy and sorrow go on rising and falling like the waves similarly of a child? Do you make of a mole hill mountain by the misuse of your imagination? Excess of sentimental trait is a dreadful vice. Children swim on the waves of sentiments. You should use your steady wit in your actions. You should be firm in your resolves.

According to your developed mental condition you should perform your action.

Now you are grown up and matured. Your mind should also develop in the same proportion of your physical development. Use your power of thought and wisdom in place of emotion. Restrain the flood of your emotion and passion completely. To be perturbed by petty troubles is the indication of your childish character.

A child provokes like a blast on a triffling issue; but you should remain calm and restrained. Have control over your emotions and passions. Maintain the balance of your mind and remain peaceful. Practise work with cool mind and firm hands.

A child avoids the uninteresting hard works. But you should give priorty to hard works. It is the job of the developed mind to find the solution of the hardest and most difficult problems. Learn to face this cruel heartless and kindless world with peaceful and fearless mind.

A developed and matured person’s two powers are very important—Discernment and intelligence. You have to use them in your performances throughout your life. These qualities teach you to have overcome the adverse circumstances. Go on developing these qualities more and more.

You are glorious. You are a mass of vitality and lustre. You are ever victorious and renowned like Indra. You are alone equal to ten thousand. Your sprirt has the vigour of ten thousand. Don’t consider yourself a child. Always remain prompt to shoulder the social, moral, domestic, responsibility of the developed mankind.

Like the children, don’t waste your time in decoration, fashion, artificial show, tip-top, dance, enjoyments and momentary tongue-taste; lead a life of ‘simple living and high thinking.’

You are the self-confident citizen worthy of shouldering the complete responsibility.

 

The secret practice of progress

There are two parts of human nature—The one part of human mind is indolent, carefree, lazy, and pushing towards downfall; but the second is the part that inspires him towards progress, awakening, permanent gain and superiority. In other words it may be called the inner spirit also. Both of these parts want to dominate the man turn by turn. Its result are decided by the talent and wisdom or reason. He who is guided by reason despite the difficulties and reverse circumstances sets on the path of prosperity, glory and progress like a lotus of the mud. He who is dominated by wicked propensity or evil wit, in spite of favourable circumstances, falls down and goes towards decline. As the path of decline is sloping if he falls once, he goes on slipping to downfall. He who goes ahead towards progress, is considered ideal in the eyes of the society. People remember him only. His parents and family members don’t have the consideration of his primary conditions at all. They forget it.

None can be glorious or reputed for a long time on the basis of his old family reputation, property, prosperity, noble deeds, glory or richness. The element of repute lies in the man. It is his own character, habits, nature and way of action that determine his popularity. Man has his own individual importance in every direction. He has his own original way of action. This is his quality. On the basis of his this originality the people have amazed the world.

Numberless famous and great persons came into existence, who were in the detestable condition primarily, but they were enlightened abruptly with their distinguished characteristics, divine gift and hidden virtues in them; a kind of quite new awakening was created and they set a wonderful example of their action.

You will be able to understand this rule when you also come to know your qualities and virtues. The moment you recognise your worth, your life-cycle—will turn over. So, don’t be disappointed, don’t be lazy, well! Be mindful of your thoughts direction. What is your inner voice? How are your habits? Be alert of your being addicted of intoxication or you are falling into a bad company? Be careful whether you are proceeding towards progress or downfall?

Keep it in your mind that God exists in you and you are blessed with His potency. Mind, soul and body are the treasure of wonderful hidden powers. You are lying in the undeveloped condition and dashing the days. You are considering the life worthless, empty and purposeless. But you are born to become a very valuable man. You have come here to rule. A big goal inheres you.

A man can do anything if he has firm resolve. Every firm resolve has a great power. Pity it is he does not want it with firmness. If there is no will, he can do nothing. So, it is clear that first you should have a strong firm, indomitable will in you to achieve your goal.

Generally, the people go on the same track of their forefathers. They don’t think anew. They remain in the same condition. Their mind does not work in any new direction of progress. Their talent does not practise in the new directions. Their imaginations are not creative. In this way, they remain traditionalist. They become habituated of the family-traditional work since their birth. They understand that their luck may favour them even in their traditional profession, work or service. But several times the people made wonderful progress by adopting the professions apart from their traditional profession. Here is the point to think, contemplate and imagine on the new line. Just see the world, analyse the social activities, judge the people’s mentality study deeply their nature and tendency, concentrate your look towards new direction. Be sure that there are still a lot of new works remaining to be done and specially they are left to be done with your hands. New business, new inventions, new progress all belong to your luck. Every moment of life is a new opportunity of progress for a man who finds out a new way to prosper after a new and well consideration and contemplation with courage, enthusiasm and self-confidence.

There are many people of the understanding that the opportunity of uplift comes only but once. A friend of mine failed in an interview, the other gentleman’s number was eleventh, as in high rank services only ten candidates are selected. The both gentlemen are now frustrated. They say—‘What to say, my heart was broken. All the hopes of life shattered and now what is there in future for me? Now, my life got ruined. This world is useless for me. I would like to suggest such exasperated and disappointed persons that there are ups and downs at every step of life. We are bound to tolerate such bitter moments in life. On the path of life, the thorns pierce into our feet certainly, but the opportunities of progress and development are ready to welcome us not only once but a number of times. These opportunities come to us in different ways and through different means but to take advantage or to ignore it, is our right and depending on use of our intelligence. Generally, it is found that they are not utilized as they ought to be. We should be very careful to have the minute observation of the ups and downs of our life as well as of the society every day, every month and every year that whether we are proceeding ahead or going back in the field of business and in the mental, intellectual, economic, social, moral and religious field or we stand static.

Mind the chief points—‘Don’t be afraid of the difficulties. The path of progress is thorny at every step. It is you to make your own path. It is you to remove the pebbles and thorns of your path yourself. Difficulties should be inspiring to you, it should generate in you the new freshness and courage to move onward on the path of progress day by day constantly. Your self-confidence should be very strong. The difficulties are the best teacher in our life. Just as a wrestler grows his physical strength daily constantly slowly and slowly by wrestling with his rival, being defeated again and again, covered with dust and becomes strong, in the same way, every difficulty makes us strong and firm by anyway in case we don’t accept our defeat. We may fall down but we should rise up again having waved off our dust. He who becomes ready everytime again and again to fight a wrestling with the difficulties, possesses the higher qualities of progress, as courage, labour and effort and a new hope to win. The courageous and self-confident men are contented only after beating the difficulties—

A thinker’s these valuable words deserve to be saved tightly—‘In the world trouble is not impossible but it is necessary. It is sure to come, the hardships born of irresponsible and coward persons are in abundance in the world. Any of them may befall any time to oppress the weak. Not to allow the difficulties to be created from our own side and face the hardships created by others is a lofty character of man. Man should remain always ready to dash against the terrible hardships. The hardships may affect anyone either good or bad; but he who has the strong force of character the splendour of thoughts and spiritual light will overcome them smiling like the full moon of eclipse.

He who is weak in character, shattered and coward and black-hearted should be declared as a suicider. He will fall down having been broken by a mild shake of the hardship like a broken star.

 

The difficulties are beneficial also difficulties make us strong
