As a wrestler becomes strong being knocked down again and again in the wrestling and gets physical strength in the same way in the wrestling of life, a man becomes powerful by struggling the difficulties. He adds to his self-confidence. That developed self-confidence is the root of all victories.

You should greet the difficulties. You should beat them by your self-confidence. The victory over your every difficulty is the constant source to increase fortitude and courage.

You should be always ready to meet the difficulties whatsoever may be. The more you suffer from the hardships, the more easy will be your path of progress. Difficulties make us strong.

You are ambitious of progress and its cost is ‘Difficulty’—If you can pay this cost, there is no delay in getting the progress and success because the object is available to him only who pays its full cost. There is no suspicion about the accomplishment of the work for him who can pay the real price in the form of labour in the right way.

Difficulties strengthen our self-confidence

Your circumstances might be of any sort always go on striving with your self-spirit to move onward. Don’t be nervous with the hardship and miseries. When you are successful in overcoming them, you will feel a great pleasure to see your courage and prowess exceeding. Never be in dark that you are not in gain by any certain difficulty or misery or work. It is your illusion to consider the difficulty a misery or a burden; it is your false timidity and fear which is dashing you towards down-fall. By fighting the war against the miseries and pain and to stick stubbornly against them, you will evolve yourself morally and spiritually. You will rise above the common condition of your life and the world will honour you.

The heroes unfrightened from difficulties

You are well known with the hardships of the prince, Gautam Buddha. He performed hard penance sitting in the caves of the mountains. Hundreds of obstacles and hardships came before him. His body turned to skleton, the violent wild beasts attacked him, he suffered cold-heat-storm etc., but he remained firm on his Sattvic resolve.

As emerging from the mountain the spring of fountain ultimately makes its way breaking and dashing against the stones of the hill, similarily the courageous persons of firm determination and courage at last reach their goal removing all the obstacles of their way.

Maharana Pratap Singh’s life is an example of a courageous fighting war against hardships throughout his life. Pratap’s life clears to wage war for freedom without any comfort and means from the opponents and constantly moving onward towards his highest goat. You are also the modern Pratap.

In his small age the Mughal Emperor had become his enemy. His opponents were present all around him. The greedy persons of wealth were thirsty of his life. His own well-wishers and related to him were playing in the hands of Muslim rulers. Except a handful of patriots there was none his follower. He had only courage and spiritual power with him. With its support only he blew the trumpet of freedom. This was the only ambition of Pratap’s life—the liberation of Mewar. Just imagine, without any strong support he had jumped into the great sea of Mughal army taking the strength of his own hands. Hungry and thirsty he remained wandering about from forest to forest. His wife and children were pining for food and shelter, they remained distressed, restless and suffering from hardships. Ultimately his army had been defeated but he had never lost his courage. He never felt disappointed. He used to call the hardships as the mountain of cotton to be destroyed without effort. You are also expected of the same courage, same firmness and gradual awakening of duty.

The great hero Puru

Sikandar was dreaming of conquering the whole world; He had overcome several hardships with courage. He was coming to India from a foreign country to rob India and subdue it under him. His army was expert and well-skilled. He had the best quality of war weapons and war materials. He had already won many states of Punjab, but he had to face such an Indian warrior, who was the crown of India. Even today he is reverent in heroism. He was the king of a small state near the Jhelum river. His name was Puru. He had faced Sikandar with his very poor strength and had harassed him. A fierce war had broken out. In the war Puru had to suffer a great loss but he had not cared even to sacrifice his life to protect the freedom of his country. Unfortunately the brave Puru was arrested but he was the embodiment of courage. Sikandar asked the arrested Puru—‘O the Prisoner! How should you be treated?’ The brave was not a man to be perturbed by the hardships. Even among the men of his enemy he remained stood fearlessly. He answered boldly—‘Treat me as a king treats to a king. An Indian brave is never afraid of difficulties.’

All were striken dumb to hear his bold words. Sikandar, too was amazed.

The Indian braves are never perturbed in hardships. You have got the blood of the same braves, the same hero deserving emotions and the same admirable heroic traditions.

Go ahead on all the fronts of life

Whatsoever the situations may be but there are opportunities in all the spheres of life to move ahead. There are four aspects of human life—domestic, social, cultural and spiritual. Ponder over all these aspects carefully and judge yourself where you stand. In which condition and how far are you backward? Then, start from there to go ahead. How should be your family life, your wife, your children, your relatives, kith and kin prosper? By whom should they prosper? How should you enjoy the honourable status among your friends, your acquainted ones and the society? How to advance in the field of recreation, Art, music, tours etc., with cultural point of view? How to advance in moral, religious and spiritual world? All these fields are open to you equally for progress. Solve the problems there. Take equal interest in them. Make effort to be champion in all the fields. You will find how splendid and grand your life is.

The victory over every hardship will give you pleasure. Learn the art to take advantage from the miseries. You don’t think of your condition yourself and so remain inactive. If you make the true effort to go ahead, knowing your weakness the progress is sure.

Those who make efforts, reach the top

Remember it, those men who are ambitious of progress and are courageous, fast and hard working, reach the peak; but the lazy and cowards remain there and there only. Those who don’t make effort and are deprived of viewing all the sides, pros and cons are foolish and remain always rotting themselves. By shouldering the responsibility and doing it whole-heartedly we gain strength. The bigger responsibility, one takes the higher position; glory and repute he gains, The great men have never got frightened by new and hard responsibility. High thinking, new plans and constant labour are must to become a great man. These are those factors, which have been practised by every great man.

They were always confident of their ability. They knew their duty. They did the work whole-heartedly. Their self-confidence is the root of their success. They, who are not confident of fulfilling their job and are doubtful in the beginning of the work, who have the false imaginations and feeling of doubts of hurdles and hardship in their hidden mind, are unable to start the work even. Those who achieve the high posts, have to face the great adversities; opposition and troubles. Many great inventors have been inventing new inventions by remaining busy in their researches throughout their lives with hard labour but their work could not be fulfilled and they passed away from the world. Some were ridiculed by their companions, they were caused trouble, created many obstacles in their experiments even the primary needs of their lives could not be fulfilled; but they remained dedicated to their work and remained trying firmly to get even a little success. In the end they got fame and renown, one to them other thousands of men got overflowed with riches. Hard earned money leads to progress.

Everyone wants to do something but he does not want to take any trouble or does labour to do it. He does not take whole-hearted interest to accomplish it; in other words it may be said that he sows vice and wants to reap virtue. It is sure that such false dreamers fail in their goal and blame their destiny or God for this.

If a man is devoted with a firm determination mentally and physically to achieve his goal, it is dead sure that he can accomplish his aim. They, who are determined in their mind to do any work, never care for obstacles and hurdles. They do not feel any obstacle. In the path of progress, the difficulties come only to the cowards and fickle-minded people. The difficulties run away before the firm determination. They do the work of a guide on the path to the progressive men, ambitious of progress.

The storms are to be faced

Never think that your life-boat will be sailing always secure and balanced. The troublesome paths will also come across. The pebbles, stones and thorns will also pierce. There will be blow of wind and storms also. The suffering will also clash. Actually all these occur to test your firmness. Be careful lest the rush should dash you.

In the path of progress, fear and doubts are such mental demerits which detain a man far behind. Fear whispers your ear—don’t do so otherwise it may be defective. Your entire prowess will be fruitless.

On account of this doubt in place of doing our duty sincerely and perfectly, we lose it. Because of the doubtful and suspicious mentality, we build such walls around us that we fail to find any gate to go out. In such a declined situation we can never progress.

For the accomplishment of any big work and progress we have the great need of courage, firm determination and fearlessness. To initiate and awaken the prowess, latent in our mind, in the ancient time the Gurus used to say in the ear of the pupil— You are the form of ‘Brahma; root this mantra in your hidden mind. Say with full self-confidence—‘I am the form of Brahma. I am the brave son of the Lord. I will not sit without attaining the high status.

 

The sensitive nature is very harmful for life

The great poet of English Literature John Keats died in his blossoming young age of 27. He was not suffering from any disease. The circumstances of his death period were somewhat as follows.

Keats was a well versed poet. He used to compose romantic poems. All appreciated his poems open-heartedly. He had an honourable position in the poetic world.

Once, by chance, a destructive article against him was published in a critical magazine. It had been written in personal enmity and jealousy. Here, he had been indulged in false denunciatory remarks. He had been blamed for false and baseless allegations only to defame him and take revenge of the old hostility. Keats read this criticism and it had a dangerous effect on his sensitive mind. He fell ill due to this mental agony and died in his prime age being the patient of T.B.

Just, imagine, in the prime of youth, when the people enter the active field of life by ceremonising the wedding, in the same young age that poor emotional poet died on account of his sensitive nature. Such an unimportant reason, the baseless criticism and the weakness of the poet that considering it true he got mentaly disturbed and frustrated inwardly! And that shock dragged him to death. It is clear that the poet had no courage and strength to tolerate his slander. He had no inner power to protect himself from the outer demoniac force. He was unaware that the sensitive nature could be the cause of death. The excess of emotion can also push into the jaws of death.

King Dasharath died due to the severe shock of separation

Maryada Purushottam Shri Ram was departing to serve the banishment. The entire Ayodhya was grief-stricken. The citizens were weeping bitterly: many had fallen down being fainted. In the royal palace, the mothers were wailing pathetically in lamentation. All the family members were in tears in the grief.

The women are more tender-hearted than the men. Very simple matters have very bad impact on them. It was simple and natural for Kausalya, the mother of Sri Ram to be more affected by her son’s separation. Her only son was departing from her in the full young age with his wife to wander about in the forest leaving her alone lamenting. It was a very pathetic sight. The whole Ayodhya was afflicted with the dark cloud of anguish.

Really, the mother Kausalya and the father Dasharath both were distressed. Probably Kausalyaji was more anguished than Dasharath, but Kausalyaji was more considerate and tolerant while Dasharathji was of sensitive nature. He was very tender-hearted and emotional and his this emotion and sensitive nature took his life. He could not bear the mental shock.

The sensitive plant fades away only by touch. The men of such nature also come to disorder only by the mild blow of opposition, reproach, sorrow and hardships. Their mental balance is disturbed. They come to sudden perturbation. This type of emotion is a big demerit. This excess of emotion results in dreadfulness. So, being free from sensitive nature one should adopt tolerance.

This world is full of bad elements people resorting to Uselessly and habituals of condemnation are in abundance in the society and they are like serpents and scorpions. The thieves, robbers, crookeds, sinners and demons are used to creating obstacles even in noble deeds. The demons create disturbance in the penances of the sages. Ultimately, Maryada Purushottam Sri Ram had to use his bow against the torture.

Don’t be afraid of reproach without any reason

In every country of the world and in all ages all the altruistics, the benefactors of the human beings, progressive, benevolent great souls have been reproofed; that is in practice even today and will continue in future also. The mutual hostility, censure and jealousy are in the nature of the men of demoniac character. No great man or leader has escaped from censure.

Generally, this reproach is baseless and guided by the ill motive of revenge behind the back. Some persons of polluted mentality are jealous of your outstanding ability and virtues and so they want to create hurdle in your progress. When they, themselves fail in their motive, they provoke others by back-biting. To tolerate such baseless reproach and without any reaction of annoyance and digest the poison of reproach like the poison as Lord Shiva drank, is the great quality of man. This spirit of tolerance should be developed.

The great men have paid no heed to the censure. On the other hand they have taken its advantage. Censure has a great gain that the liking of the public comes to notice very easily. Mostly that, which is the liking of the majority becomes the issue of censure. The popularity expands by reproach. By the pretence of reproof, people usually try to understand the public servants. Indirectly, censure is the mental reaction of man’s popularity.

The reprover practises the means of back-biting because he spreads the false rumours which have no base at all. He fears to speak openly before you.

Anyone, ambitious of progress should not deviate from his goal by being disheartened by the short-lived baseless reproach. He who can tolerate the condemnation, is capable of bearing the great sufferings of the world.

Need not lose the mental balance at the time of censure and miseries

The words of Prince Vismark are the words of great experience—

‘At the moment of censure of any kind or at the moment of opposition, a man should protect himself from the mental shock that can make us empty of courage by causing wound to our mind like with the fall of rock. Let coolness remain pervading in our mind! Let our mind remain fully balanced! If our mind is depressed or gets frightened, it should be considered that all the arms and weapons have been snatched away, all the weapons and means to face the adversities ended.’

To protect the mind from the mental shock the easiest way is—‘neutrality’. In other words by making yourself neutral from the hardship, study it as if you are unconcerned and the hardship is there on the other one’s head and you are a mere spectator.

James Allen’s example

The great soul, St. James Allen has written in one of his memories—I have found two men of my acquaintances whose earning of the whole life was destroyed at a time. One day, in the morning he read in the newspaper that the bank where they had their deposits, became bankrupt. Just reading this news one of them was so much shocked that his mind failed. He became mad. It was because of his excessive emotional mind.

But the second one who was not afraid of the adversities the least, said with a serious smile—‘Alright! God always does better for us. The earning of my whole life went now out of my hands. That money cannot be obtained again by my mourning, but yes, that can be earned again by labour. I lost my money only, at least I did not lose my hands, legs and enthusiasm. I will earn again.’

Thinking so, that man again engaged himself in the work with new zeal and firm self-confidence and in a short time he became rich again; but the emotional man remained mourning weeping and beating his chest. He caught the way of disappointment instead of being industrious which made him the victim of misery, growing day by day miserable.

The mind should be made tolerant.

Make the mind tolerant

It has been said in our culture—

उत वा य: सहस्य प्रविद्वान् मर्तोर्मतं मर्चयति द्वयेन।

अत: पाहि स्तवमान स्तुवन्तुमग्ने माकिर्नोदुरिताय धायी:॥

(Rigved 1/147/5)

It means—(‘There are many persons to reproach) and to harbour malice. They who are always busy in reproofing and fault-finding in others, deserve to be left away by the understanding men because their company transforms us in a reproover.’

दीर्घतमा मामतेयो जुजुर्वान् दशमे युगे।

अपामर्थं यतीनां ब्रह्म भवति सारथि:॥

(Rigved 1/158/6)

Remember it—‘The ignorant persons being overpowered by greed because of shock and sorrow (due to emotion) suffer from great distress; but the men of morality and nobility, and of firm resolve and prowess, growing their knowledge and realization become liberated from the worldly bondage and liberate others also from this worldly ocean by their examples.’

मा नो अग्नेऽव सृजो अघायाऽविष्यवे रिपवेदुच्छुनायै।

मादत्वते दशते मादते नो मा रीषतेसहसावन् परा दा:॥

(Rigved 1/189/5)

Remember it—‘There are all types of creatures—good and bad here in this world. Here on one side if there are men of auspicious and modest nature and noble persons, then on the other side there are lions, serpents, scorpions etc., violent and poisonous living-creatures also. They are covering the society hidden here and there. Therefore, men of understanding should seek the company of noble persons escaping from wicked persons and their baseless censure. If in fact there are bad habits and vices in our character. We should make effort with indomitable will to remove them so that none may get any chance to condemn—

क्रत्व: समह दीनता प्रतीपं जगमा शुचे।

मृळा सुक्षत्र मृळया॥

(Rigved 7/89/3)

It means—‘God as witness, go on admitting your errors, shortcomings, vices and evil deeds so that there may not be slackness in removing them. This is my prayer to God—

‘O the Lord! free me from vices!’

Give up the sensitive nature. If anyone opposes you without any reason, don’t pay any heed to his reproach. People always condemn the good, the persons eager to uplift, constantly go on progress and uplifting. They never care for the social critics and jealous persons. The great men have to make their way of progress through the adverse rivals and hard struggles. The people could not estimate them and remained opposing for the sake of opposition only. Ultimately they won completely. Form your habit to remain balanced even in the condition of bitter criticism, censure, bitter words and opposition. Tolerance is the divine quality of human being. Develop it. If anyone says ill, don’t take it ill. Make your nature tolerant. Keep in mind—

मा शपन्तं प्रति वोचे देवयन्तम्।

(Rigved. 1/41/8)

‘Cast out the wickeds creating obstacles in the virtues. Consider them mean, deserving of hatred like the demons who create hindrance in the virtuous deeds.

 

Free your mind from imaginary fears

You are worried uselessly with an imaginary fear hidden in your mind. The fear of death, the fear of abashment, the fear of attack by anyone, the fear of being oppressed by the enemies, the fear of the devils and ghosts in the night, the fear of the loss in the business, the fear of dismissal from service, the fear of deterioration in health, the fear of loafing of children or the fear of loss of accumulated capital—these or numerous fears like this usually disturb your mind day and night.

Believe truly that most of such fears are only the creation of imagination point blank and they are never to cause you any harm. You have got them in vain secretly rooted in your mind being afraid of them in vain.

Ninety percent cowards are disturbed because of imaginary fears but practically they never happen visit in their real life. The practice of fear becomes their habit. In every condition and situation they find themselves afraid of. The long stay of fear in the mind, makes us coward and timid, The prowess of a coward is lost.

Such a man can never do any work of courage. The habit of his timidity makes him unsuccessful in every sphere of life.

The cowards always think—‘I am nothing. I am a mean. Any big work of importance is not possible to be done by me. I am helpless, mean and destitute. Others are superior to me in knowledge, talent, strength, capability, shrewdness and they are better than I, they are endowed with all the qualities.’ The feelings of inferiority are hurdles in the right development of a man. Due to the root of fear in the mind, man’s valuable inner plans are destroyed in the dust within a moment.

Fear is the indication of our ignorance

The tendency of fear is the enemy of human life. The life of cowards and timids is worthless. Cowards die thousand times in a day. Thousands of lives are being doomed due to useless imaginary fear and becoming the victim of untimely death.

Just as the stormy blow of wind and heavy rain shatter the delicate flowers, plants, charming buds by shaking off, similarly the ill imaginations of the demon of fear shatter and leave the delicate and immatured heart in the undeveloped form and timid forever by its black-like death shadow.

Fear is the symbol of our ignorance and lack of understanding. As the feeling of insecurity increases in human mind, so do the creative positive capacities go on being crippled. His real fearless personality of lion with strong manhood goes on setting in the darkness. These cowards and timids don’t have their fear, superistitions, sorrow, timidity, hesitation, shame and lack of confidence limited to themselves but spread their timid mentality among the neighbours of the vicinity, friends even into their own children. Our female class is badly entangled since the ages, with the mentality of fear and timidity. The Indian women specially uneducated living in the villages and backward women remain striken with fear and lead their whole life in the prison of fear. Due to their timidity they have to lead the life of a helpless slave. Timidity and fear is the mental disorder of man’s decaying moral strength.

Now change your outlook and make yourself vigorous

Till now, you have passed your life in fear and timidity. He have been thinking over the unpleasant, unhealthy and worrying aspect of life. Such cowardice thoughts have ruined your personality.

Thought is the most powerful base of life. New energy is generated from this very seed. As your thoughts are rooted in your hidden mind so will grow up the vigour and qualities. Determined thought is a powerful magnet. He will attract the surrounding atmospheres similar to his own self. If we make firm and well rooted mentality of creative and positive thoughts, our outlook may be puissant and self-confidence will develop.

Just consider with thoughtful mind that if you go on fearing from others throughout your life and don’t recover yourself, don’t awaken your potential energy, where will you stand? Where will you get your importance? What will you be able to do in future?

You are required to root out your imaginary fears, well-rooted worries of your mind and evil thoughts from your heart forever and create the atmosphere of fearlessness and contentment in your surroundings. Be fearless yourself and suggest your co-living beings that they should also be fearless like you. Forget your past tragic references, your errors and the dark aspects of your life. Let not your mind be involved in the future worries. Let not the fearful thoughts make you perturbed. Don’t puzzle yourself with what others think of you? What they say and what opinion have they formed about you?

Why do you think that they don’t have high opinion about you, whether they criticize you or otherwise? You should move ahead with the consideration that all are in your favour and they talk in your favour, all want your good. You have a high position in their mind. They always discuss about your virtues.

You should think that all cannot think against your welfare and bitter to you, because you are not so undesirable. You are born to rise high and become great. You are progressing every day. You are embellishing the temple of your mind with altruistic thoughts and are immersed in lofty thoughts.

Keep it in your mind that he who depends on the thoughts, suggestions or indications of others is like the child who wants to remain in the lap even after being grown up. This selfish world makes him dance like the monkey whose nose-halter is in others hands. There has been the existence of the false critics and ridiculers in this world since the beginning of the world but the brave men of prowess (You are also one of them) never cared for them.

Be brave and live as diligent. Realize yourself look towards your bright future you are not petty, you are great. Due to the hidden vigour and prowess, you need not feel any want or weakness. You need not beg before anyone stretching your palms. You have endless power. There is no limit of your vitality. The divine means you are born with on this earth, are the infallible weapons of Lord Brahma. The power of these divine weapons and means is more than that of several ‘Indra’s thunderbolts’. You have the birthright of success and pleasures. Wake up and rise up, recognise your divine weapons fully. Engage in the act of spiritual reform and self-advancement and devote yourself to your duty intelligently. Then, why and how will the purpose not be success, which you want to fulfil with true mind and heart? You are the ‘Kalpbriksha’ (the wish fulfilling tree) which fulfills all the desires of man. You are the Philosopher’s stone that turns iron to gold. Really, you are the the success personified.

 

There is no lack of gallantry, courage and prowess even today

Slap the lion

The Portguese News agency, Lusitenia reported from Lisbon that a vigorous man imbedded his teeth into the nose of a lion in Angola with such courage that it had to run away abandoning the wounded person.

The occurence is reported that two brothers naming Lusio and Jokim Chanka went to the forest for hunting; where a lion sprang upon Lusio and having knocked him down on the earth gripped him under his claws. He fell into a great dangerous risk. The death was covering him with its black shadow every moment. The lion intended to kill him. His brother Jokim could not shoot the lion; because the gun was with the servant and he had fled away being frightened. To save his brother from the claws of the lion, Jokim fell out with the lion with force to knock him down; but when it went beyond his control like the violent beasts he imbedded his teeth in the nose of the lion so forcibly that its breath stopped. A portion of the neck was cut down also. The lion was perturbed. Just as the hold of the lion was a little loose, Lucio jumping stood up and he shot at the lion. Both of the brothers remained hospitalised for a month in the injured position in the Nampula hospital; but they were saved. Such lions of courage and prowess among mankind are the true jewels of humanity.

Killed the lion with the axe

In the village, Ekulgarh a bold and brave Harijan youth named Mehataba alone killed the lion with the axe. It so happened that the lion had taken away the goat from his house in the night. He got furiated on this and his strong arms were thrilled to take revenge. In the morning he set out from the house in search of the lion. Wandering about he remained searching for the lion for a number of hours. At last, on the side of a river in a ditch he searched out the lion. The duel was fought between the lion and Mehtab. The lion gripped Mehtab’s hands twice in his jaws; but ultimately Mehtab killed the lion with the blows of his axe.

Even the insufficient means in the hands of courageous persons show their worth. A hero gets victory so many times with his more long bamboo-stick but a coward cannot in spite of being equipped with cannon and dagger. None but a brave deserves the enjoyment of the earth. Here, there are numerous heros, one better than other and you are one of them.

By strangling the neck killed the Tiger

A youth named Bhagirath belonging to the village, Khogasara, district Bilaspur, strangled the neck of a seven feet long tiger and killed it. At a place, a snake and a tiger were struggling neck to neck, where many villagers gathered to watch it. What inspired the tiger and it stopped fighting with the snake abruptly and it fell upon the crowd. All the villagers ran away being frightened. Bhagirath faced bravo in the struggle, Bhagirath caught the neck of the tiger tightly and pressed it so tightly with the best possible force that it died. This is the inspiring story of the man of prowess. In fact, the world has been bowing down before the power. In the world none but the braves are adored. The majesties kiss those who have strength and capability in their arms.

The above mentioned examples are of those who are also the men of flesh and blood like us. They had also the same body like us; they had also the same legs and hands like us. The difference was only that they had the brave passion of prowess, courage and zeal, the inner moral strength, They had full self-confidences. That is why they could take the courageous step.

The villagers killed the Lion

The news report of Tehsil Faridpur of Bareilly has been published as follows—

The residents of village Charhia Tahsil Faridpur killed one eight and half feet long lion with Lathi and Danda (long bamboo stick). It is reported that a man named Dula Singh was grazing his camel in the neighbouring forest. A lion fell upon him in the meantime hearing the noise, the farmers working in the neighbouring fields reached there with lathi and spike and released Dula Singh from the clutch of the lion anyhow. One of the villagers brought a licenced gun from his house and he shot at the wounded lion which died immediately.

It has been the tradition of the holy soil of India giving birth to such heroes. We are braves. The castes make progress ahead on the basis of courage. It is only the courage that makes the counrties developed. The courageous move ahead and the circumstances also favour them, the companions also help them but those who lack of self-confidence, who have not realised their vigour, remain in a fix about their strength and remain thinking in fear that they are incompetent to do anything. Failure greets them who are devoid of self-confidence.

Different news of valour and prowess usually cover the newspapers today, which are the signs of growing prowess in the country. Peruse a few news events—

Reward to brave villagers of Banda

As it is said that three villagers of Banda, Devasaran, Chunni Lal and Narbada had compelled an armed gang of robbers to run away from the village Khohi by hitting them with bricks and stones and had made their plan of robbery futile. The S.P. of Banda namely Shri A.M. Shah had rewarded them for their courage and bravery. The villagers had faced the robbers very boldly and had wounded one of the robbers badly who had been carried away by his companions.

This is the psychological truth that energy of a man lies inside the man and not so much externally Vitality appears outwardly, but basically it is hidden inside. He who looks fat, well built, strong and heavy physically cannot face the storm and wind and falls down being rooted out like the hollow tree if he is weak by mind, courage and prowess and if the circumstances don’t favour he will never be in position to rise.

But the man who is mentaly strong in his thoughts and feelings who has the treasure of confidence and courage, will never feel any problem in facing the adverse situations. The mental courage, prowess and valour is strong like the splendour of the sun which gives the acquaintance of its presence even tearing off the clouds. No other support or means of the world can equal to the courage ensuing from self-confidence of the world.

We need the capital of courage at every step in our daily life. Even today there are many such courageous men who are setting the examples of valour and prowess.

The old man’s jump with indomitable courage

According to the news received from Varahava (Santhal Paragana), in the recent past, a thief was caught in the 131 U.P. Sealdah-Gaya passanger train by the indomitable courage of an old man.

As it is said that as soon as the train arrived near the local station, a band of thieves threw out the box of the 55 years old man, and they themselves also jumped down from the compartment. The passanger also jumped down after the thieves. Then, the thieves began to assault him, but hearing his cry the police constables rounding on duty, rushed there and arrested the thieves.

This old man had the moral strength. The support of the Lord always follows the noble and right men.

The villagers knocked down the two robbers

One day, in the village Amba under Chhurpur police station of the district Prayag, two robbers were killed in the encounter between a few villagers and the gang of robbers. Three to four villagers are also reported to be injured with the bullets in the firing. In the report it has been published that a dozen of robbers well equipped with arms and violent weapons launched a raid in a house of the village. Hearing the loud roar and cry, the villagers gathered there with lathis and spears. The robbers started firing on them but the villagers were not afraid but they were successful in killing the two robbers. The rest dacoits ran away.

On the support of courage people protect their life and property, morality and family. By this courage, protection is possible everywhere. A courageous man takes its advantage every moment. It is not known where and how there may be the need of courageous performance. So, it is needed to remain strong in all the circumstances. The cowards suffering from inferiority complex are always suspicious. They remain in a fix whether they are capable to protect themselves or not.

Wonderful courage of the youth

There is a news of Bhardah (Ghazipur) that in the neighbouring village, Mirzapur, when a youth had bent down to detach the bullock from the peg, a very big poisonous snake fell down from the thatch of the hut on his back and it tightened the neck of the youth with its tail. This youth was not the least frightened. He showed an uncommon courage. In the middle of his both legs approaching his hands he caught the hood of the snake and twisted his fist tightly. On one side the snake was tightening the youth’s neck with a great force and on the other hand the youth was going on tightenning his fist. In the meantime the family members and the neigbourers got the youth’s neck freed from the hold of the snake’s tail and the youth threw away the snake with a jerk. The back bone of the snake broke away and the people killed it.

When the men of courage proceed onward the circumstances also support them and so many courageous helpers come forward in support. Courage breeds courage. One’s boldness encourages the otherone’s boldness. But those who lack self-confidence, who have never realized their own immense capacity, live in the darkness of suspicion and fearing and shivering remain thinking that they are at all incapable to do anything. They never start any new big work. Such fearing cowards are always unsuccessful in life. They who suffer from inferiority complex get only failures in their lives. ‘None but the heros of mind taste and enjoy the fruit of wealth, health, position, power, rule, weapons co-operation etc.

You, too, become the man of prowess

कुर्वन्नेवेह कर्माणि जिजीविषेच्छतॸ समा:।

एवं त्वयि नान्यथेतोऽस्ति न कर्म लिप्यते नरे॥

(Yajurved 40/2)

‘The mankind should desire to live one hundred years in the world only doing his duty. O the human being! This is the only way for you, no other way is superior to it. By remaining doing the duty, no mental modification arises in human mind. So, performing the objective of life in this world, desire for a long life. To pass the manliness life is the supreme goal of mankind.’

इच्छन्ति देवा: सुन्वन्तं, न स्वप्नाय स्पृहयन्ति।

यन्ति प्रमादमतन्द्रा:॥

(Rik. 8/2/18)

‘All the gods like those who perform the Yagya, none likes the lazy and inactive men. They are the vigorous men free from laziness; who subdue those doing vices; because the valorous men are supported by the gods; the careless and lazy are helped by none.’ So, it is the duty of everyone to use his vigour in performing the duties of human life and move ahead on the path of the rise of prosperity.

The command of prowess

पिबतं च तृष्णुतं च गच्छतं प्रजां च धत्तं द्रविणं च धत्तम्।

(Rik. 8/35/10)

‘O the mankind! Drink the nectar by your prowess and be gratified and go on moving onward on the path of prosperity. Thus, go on collecting wealth for the sustenance and nourishment of the public.’

जयतं च प्रस्तुतं च प्र चावतं प्रजां च धत्तं द्रविणं च धत्तम्॥

(Rik. 8/35/11)

‘O the human being! May you be always victorious in the world and protect the praiseworthy society of noble deeds and thus, go on increasing the subjects and property!’

हतं च शत्रून् यततं च मित्रिण:।

प्रजां च धत्तं द्रविणं च धत्तम्॥

(Rik. 8/35/12)

‘O the man! Destroy the enemies and provide help to the friends! In this way you increase the wealth and subjects!’

ब्रह्म जिन्वतमुत जिन्वतं धियो हतं रक्षांसि।

सेधतममीवा:॥

(Rik. 8/35/16)

‘O the man! Doing the duty of your life, attain the super knowledge and suppressing the evil deeds wisely do the auspicious deeds and remain healthy free from disease!’

क्षत्रं जिन्वतमुत जिन्वतं नृृन् हतं रक्षांसि।

सेधतममीवा:॥

(Rik. 8/35/17)

‘O the man! Being valorous may you attain the fearlessness of Kshatriya and keeping the association of noble persons near yourself destroy the wickeds! Thus, may you live always healthy and cheerful!’’

धेनूर्जिन्वतमुत जिन्वतं विशो हतं रक्षांसि।

सेधतममीवा:॥

(Rik. 8/35/18)

‘O the human being! Growing the number of cows and looking after them, add to your animal property and sustain the subjects annihilating the demons protect the human being. This is your duty.’

आशीर्ण ऊर्जमुत सौप्रजास्त्वं दक्षं धत्तं द्रविणं सचेतसौ।

जयं क्षेत्राणि सह सायमिन्द्र, कृण्वाना अन्यान धरान्त्सपत्नान्॥

(Atharva. 2/29/3)

‘O the Lord! Bless us always with benevolence and welfare! O the even-minded men! May you be the gainer of grain, vitality, riches and strength including the noble offsprings and donate always in charity! O the Lord! Bless us with such energy and strength that may we be the victorious by our own prowess and may we be always capable in annihilating the enemies!’ Thus, we should guard our nation also.

उद्‍बुध्यध्वं समनस: सखाय:, समग्निमिन्ध्वं बहव: सनीळा:।

दधिक्रामघ्निमुषसं च देवीमिन्द्रावतोऽवसे नि ह्वये व:॥

(Rik. 10/101/1)

O the people of similar thought and similar knowledge! Rise, wake up and know your duty. All of you, belonging to one family in unison with love enlighten the God, the illumined and the knowledge with superior method. O the Lord! With the power of fortitude for the progress, development and advancement, bless us with divine power! We humbly invoke you for the protection of the nation and society.’

 

You are hero, so don’t be afraid of the enemies

The more you have fear, the more you are threatened, frightened, censured and slandered. The world always valuates your strength and prowess. If it is found that you are caving in, then, the people serve their self-interest by curbing, coercing and frightening you more and more.

If you under-estimate yourself, you will grow weaker, devoid of influence, more impotent and more afraid. Your vigour, prowess, willfulness and resolve will be deteriorating day by day. The imaginary fear will push you down into the hell of downfall. If you step back being afraid of your enemies, you will inspire and strengthen them to be more active against you. Your own errors and short comings will be bent upon in standing against you.

The enemy-fear is a false thinking of an imaginary mind. Being overpowered by it merely, we form the false imagination of our inferiority complex and meekness in the delusion of mind we overestimate our hostile. This false fear of mind has converted most of hearts into the funeral ground.

In reality you are valorous

Believe in my words, you are a valorous one. The capability of the protection of the nation runs through your veins.

I know several such men kind who have fallen down into the miserable condition having been entangled into the clutches of their fancied enemies and have reached this miserable condition. Their mind is filled with the imaginary fear. Such men always dream of the coming miseries and various devastating adversities. So throughout their life being under the spell of the imaginary fearful tendency they have shattered their courageous efforts and ambitions.

This fear is our terrible enemy to arouse the feeling of weakness in our life. This fear is the sole creator of disbelief, laziness, impatience, boldlessness, dissatisfaction, weakness and such type of different weaknesses of mind. After casting off the imagination from our mind, the noble qualities of man begin to develop.

There are a number of persons who are desirous to know other’s opinion about themselves. He always thinks about the opinion of some man or what does the newspaper speak of him? What is the attitude and opinion of anyone about my caste, race, country and religion? What is the reaction of the public about me? When I cross through the market what they talk about me?

When a man is involved in such types of logical or illogical arguements, it should be concluded that the man has been caught into the net of imaginary fear. In his secret mind, any weak mentality of his childhood is hidden anywhere and he is glancing the shadow of their pictures here and there.

As to see the faults in others is considered to be the mental blemish, similarly to suffer from inferiority complex and find fault and weaknesses in our ownself again and again is also to make the man weak and inferior.

It is mentioned in the Bible at a place that the object which a man has in abundance that very object will be given more to him. That what is lacking that lesser object or virtue will also be snatched from him.

In other words it means that if your weakness is more dominant then the weakness, poverty, inferiority, sorrow, wretchedness, shortcoming, defeat will be available to you in abundence. If you think of your weaknesses, the same poisonous and foul atmosphere will continue to be created in your hidden mind. Even in your surrounding atmosphere, the weakness will remain spreading. You will be afraid of even the triffling matters. You will go on fearing of the nightmares the whole night.

Contrary to it, if you are overwhelmed with vigour, courage, gallantry enthusiasm, exhilaration and auspicious thoughts, the sentiment of courage and gallantry will be originated in your mind.

Your fears are imaginary. Your worries are your self-creation. In your full natural form, you are perfectly fearless, fear from worldly sorrows, miseries and all sorts of worries. Your real form is the form of hero. Any kind of cowardice thought should not come to your temple of mind.

Your inner-sense is such a mirror where you can see your fearless form. By rubbing that mirror with the sand of courage and self-confidence make it dignified.

If you may be capable to be free from fear in your life, you can be able to open the new chapter of your life. Only then, you can attain the life of prowess and victory.

The irrefutable principle of science is that two contradictory thoughts cannot be possible at a single place. When you fill your secret mind with the courageous thoughts in abundance, there will be no question of failure or defeat then at all.

Pass your time fearlessly. Don’t allow fear to dominate you. You are a great warrior. You are born of valour. You are the brave son of the great vigorous father. You are a brave soldier. You are the chief of the army. You have been selected the general chief of the army for the total victory in the struggle of life. There is your responsibility of the protection of your house, family, Mohalla, Province and the whole country. You are confident of your vigour. Accept it with full confidence and say elatedly—

संशितं म इदं ब्रह्म संशितं वीर्यबलम््।

संशितं क्षत्रमजरमस्तु जिष्णुर्ये येषामस्मि पुरोहित:॥

(Atharvaved. 3/19/1)

Mean to say—‘I am a hero. My spirit is strong. I have undaunted faith in the God, which has made me fearless from death. I can go to the battlefield fearlessly. My spiritual knowledge is also deep. I am well versed with the war policy. I have the capability to take decision, knowing the strength of own side and the rival side. My moral strength and the physical strength both are strong. I am fully victorious and valorous. In the same way, May the soldiers whom I lead and I am their chief let their forgiving tendency! Be intense may it be undecaying! May their power of forgiveness be unstinting!’

प्रेता जयता नर: उप्रा व सम्तु बाहव:।

तीक्ष्णेषवोऽबलधन्वनो हतोग्रायुधा अबलान् उग्रबाहव:॥

(Atharvaved. 3/19/7)

‘March ahead, be victorious, O the braves! May your arms be mighty! O the heros of sharp weapons, violent weapons, furious arms! Annihilate the enemies, prove their arms blunt, make them powerless.’

 

The neat and clean garments have their spiritual impact

As we feel a type of freshness after a bath by the openning of the hair-roots of our body and the rubbing of the body, similarily the man’s spirit gets pleasure after putting on new and neat and clean garments.

The character of our soul is cleanliness. This is free from all kinds of vices, defilements, filthy objects. Dirt cannot stay there in it. There cannot be even the drizzle of the mud of sin. If any object makes effort to make it muddy, there arises the cry of self-reproach, repentence and remorse. When any evil thought, unholy wicked fancy, despicable sensuousness and the mean mentality inferior to our morality, disturbs our truth, love, duty and devotion entering the sphere of our mind, all of us feel an internal percussion in our soul. What is the reason behind it?

Our spirit can never support us to do any such immoral deed which is associated with any kind of physical, oral, mental dirt. The men of dirty presumptions or nasty action resort to vile actions having ignored the inner voice; but internally they remain afflicted by a mental agony. You may suppress this inner voice for a certain period but its pious action goes on continuously.

The duty of inner voice is—To perform the act of cleanliness in our innerself; To initiate the mankind on the path of truth with the discernment between right and wrong removing all the dirty thoughts, counsels or fancies whatsoever come to our mind. The man who hears the innervoice is always guided to the right path by the inner voice. The sphere of his mind is always clean. Wherever any dirty thought is created in our mind like a rebel, the very moment the auspicious instincts of our mind turn it out by struggling with them.

Our outer atmosphere should be perfectly neat and clean

Since, cleanliness is the innate quality of our soul, so outer cleanliness also gives us full satisfaction and pleasure. The clean atmosphere has its impact on our health, pleasure, internal joy.

The garments of man play a very important role in the creation of neat and clean atmosphere. The garments are in the close contact of our body. It affects our internal instincts in its creation. The internal tendencies are created by the influence of our garments. If our garments are clean, naturally, the series of pure thoughts start. The flow of thought itself goes towards the purity and virtuousness. Our thoughts are unable to rise up so high due to dirtiness. Their moral truth is hurt unexpected. Because of living continuously in the contact of dirty garments our high spirits become crippled slowly and slowly.

It was the belief of Mahatma Gandhi that only in the clean Khadi garments he used to be inspired by the pure thoughts of truth, justice, non-violence and the world-brotherhood. Every non-violent truthful freedom fighter should wear khadi garments. There is a close contact between the Khadi garments and the purity of thoughts.

Cleanliness in the atmosphere and the cleanliness of the garments generate the clean mind. The men who is habitual of cleanliness is always higher in the standard of his thoughts than those in dirty garments.

‘Cleanliness is next Godliness’—this proverb has a great message. Cleanliness makes our approach near divinity. The special quality of the gods is their cleanliness. By living neat and clean you make your reach near divinity.

What a matter of sorrow it is that whereas the other castes and races are always active for cleanliness and sow the seed of cleanliness among their children, here in our country a very little attention is being paid towards it. Cleanliness is a habit. If once it becomes our habit, it will continue lifelong and man will not forget it the whole life. It should be kept in mind that there is a big difference between cleanliness and fashion. Fashion is to show others and cleanliness is to root out dirtiness. Fashion in itself is only the indication of dirty mind.

 

Feel self-esteemed of adopting Hindu dress and Hindi language

An English writer Tomas Fuler has written—with that simplicity of dress is the sign of gentility. Our spiritual feelings remain alive. The dress of a man reveals his religion, caste, country and culture everything for the man of clean and sober dress. Doors of all the high societies remain open, while the valuable glittering fashionable dresses indicate the shallowness of the personality and we become the victim of hatred in the others eyes due to pomp and show and spuriousness. For the improvement of virtues and character your garments are also required to be like that of the civilized persons.

The Hindu Get up is the only comfortable and simple

Every caste and every country man boasts of the make up of his caste or country superior but the entire world knows this fact and accepts the reality that Indian get up is attractive. The Dhoti Kurta and the Jaket the get up of Indian Hindu males and the Saree in practice among the Hindu women is considered to be the best and comfortable in the whole world. The countries of the world wherever our late Prime-minister, Shri Lal Bahadur Shastri visited in Dhoti and Kurta his dress had been considered the best and highly appreciated. In the same way Pandit Vijaya Lakshmi’s and Smt. Indira Gandhi’s Indian Sarees have been given the foremost place in cleanliness, attraction and modesty.

The garments are closely related to our culture and religion. To distinguish every culture and religion is the separate make up also. The get up of a particular type creates a particular type of mentality and feeling in the mind. Even uneducated illiterate man are seen in the Western style in coat pant and tie and in hat boot and socks blindly following the western style. By smattering of English they complete their hypocrisy. The shallow mentality of vanity, obstinacy, false dignity, luxury and bragging begin to be created in the mind just while putting on the English dress. The prosperity, lewdness of sensuous enjoyment, luxury, glamorous show is attached to the Muslim dresses. With the dress get up and language, the culture, history and religion are attached. The Western and Muslim culture and religion are based on the lewdness of sexual passion and on the voluptuousness of eat, drink and be merry. They give more importance to the lewdness and meaningless worldly objects. At the same time there is the excess of repulsive and disgusting vulgarity, nakedness and lewdness all around there. In the Western society everywhere there is the dominance of voluptuous brutal mentality. These countries give priorty only to the artificial outer beauty (should it be called the real beauty?), pomp and show and false show. Daily the new fashions are introduced there. Among these castes the unsatisfied desires of sexual passion and different enjoyments and sensuous life are the hindrance in the rise of their thoughts and talent above the materialistic level. They have forgotten the value of high ideals of life in remaining absorbed in taking the beastly taste of meat, wine, mean objects and lower ideals. Whatever the dresses and get up, pomp and show, the fondness of fashion, false boasting, outer decoration, sensuousness and enjoyments of Western and Muslim cultures are; that is the brutish pleasure of man’s five sense organs.

Put on the muslims or Western dresses for a single day, you will feel the same thoughts like them in your mind. You are in an army uniform, your mind is filled with the sentiments of violence, brutals, terror wickedness and to oppress on others and ostentation. In the muslim dress, the sentiments of sensuousness, passion and selfishness, demonstration and shallowness are created in the mind.

Today the Indian youths who are running after fashion, wearing the half naked and tight dresses like the film actors acting in the vulgar films, wander about on the roads at the city, loafing about with transistor in their hands and remain gathered in group on the cigarette and betel shops, before the hotels and cinema halls, only make the demonstration of fashion. In such a blind copy what is beauty? Such a modernism is merely an illusion.

The Indian dresses, neat and clean while Dhoti, loose and long Kurta, jacket, sandle etc., are proper and comfortable, cheap and according to the economic status and season. They create the atmosphere of co-ordialily and compassion. There is more cleanliness, attraction and comforts in these dresses; man is free from meaningless show also. Fraternity, simplicity, humbleness, modesty and gentility have been the distinctive characteristics of our culture and religion. By the use of this dress our spiritual feelings remain alive. We consider the excess make up and showy robes ostentatious. This pomp and show has been considered here baseful. By using the minimum possible robes to establish identification with nature to have our body away from decoration and make up, fashion, pomp and show, simple living and high thinking has been the view of our life and it should continue in future also.

In the Western countries where the sentiment to win the nature prevails, the Indian culture and Hindu religion has made a humble effort to establish identification with nature. In the Hindu religion the mountains like the Himalaya, the Kailash, the rivers like the Ganga, the Yamuna and the Godawari, forests, trees and gardens have been considered sacred. They have been considered the dwelling places of the Lord, Not only the saints and hermits of India but also the public of India have been enjoying the pleasure in the laps of Nature. The Indian Hindus consider the nature as their mother instead of treating the nature as maidservant and they give due regard to the nature. They have always realised and felt oneness with the forests, creepers, mountains, rivers, animals, birds and trees of Nature. Our pilgrimages and temples have been established near the rivers and mountains. The forests, gardens and villages have been the good symbols of our culture.

So, due to the village-dresses and affinity with nature, the simplicity, cleanliness, health, modesty and liberality are found in our dresses also. The mentality of looking always embelished is considered to be the sign of shallowness. The worthless artificiality, and decorating objects of different colours have been always the objects of detachment for us here. According to the Indian culture this has been the concept that as much artificiality and show is adopted in life and as much unnaturality is there in our dresses, so much distance will continue to be created from higher life.

Indian dresses don’t mean poverty or helplessness rather it means to use the suitable and necessary objects sacredly without any show. This simplicity, cleanliness, pridelessness should be associated with our behaviour and conduct. The robes should not be very costly and injurious to health like Nylon, Terelyn and it should not be of very thin threads of silk. It is not needed at all. We have been the lover of thick white ‘Khaddar’; but it should be clean. The dresses of glamorous show, different colours and unnatural fashionable, are the symbol of worthless hollowness. The quantity of the dresses should be minimum for wearing but we should have the full consideration of its cleanliness. This is the sanctity of Indian thoughts that instead of being loaded with ornaments better to get some new dresses made and in maintaining cleanliness to spend some money is more useful. The simplicity of mind, thought, dress and the cleanliness of the surrounding atmosphere and soberity have the wonderful capacity to attract towards the high spiritual life.

The Hindu religion and culture is attached with Hindi literature and Hindi language

The slavery of language is the worst; because with the language the culture and religion of that country is also to be adopted secretly. We begin to accept the religion, traditions, the braves and culture of that country also which national language we love, adopt or fully appreciate. Behind the curtain of the language the religion and culture are also preached. Behind every word, idiom and proverb of the language, the religion, culture and sacrament are hidden and they also speak. The religion comes out in day-to-day behaviour in the garb of language. The formation of numerous words is made through the source of religion. The religion and language are co-related.

The diplomacy of Britishers; the slavery of Englishmen

When the Englishmen had won India, they were not satisfied merely with the victory over trade and business and political victory. The political slavery is the outer and external administrative slavery. The rule is administered on the base of administrative punishment, terror and fear. They planned to enslave Hindustan (the Hindus country) with the view of mental slavery also.

How was this mental slavery created?

When any brave race wins over the weak race, she tries to make her slave in all respects. The winner race thursts upon her the load of her language and literature. They have to study the language and literature of the winner race forcibly. Those who learn that language are rewarded and the appreciation certificates are distributed to them. The defeated race learns the appreciation and praise of the heros of the winner race directly or indirectly again and again; sees their pictures, sings their songs and lives in the atmosphere of their mentality. So, silently, the defeated race goes on accepting also the religion of the winner race and adopts her traditional customs and ideals also.

The bad result of the physical weakness and defeat is that they begin to consider the winner race superior to them in all respects. It develops the feeling of mental and cultural slavery in the loser caste. By reading the appreciation and praise of the other caste in their language and literature again and again, the people of weaker caste starts suffering from the inferiority complex and it seems to them that the rulers are superior to them in all respects and they are inferior and their everything is useless. This is the slavery of language.

Thus, by the study of foreign language for a long time the defeated men begin to consider the foreigners superior and consider their literature, culture, ideals, customs and traditions and their thoughts superior most. They regard their old fables and stories and their racial ideals the best one. This is the rule of the psychology that we begin to think it true (even if it may be wrong and baseless) whatever is mentioned before us again and again. Thus, by the study of a foreign language and literature for a long time, any caste or race forgets her own racial dignity and the golden glory of her cultural heritage. Thus, the mental slavery goes on increasing.

Our mental slavery in India has been continuing since long through the foreign language and literature. Behind the curtain of the language religion is also preached. It is a matter of great shock that none has yet paid attention to this minute psychological fact of preaching the other religion secretly behind the curtain of language.

The slavery of Urdu and Islam

The mental slavery in India started from Urdu and Islam religion. When the Muslims won India because of the rift among the Hindus, they had also preached Islam in this Hindu country through the Urdu language. There was the spread of Urdu and Persian reign. These languages were declared the national languages. The Hindu public were pressurised to read Urdu by terror and violence. Those who did not study Urdu, were not encouraged in the Govt jobs as well as in the state. On the other side, those Hindus who earned the knowledge of Urdu and Farasi due to fear or greed, were given superior jobs from the Gvernment. side as encouragement, sufficient rewards, honour and social status were awarded to them.

Behind the curtain of Urdu and Farasi the Islam was spread over. Secretly, many of Hindus were made muslim by converting their religion. The ideals of muslims and Islamic culture were advertised excessively. The big volums of Urdu were written and made popular. This was all the preaching of muslim life-style, rules of Islam, ideals of appearance and dresses, principles and doctorines abruptly the Islam took a turn.

The slavery of Englishmen and English language

The time changed. This time another foreign race suppressed us. There came an other big storm in the language, culture, dresses and ideals again.

Just when the age of Urdu, Farasi and Islam religious ended, the new age of English language and literature started. The Christian priests started the preaching of Christianity through the English language and literature. Lord Mackaly took the greatest interest in the conversing of English. First, by teaching English the clerks were prepared, they were given the good jobs and by awarding rewards and social status, the English was given the social sanctity and thus, a majority became well educated in English, it was made the state language then.

By getting the support of the Government, the reign of English was established in India. We began to imitate Englishmen, we began to put on English dress and began to feel proud of speaking in English.

In the primary classes, English was started to be taught from class three and in English medium schools English was started to be taught to the children. In the shadow of English, Hindu children were taught and preached the christianity; English culture, their gods, their way of living, their ideals and life system secretly. Many of Hindus, specially the men of untouchable class adopted Christianity. A number of missionary schools were started for the children. There was the priority to the teachings of Christianity more than imparting them education. The attractive publication of the ‘Bible’ were distributed among the children free of cost and in many institutions the ‘Bible’ was taught in the lower and higher classes to initiate them with the primary sacraments of Christian religion. By and by the Indians began to consider English the most superior language of the world. Thus, the slavery of English language covered the whole India due to some extent in the greed of the Government. services, to some extent due to fashion and the mentality of imitation. The natural attraction is created towards the foreign goods howsoever of inferior quality they may be. The attraction increased towards Englishmen. The English way of living, the English fashions and get up and English speaking had a great impact on the uneducated public of India and it went on continuing.

Contrary to it due to the spell of English, the minds of Indians began to suffer from the inferiority complex towards their literature, Hindu culture, Vedic religion, Indian dresses and culture.

To conclude, with the language, literature, dress of any country, the religion, culture and racial ideals of that country are closely connected. These sacraments are very easily rooted in the minds of the tender-hearted children. When our children study English language and literature, the feelings of the superiority of English men influence their minds. We became fan of Christian religion, their gods and goddess, materialism, perversity, their customs and traditions and voluptuousness and lust of sexuality. In English we read heroic tales of Christian braves. By reading it again and again, we become the inhabitant of their mental atmosphere. Their ideals and thoughts look us better and superior. Their religion and culture seem to us superior to Hindu religion and Indian culture. We read about the wars which they had won. Thus, the sentiments of the foreigners prowess, superiority and heroic feelings leave their strong impression on our hidden mind and thus, a type of mental slavery overpowers us. This mental slavery is prevailing today in this Hindu country. This slough must be given up without any delay.

It is only Hindi and Sanskrit that can protect our religion

With Hindi and Sanskrit languages, the Hindu religion and Indian culture and the old ideal sacraments and purifications are related. Sanskrit represents our glorious and praiseworthy traditions. Sanskrit is full of the best literature, spiritual knowledge and the property of original thoughts. Sanskrit is the source of all the languages of the world. The highness of spiritualism, philosophy and psychology lies in abundance therein our religious books which are in Sanskrit language. In philosophy no country of the whole world has yet been able to touch the height of India. The admirable and permanent property of spiritual knowledge what the Hindus possess; the vigorous fables of our braves, and the highest sacraments of Hindu caste are collected and safe in Hindi and Sanskrit.

For the protection of Hindu religion, Hindu culture, Indian ethics and thoughts, spiritualism etc., the advertisements and preaching of Hindi and Sanskrit at broad level is a great necessity for this country of Hindus.

To study Sanskrit and Hindi is the impartible part of our religion. Who is a Hindu who does not know these languages? Hindi can unite the whole nation by creating the emotional unity in the country. This is the moral duty of the scholars of Hindi and Sanskrit that they should work for the development and preaching of the both languages and make effort so that the property of the old thoughts the both languages are under the reach of common public. The doubts of the public mind should be dispelled that there is lack of other literature useful to mankind in Sanskrit literature except only the Vedas, Shastras and grammer. There is the invaluable property of literary and philosophical thoughts in the Sanskrit Literature. The language that remains as much as popular to the common people so much developed and long lived it becomes. Contrary to it, if it is unpopular from the common public, it becomes the object of long past untimely. By chance, Sanskrit has met some unfortunate fate. It is a matter of great sorrow that in spite of being the richest literature of the world, it has been considered the dead literature of the past, but now, the interest towards the study of Sanskrit has started growing among the people for sometimes. This is a good symptom, but there is the need of the support and co-operation of Hindi for the protection of this growing interest and development. The entire Sanskrit literature should be spread in every corner of the country through the medium of Hindi. They, who know Hindi and Sanskrit and the learned men, should do much hard labour for the protection and encouragement of this growing interest and development, only then this interest can be lasting and useful.

The ancient glory of India, Hindu religion and Indian culture have faced a great loss by the compulsory teaching and learning of English in the bitter days of the slavery of British rule. Having forgotten the praiseworthy traditions of Hindus, we have began to copy the Western dress, language and materialistic views. For the cultural awakenning and to create the emotional unity, it is a great need of the time to adopt Hindi by the majority of the people.

Let us not follow the Western way of life and their ideology blindly

We should do the best possible to regain the ancient glory of our country, religion, language and culture. Let us live in the simplicity of our country. No country becomes great by the blind following of others. We should develop our own characteristics. By own mother language, culture and dress only the development of the country is possible. George Bernard Shaw has truly said—‘Such a man who has no control on his own language, can never be expert in other language!

Hindi language is in the practice of forty-three percent people of India. This is the main language of Uttar Pradesh, Rajasthan, Bihar and Madhya Pradesh. The Hindu religion, Indian culture and the ages old purest sacraments are hidden behind it. Because of the origin of this language from Sanskrit, it is close to Bengali and Marathi.

So, every Hindu should feel self-esteemed of adopting Hindi language and Hindu dress. By the propagation of these elements, the Hindu religion can spread extensively and the emotional unity can be established. The spread of Hindi means the spread of Hinduism. All the ideal high sanctities of Hindu religion, the traditional ideals, ambitions, the leading thoughts, the ancient glory and the future progress is vested in making this language popular more and more. Considering his moral duty every Hindu should study the religious literatures published in Hindi, establish the library of religious books in the family and donate in charity the Hindi religious literature having purchased it.

 

In the time of crisis, hope should not be given up

Necessity of the inner strength not of the external one

The writer named Mark Ruderford has mentioned an accident in his autobiography. It was his childhood. Once, Mark Ruderford was standing on a sea beach. Afar a ship was berthed having cast an anchor. The child Ruderford wished to take a round of the ship by swimming and come back. He was very expert in swimming and he had the practice of taking out the stone from the bottom by taking the dip of ten feet down the depth. He was a young boy. The ship was berthed at the distance of two hundred yards from the beach.

He swam and reached the ship easily but as soon as he began to return, it may be his ill luck or ill of mind, the foolish, hopeless and coward thought came to his mind that his decision of ‘return’ was beyond his power and he would die before reaching the sea-shore. He does not have so much strength in him that he will be able to reach there safely again wherefrom he had come. In his odd imagination he presumed that he would die. He thought himself sunk before drowning. He began to count the last days of his death. He lost his strength.

But his mind changed again. From the horizon of darkness the dim rays of hope rose.

Now, he thought ‘Death is sure the danger is terrible, the shore looks dim, why not to struggle once more before drowning?’ He also said to himself—‘Till today, it is clear in my mind that this will be last struggle for me before my watery-grave—‘A heroic effort’—and I strengthened my broken hope and with a new zeal, I made effort again with full capacity. I am unable to describe what way I chose in my effort (it is not known, how the God had provided me that courage). I used my will power with my full capacity to win over fear.

In a single moment the fear came to an end and my mind was fully confident that I could save my life. The hidden power of the God is in my support. I know to swim. If I have come here by swimming, then, I can return also. Patience overtook my mind. I started using my hands comfortably and in a very short time crossing the sea I reached the shore. From the innerself the divine force saved me.

To mention here this fearful event is important because it proves that the man losing the patience, should never think that whatever he did that was final and to the best of his capacity and he could do no more. This is also worth noting that I faced this terrible situation by abruptly created self-confidence in the mind and made the best effort. It had made my victory ten times easier.

In reality, the God is present in our innerself to provide us the strength of courage at the moment of crisis. From the inner side He supports us to get salvation.

We get the inner support of the Lord

Let us take the support of patience and courage at the time of hardships, think of the prowess and make the best possible efforts to fight the difficulties and beat them; have confidence of our divine powers and we can overcome the hardships without any loss.

The hair of the body may be tiny but actually it is well deep rooted. In the same way, man’s roots of courage are deeply rooted in his confidence. This vigour and prowess is present inside us.

The man who looks physically strong from the outside but inwardly he is weak, will fall down being rooted out like a hollow tree before any storm and if the circumstances did not favour, he will never rise up. But the man who is emotionally stong; and has the capital of courage with him; will never feel any problem in struggling against the reverse circumstances.

The inner force (spiritual power) is like the pungent splendour of the sun, which makes to realize its existence even tearing the dense clouds. No help, facility or support of the world can equal the support of self-confidence.

They who expect sympathy from others by showing their meekness and weakness are in delusion.

Difficulties are a must for the evolution of life

The English learned man named Carlyle has written the matter of great experience of which each and every word is the source of new inspiration—

The difficulties don’t deserve hostility but fraternity. They should be considered necessary for the school of life. By clashing with the difficulties man becomes strong. While teaching the skill of wrestling in the wrestling arena, the master makes his pupil fall down by knocking down him again and again. He is hurt, he is sprained, he gets jolts, he is soaked with dust and sweat, he feels terribly tired but the same labour makes a man strong. He becomes energetic. The each and every part of his body becomes strong.

In the same way, if the difficulties don’t occur in our life, if we don’t face the hardships of life, if we don’t clash with miseries, the life will become utterly inactive and empty of zeal. So, to build up the life the difficulties should be greeted for the progress of life considering them the necessary means. Let us be ready to accept their challenge and remain removing even one misery by suffering one hundred pains. This is called prowess, humanity and this is the only way of progress and success.

‘असमं क्षत्रभसमा मनीषा।’

(Rigved 1/54/8)

Mean to say—‘Hold unparalleled prowess and immense wisdom. Where there is indomitable courage and farsightedness, there is everything.

 

Invaluable Treasures of Experience

Righteousness is the friend and guide of our daily life; this is the life style of daily and every moment behaviour in practice. In the life of many great men the morality has saved them from the mud of sin. Some examples are given here—

God is the seer of everything

A justice named Changsen lived there in Mongolia. He was highly religious-minded. He used to practise righteousness in his day-to-day behaviour. Due to this reason he had to pass his life sometimes in scarcity.

It so happened one day—

One day, his certain rich friend came to him. After the usual talks of formality, he took out a packet of golden coins and presenting it to him with due regard he said—

‘Nobody will be able to know the secret of this money except you and me. Please, accept this packet and let my work be done. Well! Who witnesses it? None will discuss about this money and your dignified reputation will also not be hurt. Be carefree from this secret matter. This fact will not be leaked out by me at all.’

The greed of money deviates even the men of great reputation from the path of morality. Who sacrifices the offered money and specially, when it has been offered by any reliable man?

That gentleman was confident that the bribe would be accepted and his immoral work would be done silently.

But the morality of the justice raised its voice. He was in favour of always to practise the morality in day- to-day behaviour. His inner soul gave him the moral support and he said—

‘Friend! Don’t say that none is the witness of this immoral money. Morality is a necessary part of human nature. By the secret moral wisdom of man gets the inner gratification and mental peace. We should criticise ourselves also with the same bitter point of view as we criticise others. There are no eyes of flesh to witness this immoral money undoubtedly, but the house and the earth are the witness. Hundreds of eyes of the sky are the witness of our secret deeds and the Lord of all having numberless eyes that Supreme Almighty is the witness of all our outer and internal deeds of every moment. I will not accept this immoral money at all. I will give the decision in your case according to my moral prudence.’

The judge did not accept the immoral money. The morality was winner.

I will not defy the moral prudence

This is an event of 1915—

Lokmanya Tilak thought to go abroad. There were already the obstacles regarding money and transportation but another unexpected problem came before him.

It was so as the then orthodox tradition against the sea-voyage stood as a hurdle on his way. Those days, the sea voyage was considered against religion. They who went on the journey abroad with strong will used to be outcasted. Thus, none could think of the abroad-journey.
