If the prowess is not awakened, you will get nothing. In true sense he is man who bears manliness, the second name lustrous element, in his character, he is called man, in fact without prowess he is a jackal or mouse in the shape of man.

Search out your hidden original power. Contemplate over the works what you can do better than others in the better artistic way. What are the fields where you are superior and better than others? What are your characteristics? To depend on others and remain sitting idle is good for nothing. God helps those who help themselves. You will be entitled of God’s support only when you work with your own hands. Only the self—supporting man can make progress. Manliness is a must in your life to be called a man. It has been said—

रुहो रुरोह रोहित:।

(Atharvaved 13/3/26)

It means—‘The man of perseverance and making efforts, gets the height of progress. The fatalists, depending on fate only and lazy will remain always helpless, destitute.’

 

You are a great man

Regarding our body, mind and circumstances, our several actions are done unwillingly and unknowingly. The actions which we consider being done willingly, are often the result of any excitement.

When any singer learns well to play on any musical instrument, then later on he does not need at all to pay attention to the movement of his every finger. While playing on his instrument. If he is concentrated to the words he is singing while playing on musical instrument, his fingers will work automatically exactly at the right place and according to the melody, the pitch-rhythm will come out. The same is the condition of our all actions. All these actions are done by our hidden mind. While doing any habituated action, the outer mind wanders about anywhere else, even then, by the influence of hidden mind the action goes on being done in its own way silently.

In our life we are in practice of doing any new work always which we are not even aware of. Some of them are of good habits and some bad. First, in the beginning they have light effect on us because of being ignorant of them, but in due long course of time when they become deeply rooted, it becomes very difficult to get rid of them. The habit of chewing betel, smoking, meat-eating, the dirty passion of seeing movies, using the rude and harsh and prideful words etc., among the friends and in the society start very minutely but with the passage of time they become deeply rooted in our life. The tendency of theft and crime among the children or the wicked passion of sex among the youths remain, growing up slowly and slowly. First, a very small act becomes the cause of the start of the dirty habit or poisonous thought, but when it grows up and becomes strong, it becomes almost impossible to get rid of it.

Progress depends upon our ownselves. Noble thought, good habits, or auspicious resolves are under our power. When the divine properties become silent, only then the wicked demoniac characters become active. The demoniac characters remain asleep in our mind or in other words, the divine tendencies present in our mind remain alert and awakened and keep them suppressed. The divine traits keep on the poisonous demons subdued and powerless. If we want the real joy or happiness and peace, we should maintain the divine characters as—love, pity, sympathy, service, sacrifice, modesty etc., always active, awakened and progressive. If the pious instincts or the gods, asleep in the world of your mind, remain always awakened and constant active in doing their divine acts, the demoniac characters will not get opportunity to grow up and the man will continue going ahead on the splendid path. By adopting the good resolve to activate it in practice is in our hands. If we are always alert and choose only good habits using our wisdom, we can make a good progress. We can shape our character according to our wish. The power of pious resolve is hidden in human being in natural way. The divine power is there in you by nature. We can expand it as much as we want by distinguhing it and constant practice.

By the practice of divine powers, develop them, mind it that your efficiency develops by practice day by day. If your divine powers are not used , they begin to decay. The cause of every action is thought. We are the undisputed lord of our mental empire.

The mental empire is also what a strange! There are strange imaginations in it and there are a lot of seen or unseen or heard matters of the world. In this empire there is no reach of any one else but you. This is such an empire where there is no motion of any grossness. This empire is situated in zero and that zero is not the zero of practical mathematics but shapeless. Even the air has no reach there.

In your mental, imaginary state you are completely free and you, yourself are the maker of all the rules. You are all in all. You can make impossible to possible. This is your such a hidden empire which is beyond the right of anyone and beyond the knowledge of anyone and neither there can be raised any objection by anyone against your thoughts.

Keep in mind, difficulties and comforts, success and failure, gain and loss, progress and downfall—all reflect in your life only according to your mind.

Never be disappointed, Remain always making efforts constantly for your progress, for the creation of noble habits, for the accomplishment of your good resolves, By making efforts again and again you will be encouraged and get success. Your hard and difficult works will become easier gradually. Your each and every effort, even your a little success is to enhance your spiritual power and self confidence. In future you will be able to do your work smiling. In the life it is the most necessary to go on making efforts remaining always alert for the accomplishment of auspicious resolves. This self-confidence is needed not only for the youths but for the old also.

Success is a habit

Success is a habit. Form the habit of success from the very childhood. Man’s mind is the repository of such powers which cannot be imagined by man himself. Napoleon Bonapart was considered the most powerful man of the world. He was a fearless and bold leader. It was his heroic and most courageous deed, that has made his name immortal in the history of the world, but when we see his life in the beginning, we are amazed how Napoleon could make so much progress.

‘Was he the son of any rich capatalist?’

‘Not at all. He was born in a poor family in an island; named Korsika.’

‘Were the facilities of education and life available to him?’

‘No, the poor Napoleon was deprived of any arrangement of education.’

‘Did he pass his childhood in comforts and grandeurous?’

‘No, his childhood was full of darkness. He was considered the boy of dull-mind since his childhood. In the beginning of life his health was also not satisfactory. Besides it, he was physically very weak, lean and thin.’

In spite of so many difficulties, miseries and oppositions, Napoleon had reached the top of success with the support of self-confidence, strong resolution and willpower. Despite his poverty and a little education, he became the ruler of France. This ruler was quite opposite to the Napoleon of childhood. Napoleon raised to the position of the commander of France army from a common soldier of the army. Having defeated the Europian countries he assimilated them in his ruling state. The cause behind his wonderful progress was his self-confidence. He always used to think in the kingdom of his mind that he was a brave man of the world. From the very childhood, the feeling of heroism and greatness had rooted in his mind. It was his version that with the support of firm resolve nothing is impossible in the world. From the early childhood he dreamt in his mind to rule the whole world.

You, too, should always have the dauntless faith in your confidence of greatness. Man is empowered with such a wonderful stock of power which is beyond the imagination of himself.

Because of being the domination of mind this body is named as ‘man’. The persons of developed mind should be called man. Everyone has the impact of mind in one’s life. Only due to his thoughts a man falls into the bondage or salvation. By the mental concentration to a single purpose, the energy is created. So, as are the thoughts, meditation and contemplation of mind, so will be our will power.

If your thoughts are lower graded, confined to the momentary enjoyments of sensuousness, sports, recreation and tours, the energy will also be likewise. How can they move ahead whose thoughts change from moment to moment?

You are not a feeble body but a spirit of supreme power. Where the thoughts are firm and doubtless, there is the unlimited and strong power. The steadiness and resolution in thought comes from faith.

Just consider, who are you? Are you simply a body? Are you an effigy made of bones, flesh, blood, skin etc., foul smelling and hateful objects? No, you are nothing like bone, flesh blood, you are the form of divinity. When anyone slaps on your body, you say ‘he beat me’. You, here, commit mistake. If you think seriously, you will come to realise that you are not simply a body, but thought yourself, you are yourself power, you are verily what as you think yourself. If you understand merely a body, then, you are simply a body. If you consider yourself a soul, great soul, developed, greater and supreme soul, the omnipotent spirit then, really you are omnipotent, endowed with all the virtues, a great warrior, full of patience, valorous outstanding man. You are the divine image. You can become whatever you like by your firm resolve.

You have the born natural right to become vigorous, strong, healthy lustrous. Never say that you are agonised, helpless, poor, old, sick, empty of energy and suffering from fever. These are the external matters, related to body only.

You are superior to body,—You are intellect, greater than intellect you are soul. You are the hero of the divine force. You are the lord of all. Have your mind under full control. Make it strong. The body will also obey the mind. Then, there will be no trace of sorrow, worry, weakness, old age or failure. Give up the feeling of infirmity. Wake up in the light of knowledge from the darkness of illusion.

This ‘if and but’. ‘If it had been so, I would have also made progress.’ ‘If I had favour of anyone, I would have been promoted ....... but it was not so.’ Qualification and worth have no meaning’, never talk such sentences of cowards. These words make you weak and feeble. Never allow room to sorrow, remorse, disease, pain, loss and disappointment, infirmity and misery in your mind and heart. It makes you lax, your rights are devastated and there comes the mentality of slavery in you.

Don’t make the public-slander a hurdle in the accomplishment of a higher goal. This thought checks you from the progress. It fetters your legs. ‘People will laugh, cut remark, public will ridicule, they will condemn’, don’t care for it. The path of progress is difficult and very hard and unbearable. It does not suit the world. The people of the world remain jealous of them who are making progress. If you care for the worthless matters of the world, having fallen into the pit of disappointment forever, you will always remain decaying in the same down condition. You will not be able to see the broad world coming out of the narrow well being the frog in the well. Such thoughts of weakness occur in the mind to test the power of resolution. So, without being deviated by such thoughts, testify your firmity. Don’t show your incapability. By firm resoluton, self-confidence and constant practice, even the impossible will become possible. Remain proceeding ahead having firm faith in God’s grace and spiritual force.

Don’t allow the soul to be disgraced, let not the spirit be disregarded. Let not the eternal illumination of the spiritual lamp be dim.

In the roar of the human world, despite hearing the nectareal words we behave as if unheard.

 

The noble thoughts have the power of new creations

Noble thoughts are the originator of man’s hidden mind, his present life and bright future. The desires lying in the hidden mind, our flights of imagination are fulfilled inevitably.

Contrary to it, the inferiority complex, worry, fear and disappointing thoughts decay our productive energy. The present life becomes hell. It results in suicides and heart-attacks. In spite of being alive the man lives like a dead man.

The common men lack the knowledge of what is the gain or loss of high pure thoughts and specially the uneducated persons are unaware of this fact at all. That is why in this world a numberless persons feel disturbance and problems in life.

If the people become aware of the way to have the pious thoughts and they begin to think in the positive direction, this world appearing so hard and full of problems, will become the heaven of joys. Wailing, remorse, worry, perplexity, fear, misery disappointment etc., mental feelings will be nowhere and the man will become the owner of the entire happiness and prosperity of the Lord, the creator.

Thought is the creative power. The sublime inclination and right way of thinking are the names of noble thought. This high thinking, the noble thought of self-welfare is the base of the future progress.

The thought even being invisible is everything. That is the best part of man’s mind. That is all valuable mental property. ‘Thought’ is not worthless at all, that is denomination, creative power, the form of progress. There lies the creative life. That is in itself life. That is the truth.

Thought is the original form of man. Whatever the repercussion is created, the form is shaped, the impression is felt by throwing stone, wood etc., in the water, there is more severe hurt made by throwing the thoughts through speech (speech-writing). The firm sublime thoughts create the better atmosphere. Whosoever comes in its surroundings, does not remain unaffected.

Thoughts have wonderful power to create new life, to form the new society and originate the new world. When the society adopts the new thoughts, the new generation starts pulling on life accordingly. One whose mind is full of zeal for the new and there lies the acute ambition in his mind to become great in life, one who wants to become a high officer, an eminent writer or a famous orator or leader, whose mind remains always creating big objects, high ideals in the void, in his state of mind, really, becomes great one day with the power of his thoughts—This is the experience of all the considerate and reasoning persons. All of them who have attained a very high position, rising from the ground or who have earned an immortal name, have given the priorty to the progressive sublime thoughts in every work.

The quote of a great learned man, Saloman is true to a great extent. He says that—‘As lasting emotions a man keeps in his mind, as he thinks in his mind, he becomes so gradually. Every thought forms the minute centres of his mind.’

But there is a misuse also of this power of thought. That is to remain engaged in worthless imaginations like a fool and never to do any solid work. By assuming air and sitting idle, none can make uplift. What is thought must be practised. Prove a true and pure gold in your action. There should be truth of resolution in your speech. There should be the background of action. The hands and legs both should be used together. The body should remain active.

The power of creation lies only in those thoughts where there is true faith, strong devotion and constant practice.

It is truly written in Bible—‘According to your faith, do it into you..’ So, it is clear that the power of life-creation lies only in high active thoughts.

Besides the pure and high thoughts a firm faith is needed. If a student’s mind is always bent upon doing the professional job, he will be an employee only in his later life, but if in any high ambitious mind, there are the grand thoughts of doing superior acts of benevolence, due to the spontaneous overflow of powerful feelings and resolute thoughts certainly he will be the master of any excellent action in future and rule over numbers of men.

The patients recovered by sublime thoughts

There was a report in a Newspaper that a mental doctor cured more than two hundred patients by the awakening of the noble thoughts in their minds.

Its secret is that to any patient or anybody as the thoughts and sermons are preached again and again with firmness, the same thoughts will be started to be practised by the patient with his body through his secret mind. The meritorious thoughts of health, joy, courage, prowess, vigour, happiness etc., were readout again and again to the mentally weak patients. So, their mind giving up the thoughts of disease and weakness heard and adopted the beneficial thoughts of health, pleasure, happiness etc. As a result, they began to feel themselves healthy and strong. As much gradually they attained health, happiness and energy.

Just mark, what a wonderful influence of right and healthy thoughts is!

This is the spell of the thoughts of a common category. When you make the strong practice of the reasoning science, you will realise the truth of thoughts and you will confirm it that really, it is the ‘thought’ only the most creative fertilising energy of man.

Even, by our mutual association the great purpose of ideas is achieved. They who are of pleasant and happy nature, are always happy, never worry; even in the miseries and hardships they remain absorbed in the lofty thoughts only and passs the time smiling. Anyone who meets him, how much sad, worried, distressed and troubled he might be, becomes pleased to see their smiling face. He forgets his agony and pain and becomes sharer of their pleasant company. Whenever, the men of joyous thoughts go, they rain the happiness and delightfulness everywhere.

Just contrary to it, there are such men also whose face is always swelled on account of anger, jealousy, deceit or agitation. Their face is ugly and they remain always surrounded with sad, bitter and poisonous atmosphere. Nobody wants to go to them and neither anyone wants to talk to them. Their faces remain faded due to their poisonous mentality only. They are source of disease, sorrow, grief everywhere.

There is the need of such men in the world whose heart is pious, sacrificing and full of love and who are the source of happiness to all, who may expand the empire of love, happiness and exhilarations in the society of the distressed and agonised persons.

The storage of the Supreme Lord is inside you, then why do you beg the alms of love, delight and happiness from others outside? Why do you become the beggar for man’s support?

In the boundless storage of the Supreme all the objects belong to Him, then why don’t you demand directly from Him? Why don’t you have faith in His power of making gifts?

The reason is that you were not educated since the childhood about the supremacy of the Lord and you have also started doing so imitating the weak and lethargic men of the world.

You have a great need of self-confidence. That self-confidence is the existence of God in you.

You will question, ‘Will the God bestow unexpectedly a large fortune?’ My answer is, ‘Yes, would give you’ Give place to self-faith in your mind.’

For the sake of example there are several such examples, but better you test by doing yourself. Mind again the following verse of the Gita 17/3—

सत्त्वानुरूपा सर्वस्य श्रद्धा भवति भारत।

श्रद्धामयोऽयं पुरुषो यो यच्छ्रद्ध: स एव स:॥

‘O Arjuna! The faith of all men conforms to their mental disposition. Faith constitutes a man; whatever the nature of his faith, verily he is that.’

And in the Bible there are many references at different places—‘If you demand in My name, then, believe, you will get and do realise this also that you got it. You will get certainly.’

But it is a matter of sorrow that we don’t awaken our spiritual force, don’t have full faith in our spiritual force, that is why we are agonised.

Think in the right direction

Several books have already been written on the power of thought and more others are in the process, but it seems that nothing has been written till now. We see that everyone is in the possession of that power but they are not making the best use of it as they ought to do. This is called—‘It is darkness under the lamp’.

Place your highest ideals, outstanding dreams, flourishing thoughts in your mind keep these ideals safe. Try to practise them in your daily life and daily works, apparently. If you are of firm determination on your beautiful thoughts, your future life will be shaped accordinly.

Healthy mind-creative, useful and self-supporting thoughtful mind is the architect of your life. The new directions of the progressive life are formed only by healthy and better mind and the body bears the fruits of good and bad works also due to mind. Throw out the feelings of defeat, timidity, inferiority, and worry from your mind. Don’t be afraid of defeat. Every defeat should create a new energy in you. The defeat should create new zeal and courage in you. The useful defeat means that circulates the new potency and the elixir of courage in you and makes the path easy for the victory.

But don’t try to complete all in hurry in a single day. Do your work with peaceful and balanced mind slowly and slowly. Your courage should be maintained constantly. In any condition that should not be loose. First, think over well that you are a developed soul and a man of prowess. You are fully capable to accomplish the work. You are the embodiment of victory. Make such thoughts the part and parcel of your nature. After some time, all your uphill tasks will become easy for you in the natural way.

Make your resolves strong. This firmity is the base foundation of your accomplishment. As you sow, so shall you reap. According to the men of prowess if the work is done with firmity, victory is a must. Let your hidden potency go on increasing. If you are not successful, don’t blame the nature of situations or anyone else unnecessarily.

 

Have faith, the future is ready to welcome you with golden days

Probably, you have already made up your mind, that the golden days of your life have passed away and the highest achievements to be achieved have been achieved by you.

This is a false notion. Having abandoned it, adopt the new optimistic view.

Human life is very long. Everyday and every moment a new success is achieved. Any invisible hand inspires at every moment for a new progress.

Life is like a big book of which every page goes on opening gradually. God knows! What its expansion is! How long will it go? How long is its destination!

Listen to an event of a day. I was sitting in the Post Office. At the same time an young man of thirty to thirty-five years came there to withdraw his deposited amount from his saving account. His face was faded with worry, sadness and a great disappointment. His face was growing pale.

By the way, the discussion started. I asked in amazement, ‘Why brother! Why are you closing your account?’ He turned his faded face towards me. He said with disappointed eyes, ‘Doctor Sahib! What to say! I am entangled with miseries!’ I said—‘Are you entangled in any court case?’

He said—‘Brother! I did not see even the face of the court throughout my life. Here, I have another problem.’

I was astonished. Different types of arguments were arising in my mind. He, himself began to narrate his story.

He said—‘I have been consulting the doctors since the last year and seeking their advice. Sometimes I have stomach-ache and always feel heaviness in my stomach. I consulted many doctors; but the last doctor gave his finding that I had developed a disease, named appendicitis. The last portion of my intestine has decayed. That is the cause of the heaviness, old constipation and pain. Through operation that portion will be cut down and separated. I have been postponing this operation for one year. Now, the doctor advises for immediate operation, otherwise death is inevitable. My wife and children are too much disturbed. Hence, I want to handover the amount remaining with me in the deposit and then, I should be ready for the peaceful death.’ While saying this, tear came in the eyes of the youth. I was also shocked for a moment. Then, I said, ‘Have you consulted any other doctor also?’

He said—‘I have already consulted the most expert doctors also. I have no faith in the common Vaidyas. The medical Science is so advanced and therefore, there is no scope of doubt.’

I—‘Do you have faith in God and Naturopathy?’

He—‘No, I believe in only what can be proved by logic and which may satisfy my mind and wisdom.’

I—‘For the God’s sake, postpone your operation for the next few days and let me treat you for a week. When ultimately, you have to die, enjoy the light and air of the world for a week more.’

He was impressed to some extent. I said to him, ‘Soul is closely related to God. So, you are free from any disorder, accept it. Unnatural way of living and polluted view of an atheist, has made you to consider that this God-gifted body as the storage of diseases.

“Now, get up early in the morning and concentrate your mind to the changeless, free from vices and disease, pure, immutable, the eternal Supreme Lord. Say to yourself—‘I am completely well and healthy. There is no trace of any polluted flaw. The divine spirit is getting awakened in me and it is getting me rid of all the disorders. My entire body is quite healthy, free from any disease. I have no contact with any disease. I am a man of pure and changeless body. I am healthy. My stomach is doing the function of digestion properly. All the accumulated flaws have been removed away.’

‘This was the mental treatment. It will revive your lost self-confidence and wonderful miracle of Divine Power will come out in your bdoy?’

“The next number is of Naturopathy. You are a clerk. You work for eight to ten hours sitting in the chair, bending down your waist. So, you are suffering from the acute constipation. Drink double water. Take maximum fruit juice and make the fruits your regular diet; eat the tomato and mango by sucking it. The last advice is that you should walk daily in the morning for two hours without any break. Do the manual work. Well! The body will be completely transformed.”

The spiritual treatment had such an effect and by the grace of the God that gentleman began to recover. Within a week the heaviness of his stomach reduced. The use of Anima was also continued to clear the stomach. Now his health is more than satisfactory. He has got a new life and his doubt of appendicities has also been removed from his mind.

Now he has become theist in his view also. He has developed his full faith in the prayer of God and water-treatment. I usually advise him even today—‘The best time and the best success of your life is still waiting to welcome you in future.’

He usually answers—‘I have experienced the power of God and got the healthy life. Is it not enough! The power which could not be convinced by anyone has come out by devotion.’ Sometimes, that which we have already considered the end of life becomes the beginning of success. So, we should never be disappointed.

 

The imperishable treasure of spiritual power

Spiritual Power

When you see the laughing-tittling fragment flowers on any charming juicy branch, a longing rises in your heart—‘How good it would have been that I would have also been simple, charming and attractive and innocent like them! I would have also been so colourful like them and fragrant with the scent of virtues; I would also have been innocent and affectionate; I would have also led a carefree bereft of showy life!’

When you see the bright sparking colours of a peacock’s feathers and find him in the oblivious condition completely absorbed in dance, abruptly desirous you became that—‘Would that I could also dance in such an attractive manner and could attract others fascination, the movement of my feet could express out the profound feelings of my heart. The sweet and touching songs of my heart could express my joys and sorrows, hatred and love, hopes and disappointments etc.!’

When we read the most touching stanzas of any devotional poet or poetess, or hear the devotional songs there is created a forceful desire in our heart involuntarily, ‘If I could also sing the sweet songs and compose the touching devotional song and would express my mental conflicts in the devotional voice! By the queer mixture of devotion and poetry, I could feel the spiritual joy and with the union of self-devotion, my life would be auspicious and peaceful! The people could feel fresh, with the cultural awakenning in my speech!

When we hear the highly developed moral tendency of Prahlad, Dhruv etc., the virtuous morality of moral and chaste women, the sacrifice of Dadhichi for the protection of divinity, the valiant stories of the martyrs to free the country from slavery, the firmity and courage of brave Hakikatrai, the heroic and fearless inspiring occurences of Guru Govind Singh’s sons, the intense desire is created in our mind and heart that—‘Would that I could also expose these high morals and merits, these characteristics, these ideals and high emotions in my life! I would also sacrifice my life on these altar of freedom!’

Wherever we see the high conducts and merits, health, charm or any praiseworthy art or skill, in any other one, a high intense ideal sentiment and feeling is created in ourself silently from unknown source, ‘Would to heaven that I could also demonstrate the same divine feeling or outstanding powers!’ Every goodness creates an awakenning in us, wakes up our latent spiritual potency and gives a secret indication to go a head towards higher. It is our hidden spiritual power that creates interest and courage towards goodness and superiority. The temptation and desire of our heart towards the noble qualities and virtues of others and to imitate them is only due to this storage of our potential spiritual power.

On the other side there is an other concept.

When you see any mad making delirious talk, wrapped in odd and filthy cloths, speaking meaningless, there is never a desire in you that ‘I, too, should become foolish, intoxicated and unbalanced like him.’ When you see any thief, robber, or criminal being convicted or being outcasted in the society, you never want at all to become a thief robber or criminal. When we see any leper, crippled, sick, feeble, poor, destitute, defamed, outcasted, convict our mind never tempts us to become so. To see an ugly man we never long to be ugly ourselves. To see a patient we never desire to become a patient.

We don’t want to become the tormentor of subjects or dictator like Kans. We have no sympathy at all for Ravan, the kidnapper of Sita and inclined towards tyrany and torture. We have no affection for wicked Duryodhan who tortured his brothers and got butchered the numberless men. We hate the wickeds, immorals, the oppressors of subjects, brutals, killers of mankind, annihilators, exploitors, drinkers, gamblers and lustful persons. We never want to become anyone of them. All the evil tendencies are against our spirit. Our natural attitude is never inclined towards them.

We proceed only towards the virtues, morality, noble tendency, high arts and scripts and divine qualities of Divinity. Our self-spirit is the nectar basin of all the divine qualities. That is such a divine centre, where our high ideal tendencies and feelings go on sparking like the sparks of fire. The green trees are seen flourishing on the spots where the water is hidden underground. In the same way where the spiritual truth of mankind is awakened, our mentality and tendency remains attracted towards the divine qualities of soul. That proceeds ahead towards divinity. The spiritual truth loves the virtues and all the dignities. In splendour and glory of the society it is our spiritual truth only that is circulating. The root centre of glory, supreme and beauty is our own spirit the embodiment of Truth, Consciousness and Bliss.

 

What will you collect, poison or honey?

In the earth, sky, light, air, soil, potency—all are equally available to all, but the sugarcane taking out the living element from the earth and collecting the quality of sweetness, provides us sugar, jaggery, relish and sweet-meat; lemon orange, tomato, tamarind, ginger collect sourness; the bitter gourd collects the bitter element; the chilli pungent, the ginger becomes acrid. are generated from the same earth according to the seeds. Every seed takes out the living element from the earth according to its nature and character and actions. Despite the equality of the earth, water, air, sky to all there is distinction in the new objects. The same is the condition of mankind living in the human world.

For all the human beings world is the same. It has plenty of prosperity action, honour, repute, pleasure, health, life-element, property lying scattered. For all, but everyone is collecting joy and sorrow according to his natural disposition and mentality. There are so many enjoying the happiness of life and so many are suffering the tortures of hell. We make our own separate world ourselves according to our mentality, interest, nature, character, action and our view of life.

The fancy of heaven and hell always revolves in human mind, they cannot be fulfilled in the outer world; they are created according to the individual thoughts and action in this very world. There might be heaven or hell, but here in this world, we are ourselves creator of the joys of heaven or tortures of hell for our life.

You will be astonished how a man can enjoy heaven? Heaven is the invaluable creation of the Supreme Lord. How can a human being share his hand there? Man is a feeble effigy of flesh and bones; what can be possible for him?

But such doubts are useless. In the creation of our world we are more responsible. Our mind is busy in weaving the warp and woof of heaven and hell. We can attain the salvation, supreme bliss and supreme abode not after death but in this very world, in this life by this human body when we are alive. It is the mind that changes the heaven into hell and just when our view changes by illuminating the hell with divine light our mind changes it into heaven.

You will ask, ‘How is heaven possible on the earth?’ Where is capability in us to do so? It is the vicissitudes of fortune that does everything. Who can drive the chariot of fate?

The first way to create the heaven on the earth is—healthy body. Body is that insturment through which you take out the subtle particle of heaven and hell from the earth. The sick, feeble, weak, loose, devoid of valour, filthy body is such a defective instrument that can take out only disappointment, jealousy, anger, hosility, sexual passion, bitterness, malice from the earth. That element contains only to take out filth merely and to create the atmosphere accordingly. The sick body has the sick mind. What will a sick mind create except hell? The prurient body will think of only fornication, the greedy mind will run only after money. The angry mind will collect the aids of its agitation itself. The jealous mind will collect itself the materials of its sorrow and vexation. This world will appear to sick body as a shackled, full of sorrow and difficulties, internal agony, opposite to it, he whose body is healthy and sound, finds the world as heaven.

The second element is—Man’s view towards life. The man who has the pessimistic view about life, will get nothing except difficulties, disappointment failure; what more will he get? He will get the sources of wailing and lamentation anywhere. Such men are habitual of sorrow. This will create the mental hell. Against it, the optimistic person will any how and anywhere find out the support of living a happy life and a courageous life. From mental point of view, the optimistic and pessimistic view is the creator of heaven and hell. What is the colour in our mind, the surroundings and everywhere looks accordingly. The reflection of our inner mind creates the happiness and sorrow in this world.

If we want, we can create in the inner side or outer side both the atmosphere of love joy and courage with the higher counsels, we can make the surrounding atmosphere fragrant with the fragrance of heaven by our pious thoughts and feelings. Contrary to it we can make our innerside and outerside both as hell by the vicious desires.

Whether you will collect poison like a scorpion or honey like a honey-bee?

 

Be optimistic in your view

The worried or a happy life depends on our outlook and view of life. Actually, ‘What is our point of view regarding any event’—This element creates our mental world. If you take your life with happy, exhilarating and optimistic point of view, it is certain that in spite of distressed mind, you will lead a happy and optimistic life. The man concentrated to his tragic events of life will be facing the sorrow and agony only despite his sound and healthy atmosphere.

For example, go through the life of the men of mean mentality as mentioned by Sri Anant Gopal Seware—

It is in our hand to accept the calamity as calamity or not. There are some such events, to break out fire in the house, or the death of any dear one, bankruptcy, to loose the case, long sickness, imprisonment, daughter’s marriage, son’s education etc., undoubtedly cause us trouble to some extent but we begin to consider it so seriously and excessively as if the mountain on our head and think that the great calamity has fallen on us. There is no lack of persons in our society who consider the rope as a snake and start trembling. One of my friends was in jail who had been sentenced to jail for one and half years. He counted the days daily that when he would be released.’ I said—‘O brother! Now it is remaining only one year in place of one and half years. What time will it take to pass on?’ Under the walls of prison, there are some who see either the mud of the ground or walls of the jail only and there are some who make themselves joyous to stare the stars of the sky?

When I was in the boarding, I used to purchase the objects of need sharing it with my room partner. When the bottle of the scented oil remained half empty, he said—‘Just see, how fast is this oil of half of this bottle finished in twenty days only?’

‘O dear, how is it empty? Still it is half full.’ I said.

Ponder over seriously on the above examples. Difference of views is clearly visible in it. The writer’s smiling face and encouraging others is optimism where he looks only the merits in others and takes inspiration from them. The second is the pessimistic view where he has made himself half dead due to the great disease of worry, in spite of everything with him. As long days you will remain half dead in the worry of false fear, in so long days, the optimist with his happy appearance will gather so much power and means that the mishappenings will not be effective on him. What a matter of sorrow it is that we don’t change our wrong and poor outlook? We should have the outlook of hope, courage, joy, and self-interest.

Sir Walter Scatt’s example is inspiring to us. To run a Press Sir Walter Scott had been loaded with such a heavy loan that a man of common moral strength would have gone mad due to the heavy load on mind but Sir Walter Scott did not allow his mental condition to be deviated and continuously for forty years he went on writing novels and cleared off the entire loan by its earning.

Lowal Thomas also had to face the problem of loan, he got fierce disappointments, but in spite of all he had never felt worried. He knew that if he got worried about his loans, his productive and creative efficiency would be crippled and his money-lenders would surround him and start buzzing on him like buzzing bees. So, daily in the morning he bought one flower and linking it to the button of his coat, singing the melodious song set out to walk towards the Oxford street. He always kept the feelings of fearlessness, vigour and optimism in his mind and never accepted defeat even in adverse situations. He remained always alert in making efforts to find out any way to make the circumstances in his favour.

How the change of outlook or view influences the mind to be strong or weak will be clear to you through this example of the book ‘The Psychology of Strength’ (Shakti Ka Manovigyan) written by J. A. Hadfield. He writes—‘I have tested three men’s strength in the influence of mental suggestion. That strength test was made by catching the Dynamo Metre. I instructed them to hold the Dynamo Metre strongly and tested their physical strength in three different situations of mind.’

When I tested them while working in commonly average condition their average strength to hold it was 101 pound and again they were indicated by mental suggestion that they had grown weak. The sign of weakness was growing in them. This indication had such a fatal impact on them that their energy reduced to 29 pound. Thus, they were given the solid indications of their loss of strength, weakness, decayed vitality again and again by hypnotism. As a result, they became so weak that one of them happened to say that he had no strength even equal to a child. I am a child without energy. My all the limbs of the body have gone lax.

Then, again having put these men under creative and solid clues their physical strength was tested. ‘You are strong, you are vigorous.’ There cues had such a forceful impact that their strength increased to 142 pound. By the encouraging cues, five hundred percent of increase has been found in their physical strength. This above mentioned example makes it crystal clear how much effective the view of mind is.

Once, a sick man lying on a bedstead was brought before Christ, the great. Christ’s mental point of view was always full of exhilaration, strength and optimism. He said to the sick man, ‘Son! Be happy ...... your sins will be forgiven by the Lord ...... Stand up and go home on foot.’ By this cue of firmly and self confidence, there was such a wonderful impact on that sick man that really he stood and began to walk. It was the statement of the sick man that ‘These courageous and inspiring words had such a miracle on him as if there was the overflow of the powerful energy in his innerself.’

Del Karnegi is of the opinion that man can be completely free from worry, fear and different types of other many diseases by the support of optimistic courageous views. He should develop love for life. He should get absorbed in the well-wishing emotions to throw away the causes of worries with the support of sympathy.

D. Larson’s statement is that the new psyche specialists have made the research that there are little objects in our life which have more impact on our mind and body than happiness. Spirit, body and mind all are balanced to joy. Thousands of men have been ruined in absence of happy mentality. So, for the long life, pleasure and health, worry is dangerous.

The body demands happiness, hope, exhilaration and peace. In want of necessary substance the spirit is pained. We should fulfil the demand of body by remaining happy and exhilarated always.

 

Died in the age of thirty, buried at sixty

It should be inscribed on the graves of most of the persons dying nowadays. ‘Died in the age of thirty but buried at sixty.’ Why? There are many persons in my notice who start declaring themselves old even in their youthful age of thirty. Life is the name of cheerfulness and their cheerfulness perishes to dust from their very childhood. The sweet feelings of enthusiasm, carefreeness delight, dreams and the sweet and pleasant imaginations of youthfulness have taken plight from their hearts forever. Life has become dim, tasteless, momentry and transient for them. Just pay attention to the following sentences of the letter written by a modern youth and then you will come to know what is their attitude towards life—

‘.....Sometimes I remember the room of the boarding, when I used to be with you, when there was a spring in our movements, picnics and day-to-day life. Then, life was like an intoxicating object and we could be more intoxicated and infatuated, carefree and absorbed in it. When there felt a great delight in the gossip with the friends and in the presentation of minds minute motion. Now, it seems that the feeling of satisfaction and contentment has destroyed the sharpness of mind and body. I am not in any trouble but rather comfortable. My desires are fulfilled before I express. Yet I am lacking that joy of those days. A strange laziness has overpowered. Like watch I am going on counting the hours and minutes of life. To talk with you about the unworried carefree old days; not in the present and future, bathing in the past I want to become again young and joyous for sometime.....’

Such a condition of apathy, helplessness, disappointment and inefficiency is not only of my this friend but of thousands of others. God knows why the people are not hopeful and optimistic about life. Today we see that many a man becomes old and weak untimely earlier in life and become the prey of untimely death. By decreasing slowly and slowly a man’s age has reduced to thirty to thirty-five. This concept has prevailed among us that this is our real age. The miserable result of this rooted illusionary feeling is that to see anyone in the old age, in our mind also the same idea is created that I will also reach the same position very soon. My cheeks will also be shrivelled, the eye-sight will be weak, the body will be in a deplorable and helpless condition and then one day ...d...ea...th. Enough, being afraid of this idea we have the assumption of different baseless fears. We always remain absorbed in the hearti rending and painful feelings of old age. It is not known what the more we think, and in the same worry remaining absorbed we come to invite that great monster too earlier than matured time who has chewed away I don’t know, how many.

Keep in mind—To think of diseases and other adverse results, we corrupt our mind and provide a suitable place for them in our body, and then the disease makes its claim in our body. To be fully overpowered by the imaginary fear of old age and always dreaming the old age and burning in the fire of old age, we invite of making the favourable circumstances and situation. The moment, the imagination of any wicked thought, disasterous disease or any other miserable imagination comes to our mind, at once its image or photo is printed in our mind. Then, the same disease, the same worry the same wicked imagination makes a very bad effect in the form of any serious and dreadful disease on our body. With the same types of unhealthy and disappointing thoughts we damage our fate with our own hands. We ourselves cover the moon light of happiness and health with black clouds.

William Lyan Philips asserts—‘I can tell you the exact time when the man starts growing old. That is the moment when he feels after self-examination that while sitting aloof his mind and thought is attracted towards the past more than future. When man’s mind remains stored with the old happening, the old memories, reminiscence and the past events, understand that he is growing old.’

After passing many years and facing many adversities in search of the way out to get rid of the feelings of old age, I suddenly came to know that always remaining worried about it, cannot give me success to get it. To cut short a long story is that we should not allow our mind to think even for a moment that we are growing old, we are ill, or weak. Forget your age completely, don’t pay your attention towards it at all. Never think of them. Not of only yours but don’t allow your mind to give entry to the thought of others decaying age also. Make a firm resolve in your mind that you will not be old still. But reverse to it form a habit of dreaming the happy youthfulness. Enter into it with the high ideals of youth and until your each particle is overwhelmed with those divine emotions, don’t separate those divine ideals even to the size of mole hill from your innerself. As will be our ideals, so will be our ambitions, and as will be our feelings of heart, so will be their glimpse visible on our face and the reflection of the same will twinkle in our eyes. We should be fully confident and well determined that we have no concern at all with impotency, lazinesss, diseases, disappointment, mental and physical agony and death.

If we continue the spontaneous divine flow of youthfulness and having the ideals of youth infront, having faith in our potency for them make efforts and always keep the rules of health and energy before us and throwout the worry, fear and doubt from our mental ambit, the old age will remain afraid of us. Let the courage shower on the grass of youthfulness that has grown in your heart. Follow the rules of conduct with pure celibacy. Keep it in your mind that the presumption of time of the old age to start and loosing potency has caused a great loss to the human society. Whatever such types of grass and straw have established their roots in our mental garden, should be started to be rooted out from just now. Man never grows old, but he, himself, feels old. You cannot be old so long as there is the dominance of sweetness, modesty, and courage in your mind and heart, so long as your heart remains illuminated with the divine light of ambition, so long as the fear of old age is not created in your mind, so long as there is the flow of potency in your blood to work and your physical strength is not lost. Build a grand building of pleasure and happiness in your heart with these joy giving potencies.

 

We should pass our life smiling like the flowers

There are three works on priority in human life—work, recreation and rest. Everyone of the common people takes at least eight hours compulsory out of twenty-four hours of day and night to earn his livlihood. After taking out eight hours for rest, eight hours time is remaining for leisure. This is a problem of consideration how to use these eight hours of leisure period to get maximum delight, pleasure and peace.

Evade always shedding tears

This is the version of numerous men that—‘I have no time for recreation and to enjoy the charms of life. I am surrounded with so many problems that I always remain entangled with them day and night and thus, I am very much disturbed.’ This is uttered by him in such an anguished mood that it indicates his helplessness, disappointment and incapability.

You ask the ladies—‘What do you do the whole day?’ They will say—‘In baking the bread, looking after the children, fulfilling all the domestic chores, sweeping the house, cleaning the utensils, washing the clothes, preparing the children for school and sewing the clothes, I remain so busy that I have no time for rest.’ While saying so their face will become withered with worry, disappointment, pain and internal agony. They are as if weeping, their appearance will cause you to presume that they are passing their life in wail and cry. The load of the worldly worries is so heavy on them that they are doing nothing except wailing-crying and bearing the heavy useless burden in their life. What is the gain of such life as deprived of even two minutes of recreation?

Life overpowered by wealth

Most of the rich people and shopkeepers, government officers and officials, businessmen are always assiduous in earning and counting the money, but they are not conscious of using their time and money for their life and pleasure. Some ignorant persons have made the aim of their life to earn money only. The riches have overpowered their life. That has become the cause of their numberless worries. Even the family life and domestic joys have taken flight from their life.

Remember, money is the means of life. Life is bigger and greater than money. Don’t allow so much freedom to money that it may begin to rule you and torture your life with the serious burden of worry, anxiousness and meaningless works. Life is more important than money. Its usefulness depends on the progress, prosperity and satisfaction of life. Money is needed in your life only to the extent that it may fulfil your justified needs and may not be an obstacle in the progress. More than that, to hoard the money or to become a capitalist, don’t destroy the divine element like this life. When you are in the possession of the money to fulfil your general needs, use it then for the purpose of enjoyment.

Adoration of supreme bliss

The real aim of life is to achieve the supreme joy. We should try to get maximum delightfulness, comforts, laugh and happiness. The man deprived of happiness and pleasure, who remained a toiling wretch and bearing the load of the world throughout the life or remained engaged in collecting the money, despite being called wealthy from economic point of view but on the surface of truth, could not take the taste of life. Joy is that spiritual element, which gives our mental wisdom a great delight and contentment, the entire happiness of the world is achieved.

What is joy? Joy is related to our mind. Our five sense-organs are constantly in process of giving the experience of joy or sorrow to our mind. Every sense-organ may be related to our joy or sorrow. If we maintain every sense-organ active for the feeling of joy, the expansion of joy is possible.

Our happiness is internal. The men who search for it in the outer material objects are at fault. Making contact with the worldly objects, our all the five sense organs who transmit its knowledge to our inner world, create the feeling of joy in our mind. So to get comforts and happiness, we should keep our mind in the situation of joy and happiness having our mind free from the feeling of disappointment, worry, inferiority complex. This is the main gist of our mental condition.

New life

They, whose aim of life is the maximum gain of happiness and delightfulness, reach near it by shaping the same mental condition. This is the element of our mental favour that takes out continents from the atmosphere.

The need of optimistic view

As much close attachments we keep to the worldly objects, as much we increase our artificial needs, so much worries we invite. Different kinds of worries make the music of our life out of tune and jarring and we fail to create the sweet atmosphere of happiness. We go on peering and vexing making the issue of trifling matters. Our life remains full of botherations. We pass the miserable life of wail and cry associated with worry.

Don’t remain weeping but remain carefree. Remain establishing closeness more and more with the substance of happiness. The objects or matters for which you remain worried day and night are in your contact for a very short time. Then, why to make our life thorny for them?

We should lead our life smiling like flowers. Just see the nature, there is the pleasant atmosphere of joy everywhere. How joyously is breezing the morning cool air! Listen to the chirping of birds in the garden. How carefreely flows and falls the water of small and big rivers, fountains and brooks! Every drop as if happens to laugh having been scattered and speaks, ‘O the men of world! Burst to laugh in merry making. Lead the life smiling. Leave the worthless worries.’

What is the capital with the birds? What amount have they deposited in the banks? For how many years have they made the stock of food materials to eat? How many quilts, beds, costly and decent garments to wear, rooms, motors are there they have? In spite of being penniless, in spite of no arrangement of food, clothes and house for the next day, how happy and carefree life they lead! How melodious and sweet song they sing with carefreeness! See the peacock while dancing! What a carefree and different modes of dance he makes! His dance of fifteen to twenty minutes is a bath in the ocean of joy. He has no worry of either children or worldly botherations. We should learn lesson of joy from these creatures of Nature. We should imbibe the blessedness of their lives.

Take the vow of delightfulness

Come and be a striver of the truth of joy to give up your artificial and wicked worries and ill feelings and imaginations forever. Go on tasting the taste of life. Colour your each and every nerve of the body in the colour of happiness. Laugh self and distribute your exhilaration, carefreeness and delightfulness among others with liberal attitude. Consider the world full of joy. If we, having given up the mean view about life, ‘This world is the ocean of joy’—Put up this feeling before us, then our sorrow misery, agony and useless worries will end in no time. Our mental tendencies will concentrate in truth, consciousness and bliss solidified God; and our imaginary sufferings and botherations will go away.

He who has become stable in the Supreme form of spiritual Truth, is really blessed. Having come out of the darkness of ignorance and illusion he has come in the illumination of joy, courage, zeal and hope. By the worship of supreme joy man’s inner and outer life both becomes full of self-satisfaction. He, himself begins to feel that the life afflicted with modification, fear, worry, anger, passion and sensuousness cannot enjoy the bliss of joy, Materialistic granduer and prosperity, money, paramountcy are not the cause of self-contentment.

Let us determine to enjoy happiness always in every situation, in every atmosphere, enjoy the enjoyments of the world; because our concern is with joy. We are born to enjoy only. The adverse and indomitable circumstances can not create hurdle in our merriment. Having changed your outlook and having the ideal of achieving the righteous joy before you lead your life. Wherever in any situation you are, you can lead a joyous life adopting the optimistic view.

 

The maximum engagement in work, the maximum span of life and health

शतं जीव शरदोवर्धमान:।

(Atharvaved 3/11/4)

Means—‘Live a hundred years life, spend the energy of life with such restraint as you may live fully for one hundred years.’

वर्च आ धेहि मे तन्वां सह ओजो वयो बलम्।

(Atharvaved 19/37/2)

Means—‘Considering your body the divine temple of the Lord look after it in all respects. Increase lustre, courage, vigour, age and vitality in your body.’

अश्मानं तन्वं कृधि।

(Atharvaved 1/2/2)

Mean—‘Make your body strong like stone, By hard working and endurace the body becomes strong.’

In my neighbourhood, a Govt. employee retired from service in the age of fifty-five. He used to say, ‘There will be no work after the retirment from Govt. office and then I will live very happily. I will make my health better only. The rest life will pass very smoothly and there will be relaxation from the hard work and control.’

And one day, he got his pension. He got relief from the work. Now, he was the sole owner of his time. There was no work but only rest.

No doubt, he got leisure but his mind began to feel heavy and his health also got as if rust. He passed a few days here and there on the shops, the houses of the friends and acquainted and sitting anywhere in the Mohalla but yet his mind was restless. One day, four days, one month, two months! Ultimately how long to sit! Life is very long, it is unknown how long is its root? He got fed up with inactive life. He became ill. The disease went on increasing and he became confined to his bed. The doctors treatment continued. The man who worked hard for eight hours till a few months back, was the same man showing his pulse to the doctors and was counting the hours of death.

While lying on the bedstead, there was an inspiration by God that—‘idle life without any work being rusted, will cause death. That is a sort of suicide. So long as body is active, something must be done.’

Well! He went to his old office. By chance, he got any simple job in the same office on daily wages. He accepted the same.

A matter of great astonishment! God’s sportive activity! For two to four days, he went to the office any how, but after three to four days, his physical instruments became active and began to work. The instruments that had gone rusted again began to work on account of the practice of work. Due to the engagement in work, he had no time at all to imagine of old age, disease and weakness or useless imaginations.

Now, he goes to the office as usual. He works like the young men. He gets a meagre amount but he does not care for it. His shackled life is pulling on ahead. From 10 a.m. to 5 p.m. his day passes in work. His wife is already dead. There is no work at home, but yet he remains busy in work. He expresses the gist of his life in the following words—

‘I consider the work the best medicine for a man. The active life solves those problems of life where the costly medicines fail. Action expands the span and health in life. By continuing some mental and physical work, a man can live a long life. The long-lived creatures of Nature remain always active. If long life and health is to be achieved, remain busy in work till the last moment of life.

Eighty years old a female student

This news is related to Paris. A snow-white haired grand mother had been divorced sixty years ago by her husband due to difference of opinion between them. When she searched work for herself, she found that she could remain more happy in the mental work of study and writing. She again started to study in the Sarbon University of Paris. Eighty years old this zealous lady was still a special student of Sarbon University even in 1905, because in those days, she was studying Science. This lady has three sons, seven grand daughters and one great grand daughter. She considers work most important to remain mentally healthy and long lived. Now, she has taken admission in the University to study English and German.

She usually says, ‘This is my personal experience that I have come to conclude that by running the machine of man’s body regularly, it works for a long time. The man who remains busy in doing any useful work as much, so much he enjoys the sound health.

Here, the words said by Mahatma Gandhi, come to my mind that—‘He is the true student, who has a true thirst of getting knowledge, who feels joyous to meet the hardships in acquiring knowledge and who forgets everything making the knowledge the centre and end of life. It anyone studies with the consideration of the knowledge as the means of earning money, then, neither he will achieve the high ideal to achieve his goal nor will his labour prove to be worthful.’

One hundred fifteen years old employee of the Post Office

At Dhanbad, recently, one hundred fifteen years old employee of the Post Office has passed away from the mortal world. People have been heard admiring him highly.

This is the statement of the acquainted persons that the above mentioned employee of the Post Office performed his duty of a Postman going on foot. Throughout his life, he remained moving out sufficiently. He had a great hatred for the lazy and inactive life. He had not preferred even to buy a cycle. Even in this old age, his mind was cool. He was never found indulged neither in any intoxication nor ever angry.

Even after retirment from his service, he had availed pension for sixty years. The health of this employee, leaving after him a brimful family of grand sons and great grand sons, was fully maintained due to walking, moving about and remaining busy in any work. Whenever anyone querried of his health, he uttered only one thing, ‘I never sit idle, remain busy in doing something always. This is my conviction that it is the practice of work that can make a man healthy and long lived.’

Horse-riding even in the age of 159 years

The oldest man, Shirali Mislimov of Moscow of the republican state, Ajarbejan of Soviat State celebrated his 159th birthday in Baku. In Baku, a ceremonial funcation was organised in his honour. Mislimov refused to cover the distance of six miles from his house to Baku by car. He went to the place of the function on foot to a distance and then riding on horse. According to ‘Tas’, in spite of being so old Mislimov is quite active. He remains busy in walking on foot and taming the sheep. He does not sit idle. He has interest in work. He neither drinks wine nor smoke cigarette; but he eats vegetables and fruits mostly. His wife is 85 years old and his eldest grand son is 65 years old.

The growing age in Russia

In Russia, generally people are long lived. In the recent past, it had been published in the papers—‘A one hundred fifty-eight years old farmer, Makhmud Evajov, who had participated in the ‘Agriculture exhibition’ is famous for his long age and balanced moral life in Soviet Union. In the honour of his praiseworthy work last year in 1965 the Soviet government has awarded him with the award ‘Order of Red Banner of Labour’. His experiences are as such—

‘In continuing the practice of some mental and physical labour the taste of life is created and the body organs remain active properly. By sitting idle they are rusted and grow old untimely. Just as the water remains soft; pure and healthful due to its flow, similarity the nervous system remains active by work. To maintain the youthful potency of the body organs ‘work’ is the most important factor. This is the fatal mistake of a number of persons that they understand that the old persons should not work or minimise their movement. I do tell you on behalf of my personal experience that so long as this body is fit to work, the mind and spirit should be kept loaded with the burden of work. All the limbs of the body should be kept active more and more. To sit idle is harmful to the both—the mind and the body.

The work plays the decisive role in the growth of the age. It is the well known fact that a man can live long only on the basis and support of the systemetic work.

The tainted effect of sitting idle

On one side Iran Patrovich Pavlov the scholar of physical science used to say—‘A clerk remaining busy with his work, which is not very difficult maintains a satisfactory health till the age of seventy, but just when he retires and as a result leaves his daily routine, his body organs become incapable to work and he dies soon. It is so usually with everyone who becomes free from all types of work in the old age. There are so many matters in my knowledge where comparatively active, smart, cheerful and hale and hearty persons who retrive on pension, have suddenly grown weak and fallen ill. This is the reason that after retirement the man should not leave the work completely but he must go on doing some easy works like gardening, music, literary work, moving about going on tours, to tame the pet animals, to feed seed to the birds, full bath, to live in the open atmosphere, to play with the children or to teach them, worship and devotion and to do the work of cleanliness in the temples etc., life giving works.’

The whole world is active

Actually, the whole world is active. Inactiveness is apperantly death. Only the man busy with work is healthy, under self-control, free from defile and agitation, cheerful and liberal. The perfection of work gives joy to the living being.

Lord Krishna has said in the Gita the same thing in these words—

न हि कश्चित् क्षणमपि जातु तिष्ठत्यकर्मकृत्।

कार्यते ह्यवश: कर्म सर्व: प्रकृतिजैर्गुणै:॥

(3/5)

‘Surely, none can ever remain inactive even for a moment; for, everyone is helplessly driven to action by nature-born qualities.’

Ò Ò Ò Ò

शरीरयात्रापि च ते न प्रसिद्धॺेदकर्मण:॥

(3/8)

Means—‘Without action a man cannot remain alive even for a moment. Each and every creature has natural tendency that he should continue doing something. If anyone does not even agree with any purpose of life, even then only to remain alive, work is necessary. The whole world is active.’

Then, why do you only considering yourself more aged sit idle doing nothing? Must do something.

Just mark the working of the world. What is law working in the secret of Nature-functions? What is the character of living being? What is difference between animate and inanimate objects? What is that character that helps us to differenciate the living from non-living? It is very necessary to understand them.

कर्मणाभि भान्ति देवा: परत्र कर्मणैवेह प्लवते मातरिश्वा।

अहोरात्रे विदधन् कर्मणैवातन्द्रितो शश्वदुदेति सूर्य्य:॥

Means—‘Do you know why do the gods and goddesses shine with the undecaying illumination in the heaven? Why does the air remain in motion day and night? Why is there consciousness and pulsation in them? Why does the Lord Sun continue making day and night from several ages with uninterrupted speed? Why are all—this Nature, this world, this society this great universe—are functioning?’

Its sole reason is ‘Action’ means activity. In other words all are engaged in action day and night, every minute, every moment. They don’t stop even for a moment. They never take rest. All the animates and inanimates of the world are engaged in action. The whole universe is active.

This world is the field of action. There is no place here for the inactives and idles. The only way to achieve metaphysical, divine and spiritual pleasure and peace is to continuously going on doing something. Remain busy in work. The work must be truthful.

 

It was nothing but a little delay a fierce accident

The speed of the train was very fast. There was a turn just infront at a distance and onward there was a junction station. Where the two trains running together could collide and break to pieces. The conductor was a little late in detaining one train, He was thinking that this train would have reached the other main rail line before the next train arrives on the main rail line. Oh! suddenly on the next rail line also, the engine of the other train was seen coming exactly at the same time. The speed was very fast. The signal was down. Within a moment both the running engines collided fiercely and the dreadful accident took place. The whole atmosphere was resounded with the pathetic cries of thousands of passangers. A number of lives were lost and a number of families were ruined. Some were crushed and some lost their legs and hands many were wounded badly. It was a great loss of life and property.

What was the reason behind all?

Behind this accident there was only one man. It was a little carelessness of that man; a little laziness! It was a little delay in giving the signal. His momentary laziness became the cause of several deaths.

The junior army was bit late in reaching

The event is related to the great war of France. A big war was being fought out fiercely. The troops of the force were on attack with the speed of wind on the enemy one after another. The battle of bloodshed and butchering continued for eight hours. The soldiers of the next side of the hill were dedicated active in their defensive role. Both armies had already exhausted badly. If they had fought once more but the last they would have won. A very strong force in aid had been summoned. Every moment the junior army were being waited. The winner side was now confident of the victory. They were now fully confident of the aiding force to arrive in time. So they converted their reserve force of self-protection also into attacking force, and they had begun to fall upon the enemy coming out from the hidden places of the hill. They were confident that the aiding force would join them and they would be victorious.

But what ill! The aiding force did not arrive in time. The curious eyes were waiting for them every moment in the hope of their arrival. The captain of the troop named Grauchi did not reach in time. What was the result? Do you know?

The royal force had to face defeat. In the famous war of WaterLoo Nepoleon was badly defeated. He was arrested as a prisoner in the jail of St. Halina and died as a prisoner.

Ultimately why did it happen so? Napoleon was extraordinary expert in war skill. He had won many indomitable wars. His experience of war fighting was unique. There was not his least fault in losing the war.

The mistake was that his one Marshal assistant had reached a bit late with his force for aid and had become the cause of a great warrior’s defeat.

Would that! They had been a bit earlier!

In the business field, a famous firm was struggling against bankruptcy. This firm had a big permanent capital deposited in California. They were expecting the payment of the money to them in a certain period. If that money is in hand, the credit of the firm, the reputation of its owners and their future prosperity was safe.

But the hammer of destiny! The crooked circular motion of destiny! After one week, the next week and so on the days passed but the gold was not available to them from there.

At last, that unfortunate the last day also came to reach. When the firm had to pay many bills of big amounts at any cost. Now, the debt had increased the last limit, yet the reputation of the firm owners was giving a semblance from the thin curtain of hope. They were hopeful that they would be surely getting the payment of money from the safe fund of California to make the payment of the increased emergency amount.

Just in the early morning by cablegram a forceful demand was made to send the amount without any delay.

Everyone was fully hopeful that there would be no carelessness and the deposited money would be available before any objection.

But ill luck! Very shocking! When the steamer reached, it came to knowledge that the money had reached late and till then, this steamer had already been driven away from there.

The next steamer came with one and half times more than the total increased amount, for the bankrupt firm but oh! Till then, the firm had been declared bankrupt. Due to a bit delay, its credit and the reputation of the owners had been fully ruined.

Its reason was that the senders of the money support had made a bit delay in sending the money. Would that! They had sent the money a bit earlier, their credit, repute and honour would have been saved.

An innocent was hanged

A criminal was sentenced to death with the charge of murder. He was being brought away for hanging. He had faced a wicked murderer being compelled of the circumstances. The situation was to do or die before him. That courageous person did defeat that wicked but now, there was the charge of murder on him.

Law is blind. Whosoever comes under its approach anytime gets punishment certainly.

The public was in favour of this man. There were hundreds of prayers in his favour sent to acquit him showing him mercy. The public was in his favour and all had the full expectation that one day before the execution, the order of his acquittal would be served certainly. Even jailer was confident that the prisoner would be released.

But the morning approached in the wait of the order. The time was running very fast and the black faced death having opened its dreadful jaws, was approaching him to swallow.

The last moment reached. The preperations of hanging him were being made; even then, everyone was hopeful of the Govt. order to release him. A man remains alive till the last moment with the support of the bright light of hope.

Probably, the Govt. messenger must be bringing the release-order. Just to come! Came now! But none came. The criminal was taken on the platform for execution. His face was covered with the black cloth like black death. The down bolt was pressed.

Now the dead body was hanging fluttering. The soul had gone away, the lifeless body was shaking in air. Just at the very moment a horse rider was seen coming with a fast speed. Everyone’s eyes were concentrated towards him. He was the royal messenger. With the release order of the prisoner. Riding the horse madly he was coming. The release order was there in his hands which he showed to the agitated mob raising his hands from a distance.

But Oh! He had reached a little late. A little hurry could save the life of a man. It was the only mistake that the messenger to bring the release order had reached the emergency spot a little late.

All these events clear a very important formula of life and that is that we must be very careful about the binding of time. Never get delay or show laziness in the fulfilment of duty.

A little delay may cause the death of hundreds of men. The repute of the years may go to dust. The pleasure, prosperity joy, peace may vanish.

The people remain thinking of moral teaching, doing the work of the highest sublimity; remain postponing for the next day to the extent that by postponing that high resolve fades away.

How short is the five minutes time; but the right use of the same may change the course of life. To be back or get delay, may cause a great loss.

If we want to develop any noble quality in our character, that is the punctuality. Let life run according to the needle of a watch. Let us make our life regular and never remain lazy. The work should be done at the right time. We should shape our life regular, planned and according to definite contour. The usefulness of life is possible only in spending the time mostly in higher works according to rules. There is nowhere irregularity in the course of time. The universe, the regents, the earth and the sun, the moon all the rest eclipses and stars are in the movement with the motion of time. The creation cannot function by the disorder of time. In the entire system of creation this rule is implemented. Then, why only you, should be irregular?

 

Let us not be mentally thief

Smt. Vinona Bohara is an Indian M.B.B.S. lady doctor. She had visited Geneva (Switzerland) recently in connection with her study. She is expressing her opinion about the labour class of the Western countries.

‘I found that the labourers there have a high sense of honesty. I have seen them working at such places where there is no officer or any contractor rebuking them for any dullness in work to superwise their work; The labourer will start doing the work at the right time whether the work is a very simple work of merely digging a pit. He will do the work with full concentration for eight hours—neither a single minute less nor a single minute more. Even the sweeper comes by his car and having cleaned the road he goes away. In the countries like Sweden and Norway the living standard of a truck driver is very high; because he earns much more than the labourers here due to his honesty. I have noted it that if the wages are so high there, they have the habit of doing the work with great zeal, honesty and sincerity also. If anyone’s purse is lost, they don’t deviate from their morality for such a small thing; they return it as it is. Here, we always cry of ‘Dharm-Dharm; we maintain the religious clothes outwardly to prove our religious tendency and mind, paste the sacred mark on the forehead and garland in the neck. There is the practical religion. In every day-to-day life there is the religion of honesty. I saw them nowhere telling a lie for very simple things in general. We indulge ourselves in deceit just coming out of the temples. They live the life of Christianity. Their conduct is based on the principles of morality. Their religion is practical religion. Their religion is the practice of morality in conduct. The real strength of any country can be measured by the practical behaviour in righteousness. The practical form of religion is considered the worship of God by them.
