This conclusion is the eye-opener to all of us. In reality, a man may be very honest and true outwardly, but if he is not so in his daily routine of life, he should be called verily a thief.

He who is not true to his work mentally is a kind of thief. Not to steal any other one’s object but in spite of not even taking the object of others, but if there is desire in the mind to get it, if his mind is tempted for it, really he is committing the act of theft. Not to speak ill of other even, but to think ill of him—is brutish and sin.

Outwardly such a man may not be considered the victim of punishment but he is a culprit before his soul and gets its punishment also in any form.

One who is outwardly a thief is a thief; but one who is thief in his mind is a double thief. Firstly, he has the mentality of theft, secondly he shows himself honest outwardly. He is in practice of deceiving others. The practical thief may give up his habit of committing theft to some extent due to some reasons but immune of state rules a mental thief remains always the real thief.

 

This is the best means for a pleasant life

If in mind the old tragic memories are active it is better to forget them. Unpleasant matters must be forgotten. To forget them is as necessary as to remember the noble things. If the useless old dry grass are grown in the fields you root out them. The mean, the agitating, jealous, painful memories are just like those old dry grass which spoil the purity of the orchard of innerself. They decay the productive energy. By remembering the mean, worrying feelings again and again, we create a mental hell around us and remain suffering from the sorrow and pain in our past tragic memories.

It is wise to disband our mind from such tragic concerns. When we disband our mentality from there, it is certain that we will be free from the hell. Forgetfulness has a very auspicious impact. As soon as we are detached from the memory or imaginary fear of pain, sorrow and remorse, we start moving onward towards light from the darkness. So long as a man’s mind is full of tension, sorrow, disease, pain, fear etc., its prowess does not reveal out. Our divine auspicious endowment remains crippled.

Pt. Ramlal Pahada’s opinion is quite reasonable—‘Whenever the ominous feelings are created in your mind, it is wise to disband and remove them from your mind then and there. It is very difficult to forget weakness, helplessness, inferiority, fear and pain; but to remember God is easy.............If we crush the imaginary bindings, the God will support. Just when we turn our mind towards Him, He supports us in a wonderful invisible way. We remain even unaware of it.’

A famous doctor of America writes in his article named ‘Medical Talk’—‘After the experience of years I have come to conclusion that There is no other medicine more effective than ‘Forget’, to be free from worry and anxiety, He writes—‘If you want to be healthy by mind and conduct then forget all the things concerning ill health.’

In the daily routine of life don’t remain peering being involved with triffling worries. Forget them. Don’t grind them in your mind. Don’t tame it in your innerself or imperceptible, throw it out of your innerself and forget it. Remove it out of your memory.

I do agree that someone your ‘own’ has hurt you. He has hurt your heart. It may be possible, he might have not done it knowingly, and suppose he has done so deliberately will you then remain engaged in mental conflict with it? Will this worried mental condition lessen your mental hearings? O Brother! Forget those painful unpleasant episodes. Don’t pay heed to them and concentrate your mind to the auspicious noble deeds. Don’t allow the net of worries of the old bitter memories to be weaved. Forget your pains, sorrows and sufferings. Who is there deprieved of sorrows and sufferings? Forget and detach your concentration from there; fix your glance towards hope having removed it from worry, join your mind with pleasure turning it from bitterness.

Whatever the wounds of hatred, hostility, jealousy, ill will etc., are there in your mind, are being festered and they are creating poison in your own mind, body and spirit. Why do you commit suicide with this poison? Why don’t you enjoy the life? Then, why not to throw off all these matters out of your mind and heart, wash them away from your heart? You will see that by standing on the bright side of life, such a purity will welcome you that your mind and body will become completely pious and healthy; why are you committing suicide with your own hands to think of your agonies again and again? Perhaps, you don’t know about them. That is why I tell you—Forget the worries, remorses, the bitter experiences from the surface of memory.

‘What should we do at the time of great hardships, miseries? What should we do when we are loaded by the burden of the mountain of miseries, when someone has planned to ruin us and someone very close near and dear to us has entered the jaws of death, on such occasions when our wound is very deep and fatal? Should we forget them also, make them beyond memory? Yes, certainly, forget them also. It may be slowly and slowly but forget them also. Here, is your welfare. In future, you will get more and more pleasure and peace.’

Neither listen to nor talk of sorrow, worry, and disease. Listen to and talk of only health, joy and love, peace and fraternity and compassion. You will see that you have health, joy, love and peace—everything.

Now, I tell you on behalf of my own experience, take it granted that it is not very difficult at all to be free from sorrows. It is very easy. It will take some time to make the habit in the beginning, it may be possible that some hurdles might be created, but when the habit is formed, instantly you will dismiss even the biggest worries in a joke and you will become such an expert in forgetting that the problems, making the life poisonous and miserable, will disappear just coming before you. This world will appear pleasant and joyous to you and no wicked feelings of sorrow, scarcity, pain, suffering will exist in your mind.

Learn to forget. If the health of body and peace of mind is your desired object, then learn to forget. The best means to get rid of worry is to forget.

Don’t peep into the past with mournfal sight. Make the progress of present and future wisely. This is only in your hand.

 

Hindu religion gives importance to the useful elements of life

In Hindu religion the useful deeds have been valued

There are hundreds of religions in the world. They have their different base and different recognitions. When we compare these religions with the different recognitions of ‘Hindu Sanatan Dharm’, we find one thing very important that Hindu religion stands on the theory of ‘Utilitarianism’. The ancient Hindu thinkers, meditators, scholars and the preceptors have filled their long experiences, deep study, minute vision and observation and original useful thoughts in Hindu religion, only the useful and beneficial matters have been given place in the religion.

Wereas in other religions, the moral substances, recognition and customs and traditions are not clear in meaning and purpose, but at the same time, every moral recognition in Hindu religion has its meaning, purpose and usefulness. There are some useful substances hidden behind them.

This religion gives no importance to any outer hypocrisy and false show. There is the priority given to health and healthy thinking everywhere.in it. Such useful proverbs and beneficial hymns are in plenty here which form the healthy mind, healthy body and a developed society. In our ancient books, specially in the Vedas, the Supreme Lord and His worship and devotion, the evolution of spiritual power, the character formation, moral conduct, self-restraint, association of virtuous persons like useful subjects for the individual practice have the valuable priority including the consideration of all round development of the society and nation. Many very useful elements like marriage, happy domestic life, woman’s grace, the preclusion of demerits, health and healthfulness, prohibition of vices, etc., and other many useful elements have been included in religion, where there is only gain and gain.

Hindu religion is the way of life, useful in all respects

The Hindu intellectuals have remained desirous that those elements, duties, the ways of worship, hymns, exercises, customs and traditions recognitions, the views and thoughts should be included in religion so that the progress and evolution of man and society in all respects—individual, social, physical and spiritual might continue till the end of life. The Hindus might be healthy, long-lived, self-restraint, developed and progressive in all respects in the world. Whatever they thought proper, useful and beneficial for the human life, they included it in the religion, so that the Hindus as a whole should adopt them certainly and go on taking its advantage. There has been the priority of the benefit of scientific outlook in the social conduct of Hindu religion, in all the sixteen ceremonial rites, different functions and festivals. In the idols of gods the support of symbology has been taken. Each and every god has been named with some occult symbolic meaning. The symbolic meaning is hidden in the incarnations also.

In the ancient time, the awakened public understood the methods of Hindu-worship, the hymns of the Vedas, gods, goddesses, festivals, idols, and the religious books. The Vedic spells were used to be on the tongues of the Public, the divine language like Sanskrit was our mother-tongue. But it is a matter of great regret that our entire religious knowledge has confined to a few learned men because of the inability to understand Sanskrit language. The public fail to understand Sanskrit. So useless blind-faiths, false notions, foolishness, imbecility, have entered the field of religion which are needed to be rooted out from the public mind.

What are the ordains of our religion from the utility and beneficial point of view. What are benefits from rites and rituals? This is a long subject. Here only a few conducts, rituals and festivals can be discussed from the point of view of their utility.

The useful element for health in Hindu religion

Hindu religion considers the healthy body as the root of the entire religion. The man of healthy body only can lead a moral life in real sense and only he can enjoy the pleasure of the full span of life and provide the full benefit to the society. What will a weak, sick, deformed man devoid of health understand the secret meaning of religion?

So, here, human life has been confined in the limit of one hundred years.

Spend the energy of life restraintly—

शतं जीव शरदो वर्धमान:।

(Atharvaved 3/11/4)

Means—‘O the Hindus! Live for one hundred years., a progressive and prosperous life. This life potency has been blessed to you to spend very carefully. Spend the energy of your life so wisely and restraintly, that you may live for one hundred years. You should not have the loss of energy before the time.’

Make your body strong

स्वयं वर्धस्व तन्वं।

(Rigved 7/8/5)

Means—‘Build your body strong constantly. Only in a strong body, the strong spirit dwells. It is he only who can fulfil all the moral duties. If the body is not strong, in fact there is nothing. The physical strength must be increased for a progressive life, never forget it.’

अश्मानं तन्वं कृधि।

(Atharvaved 1/2/2)

Means—‘Make your body strong like stone. Only the strong body can bear the hard moral life. He who is weak, deprived of potency, helpless and feeble, falls down on the path of morality. By labour and desire only, the body becomes strong for the morality.’

वर्च आ धेहि मे तन्वां सह ओजो वयो बलम्।

(Atharvaved 19/37/2)

Means—‘If you want righteousness, delivernance, to make this life fruitful, then, go on increasing lustre, courage, vigour, life-force and the growth of energy.’

Body is the Temple of God

This body of yours is not only the lump of flesh and bones, not any mean and hateful object, not ignorable, but this is the holy temple of God. God, Himself exists there in the form of soul. On account of the presence of God, it is the most sacred. It needs full care and look after. Considering your body as the holy God-temple, look after it and protect it under the careful watch. The protection of body is the first priority of our religion.

Some are alway engaged in looking after, increasing the strength and building the body—It is not at all right. Only the body goes on developing and mind, soul and knowledge are neglected, then perversity is created. This perversity must be given up. Making alert from this it has been written—

दृंहस्व मा ह्वा:।

(Yajurved 1/9)

Means—‘Do become strong but not uncontrolled at all. Improve your health, but don’t torture a weak with your strength. Don’t indulge in vices, mind it.’

Remain alert in edibles

In the Hindu religion, edibles and non-edibles have been given the top priority. Non-edible objects (as eating meat, wine, eggs, smoking, stale objectes, heavy, intoxicating edible, gluttony) are totally prohibited. It has been said—

विश्वं समत्रिणं दह।

(Yajurved 1/36/14)

Omnivores (without considering edibles and non-edibles) burn themselves in the fire of diseases. They suffer the pain of the hell even on this earth. The fools, having no consideration of edibles and non-edible, remain sick and short-lived.

स्वादो पितो मधो पितो वयं त्वा ववृमहे अस्माकमविता भव॥

(Yajurved 1/187/2)

Means—‘A Hindu should eat such food which is sweet, tasteful, prepared by the Ayurvedic method. A progressive man should take that vegetarian food, which protects the potency of life having eradicated the diseases. The spicy, pungent, stale meat, eggs and pungent intoxicating meals are abominable.’

Our meal should be such as may expand our wisdom, talent, age and vigour, constantly.

Sun and wind also like God

Here, we should get up early in the morning and being fresh from usual body routine, offer water to the Sun. This is considered the part of our religion. It is most beneficial for health and long life. It has been said—

यदद्य सूर उदितेऽनागा मित्रो अर्यमा सुवाति सविता भग:॥

(Samved 1351)

‘Early in the morning, the life giving air is unpolluted before sun-rise. So, leaving the bed early in the morning, in Brahma-Muhurta let us breathe in the freshness of life-giving breeze. It improvers our health and healthfulness remains stable and it causes the gain of wealth.’

उत वात पितासि न उत भ्रातोत न: सखा स नो जीवातवे कृधि॥

(Samved 1841)

‘Air is life, providing healthfulness. So, leaving the bed early in the morning, we should take breath in the cool breeze of early morning regularity. It gives us pleasure like father, brother and friend.’

Celibacy has been given more importance

ऋजीते परि वृङ््धि नोऽश्मा भवतु नस्तनू:।

सोमोऽअधि ब्रवीतु नोऽदिति: शर्म यच्छतु॥

(Yajurved 29/49)

Means—‘Just as a man builds house on the earth and resides in it, in same way this body is the house of the embodied soul. So, always keep it, healthy, freedom from any disease by maintaing celibacy, eating the food combining with purity and simplicity and self-restraint. To keep the body healthy is moral.’

इमं जीवेभ्य: परिधिं दधामि मैषां नु गादपरोऽअथमेतम्।

शतं जीवन्तु शरद: पुरूचीरन्तर्मृत्युं दधतां पर्वतेन॥

(Yajurved 35/15)

‘The God has blessed the mankind with the long life of more than one hundred years. So, he should lead the life of celibacy with control and may not die untimely.’

देवैर्दत्तेन मणिना जङ्गिडेन मयोभुवा।

विष्कन्धं सर्वा रक्षांसि व्यायामे सहामहे॥

(Atharved 2/4/4)

‘Let us keep away the evil thoughts and the germs of all the diseases, sucking blood, by physical exercise and maintain our energy safe in our body by celibacy. May we remain in practice of celibacy and physical exercise, both!’

Celibacy protects semen, this semen is life. The loss of semen or potency is death. After the birth of an issue, it has been considered proper even for the married people to maintain the life of celibacy. The protection of semen is religion. All the sense-organs remain under control by virtue of it.

The science of morning-bath

The purity of mind and soul comes by the purity of body. By washing the body with water the inner peace and balance is created. The inner and outer germs are destroyed. As a result, there is the gain of appearance, lustre, vigour, age, healthfulness, greedlessness, the damage of ominous dreams, penance wit and purification—all these ten merits. The Hindus have given the top priority to bath. This is the means of the outer purity of the body. In our religion, to bathe in the Ganges, Yamunaji, Godavari, Saraswati, Narmada, Sindhu, Kaveri, etc., rivers is considered the part of religion. While bathing, the Hindu devotee remembers these rivers. These rivers are situated in all the four corners of India. Thus, the attempt has been made to maintain the integrity and emotional unity of India. There are chemical qualities also in the water of these rivers, which provide health as well as long life, our outer and inner are purified.

The science of bath at sacred place of pilgrimage

There is the provision of several Hindu holy places of pilgrimage in the Hindu religion. These sacred places are situated in all the four corners of India. There are some pilgrimages situated on the places at hills and mountains. There is a very pleasant and healthy atmosphere of Nature. On those moutntains there are very useful medicinal herbs and fresh air. The sun-rays create purity here. The sacred places of pilgrimage are situated mostly on the banks of the Ganga-Yamuna rivers. In the water of the Ganga there is the mixture of many qualitive effective chemical elements. It is very curative for the body and the health. The curative rays of the sun, moon and stars have also the chemical effect on these sacred places. In the old age, by the movement on the sacred places of pilgrimage we have a sufficient walk, we get fresh air and it solves the purpose of exercise also. The life of an old man extends to one hundred years. He gets a spiritual atmosphere to live.

The purity of Basil-leaf

In the plant of basil there is the chemical quality to maintain the health, to cure from the diseases and to make the effect of poisonous germs ineffective. In the Malaria fever it kills the poisonous germs and purifies the surrounding atmosphere. Due to its scent the diseases don’t come near us. At the time of death, the basil-leaf in the water of the Ganga river is made to drink. There is a conviction that it removes the obstacles of death. The modern scientists are making researches on the chemical qualities of basil-leaf. The doctor’s conclusion is that by the use of this nectareal plant the mucus is removed, it cures the obstacle of the urine, it sets right the function of digestive system and purifies the blood. The basil-leaf is very useful and effective in curing from breathing problem, Pneumonia, cold-fever, the urine-infection. The clever Hindus gave place to this plant in Hindu religion to give its benefit to the people.

The scientific view in the water of the Ganga

The Hindu caste has considered the means of Self-purification to go to take a bath in the holy Ganga river on different occasions of the festivals, but from the Ayurvedic and Scientific point of view, it appears that this clean and fresh water that emerges from the high mountains, is very useful and beneficial for the nourishment of the body. The water of the Ganga has wonderful power of the growth of strength in the body, it is beneficial for the patients like a tonic. We feel energy in our body after drinking in this icy water and by bathing in this water, the diseases of indigestion, fever, Tuberculosis, Asthma and sprue etc., disease are cured. All the diseases related to our head and skin are cured. The water of the Ganga is never polluted by the germs of how long days it may be.

Hindu religion is a beneficial religion

There are some recognitions mentioned above, where the scientific outlook of Hindu Dharma is clear. Not only one but there are numberless recognitions in Hindu religion which are based completely on the scientific principles, which are directly beneficial to us for our health, youthfulness and in the worldly gain in addition to the spiritual gain. There is a rule of definite conduct from morning till evening and in fulfilling these definite rules there is gain after gain. All our recognitions and entire convictions as—the simple and pure food, the science of remaining silent, the prohibition of eating the market-food objects, fast and Ekadashi vow, fast on particular dates, the benefit of drinking cow-milk the science of the lamp lighted with ghee, the consideration of direction while sleeping, the concept of next world and the science of untouchability etc., are purely based on science. We ought to obey these rules with full conviction and zeal seeing its benefits. By following it, this will give us moral benefits besides direct benefit to health and worldly gain.

 

Mother Lakshmi should never be insulted with your hands

The Hindu seers of the highest truth are famous for symbology. They have made such symbols for gods and goddesses which are the source of original thoughts and auspicious feelings to the common people. Our all the three goddesses—Saraswati, Durga and Lakshmi are the three symbols. It is a matter of great regret that we are forgetting its meaning day by day. Saraswati is the symbol of knowledge, Durga is the symbol of strength and Power and Lakshmi is the symbol of wealth and prosperity.

The inclusion of purity in wealth

The goddess Lakshmi is the symbol of wealth power. According to Indian culture and from the point of view of Hindu religion, goddess Lakshmi is the presiding deity of wealth-power. By her grace, the economic prosperity is gained.

The Hindus are extremely farsighted. What suits them useful, they make it the part of religion and include purity, sanctity, divinity, proper utilisation, supremecy and restraint in it.

To give the wealth the form of the goddess means to bring purity in it. We consider wealth to sacred power of the society. The wealth has been given the form of Lakshmi so that it may be used to lead the society on the moral path, to assist the backwards to advance and to fulfil the divine performances. The true meaning of the worship of the Goddess Lakshmi is to use the riches for the upliftment of the society, individual and the nation and its auspicious deeds. That should be spent in the social welfare. Only then, there is the usefulness of money. This is called the worship of goddess Lakshmi.

Lakshmiji is the symbol of Indian economy. In the use of money whatever the alertness should be observed is included in the worship of the Goddess Lakshmi. They who misuse the money, insult mother Lakshmiji evidently.

Make the proper use of money

If any domestic virtuous Hindu accepts wealth in the form of Lakshmiji, he should make the proper use of money. We realise the power of money at every step in the modern age. By its proper use we can serve the public at large. Let some basic principles of life suggested by the Indian thinkers be kept in mind. Having the consideration of wealth, truth, justice and public welfare in mind, the earning should be made by moral means and it should be spent in the common interest of the public—

उतो रयि: पृणतो नोपदस्यति।

(Rigved 10/117/1)

Means—‘The wealth of the charity donators never decreases, it multiplies more and more.’

The money invested in virtuous deeds is secured like the capital deposited in the banks. To use this capital in getting the public rest houses built, in opening the libraries, to start water kiosk, in getting the trees planted, in opening the new schools, in establishing the charitable hospitals, in managing the water for the animals, in managing the work of cleanliness in the villages, granting scholarships for the perspicacious students are the infallible means of the goddess Lakshmi’s worship and service. These virtuous deeds are to uplift the society higher. According to our interest and economic reach let the work of charity and service be decided.

The money spent in the advancement/uplift of the poor people is fruitful like worship. Money is not to be hoarded but to be spent in the public interest. It has been said—

अदित्सन्तं दापयतु प्रजानन्।

(Atharvaved 3/20/8)

Means—‘Remain inspiring even the misers to donate constantly.’

It is not only sufficient to remain confined to himself in doing the noble deeds. It is your moral duty; you should inspire your other close friends also to spend money in the pious deeds. Admonish these misers also lacking in wisdom that this money does not belong to yourself but it belongs to the whole society. Money is not to be amassed only meaninglessly but it is the means of making its good use. You, your offsprings, your family, your neighbourers, the state, the country and the whole country can be benefitted by this. It should be spent in the service of poors, penurious and the sufferers.

Always remain mindful of deservings and non-deservings

But the support should be given to those who deserve. If you support any non-deserving, he may create disorder in the society. After patient observation the service should be given to the men of noble conduct. It is said in the Shastras—

रयिं धत्त दाशुषे मत्यवि।

(Atharvaved)

Means—‘Always use your discernment in charity, make the charity donations only to those who deserve.’

When you start for public welfare, scrutanize the deservings and non-deservings carefully. Think over patiently. Those who are of noble conduct and deserving and they are thriving, deserve charity donation and donate them only. The charity donated to the non-deserving leads the donator towards hell.

न पापत्वाय रासीय।

(Atharvaved 20/82/1)

Means—‘Don’t donate charity to those who don’t deserve. Don’t increase unworthfulness like drinking milk to the serpent.’

दत्तान्मा यूपम्।

(Atharvaved 6/123/4)

Means—‘The divine tradition of charity donation should not be stopped.’ The mother Lakshmi says that whatever the knowledge, vigour, ability and wealth you have, that is to donate to the sufferers in the society, continue to invest it in the interest of others throughout your life.

Watch it attentively and then come to conclude who is that person of virtuous character who needs your financial support. Don’t be mindful for the propogation of your name. The best financial support is where the donator is unknown.

This wealth and property belongs to the whole society

कस्यस्विद्धनम्।

(Yajurved 40/1)

Means—‘Whatever the property you have in your possession, it is not only you are entitled of, but it belongs to the whole nation and it should be spent in the collective interest only.’

This is the message of the mother Lakshmi that don’t grab the money. Make its proper use in the interest of the family, society and nation.

Adopt only the moral attitude in the business

न स्तेय मद्मि।

(Atharvaved14/1/57)

Means—‘Don’t use the money earned by theft. That, which is not just, where there is no honesty and labour, needs to be given up.’

इमां मात्रां मिमीमहे यथापरं न मासातै।

(Atharvaved18/2/38)

Means—‘There is the message of mother Lakshmi that you should not play trick in the originality and measurement of any object. Be accurate in the measurement of the objects in your business. Any type of dishonesty in business spoils the entire business from its root.’

The sinful business seems to shine for a few days but ultimately it ruins even the capital amount. The mother Lakshmiji says—

प्र पतेत: पापि लक्ष्मि।

(Atharvaved 7/115/1)

Means—‘Give up the money earned through foul means. Money earned with hard labour, perserverance and pious feeling and with the mentality of service, stays long with the man.’

A man remains happy and mentally contented only with the sacred earning of hard labour and truthfulness.

The money should be earned for the expansion of virtues

The virtues and wealth are related to each other. The business of those who suffer from the mentality of jealousy, hostility, aversion, greed, is ruined.

The Indian sages have given much more importance to the earnings with honest and proper means with the service motive. It is said—

रमन्तां पुण्या लक्ष्मी:।

(Atharvaved7/115/4)

Means—‘This is the tested prescription that the money, earned honestly stays with the man long and causes him lasting gain and benefit. No one flourishes with dishonest earning.’

देवो वार्य बनते।

Means—‘The wealth stays with them only who are virtuous citizens otherwise in the second generation it is wasted and spoiled by the son of bad conduct. If you failed to shape your child virtuous, the plenty of property also is wasted away.’

The Indian intellectuals have always given recognition to the money earned honestly with better and sacred means. It has been the Indian concept that the moral outlook in business provides divine support. It is never found that the immoral earning has ever proved beneficial. The coming generation has finished it. So, the money should be used in evolution of virtues.

Always have the consideration of the purity of means

The mother Lakshmi gives us message of the purity of riches, the justification of means and the purity of innerself. This point of view should always prevail in human mind that he should not be blind after money, he should not adopt the means of cunningness, deceit, arrogance, hostility, hypocrisy, untruthfulness, theft, injustice and other immoral means, he should not be entangled with the demoniac vices.

On account of the impurity of wealth, greed and fraud the behaviour of brothers is guileful, the master and servant are not in harmony, the shop-keeper and consumer are not in good relation. This is all due to the selfish policy of economic transactions; so these relations should be sweet.

Economy is also the most important part of wealth. This is one of the powers of the Supreme Lord. That is the means of human service and worthfulness. This property of wealth should be used for the evolution of the human greatness.

The message of the freedom from debt

Whereas on one side, the alertness from the immoral earning has been suggested, on the other side, we have been made cautious from being indebted also. Whatever we earn by moral means, we should live under our means; we should pull on accordinly. We should remain away from false show, fashion, waste of money, spendthriftness, intoxication, cinema, decoration, outer show etc.

We should have our palate under control. We should lead a restraint life according to the rules of conduct. This is the suggestion of the great persons well-versed in scriptures—

अनृणो भवामि।

(Atharvaved6/117/1

Means—‘Limit your expenditure according to your earning, Don’t become indebted even in any adverse situation. Don’t do any such work as may push you into the hell of debt.’

अनृणा: स्याम।

(Atharvaved 6/117/3)

Means—‘O the mankind! If you want to live happy and with reputation in this world; don’t do any such deed that you have to take loan.’

सर्वान् पथो अनृणा आ क्षियेम।

(Atharvaved 6/117/3)

Means—‘He who is free from debt makes progress. The man in debt decays day by day.’

The intoxication of riches is a demoniac delusion

If the foolish, those having a little knowledge and arrogants and sinners, become rich and the excess of wealth comes in their hands, this wealth becomes the cause of their downfall. Let us be alert from that side.

The demons had taken Lakshmiji under their control. So, there is shadow of demons on the wealth. The money collected in the hands of wicked and undeserving persons is invested in demoniac deeds and it is deformed. The pleasure-seeking persons, the lustful persons, having various cravings, libidinous persons, unwise persons do the unholy, dirty and immoral deeds with the money which are always worth shunning. Lakshmiji remains displeased with such works.

How it is misused when it comes to the hands of fools and immoral persons, has been mentioned in ‘Kadambari’ as such we should always remain alert and active to be escaped from them—

यथा यथा इयं दीप्यते तथा तथा दीपशिखेव कज्जलमलिनमेव कर्म केवलमुद्वमति। अनया कथमपि दैववशेन परिगृहीता विक्लवा भवन्ति राजान:, सर्वाविनयाधिष्ठानतां च गच्छन्ति। तेषां दाक्षिण्यं प्रक्षाल्यते, हृदयं मलिनी-भवति, सत्यवादिता अपह्रियते, गुणाश्चोत्सार्यन्ते। केचित्सम्पद‍्िभ: प्रलोभ्यमाना

रागावेशेन बाध्यमाना विह्वलतामुपयान्ति। आसन्नमृत्यव इव बन्धुजनमपि नाभिजानन्ति।

Means—‘The evil minded, sinners and the pleasure-seeking persons begin to engage themselves in the immoral, vicious and corrupt activities with the same speed as the speed of the growth of their riches. It creates the evil thoughts in mind just like the flame of the earthen lamp throws out only the black soot after it.’

‘If unfortunatgely any how one is caught (means—on bad influence of Lakshmiji), even the kings lose their sense and become the dwelling place of evil deeds. Their liberal mindedness is washed away, their hearts become impure, the truthfulness goes away from them and the virtues run away.’

‘Some are compelled to be out of sense in the greed of money due to the attack of the defilements (Pleasure seeking attitude, evil thoughts, violent and cruel deeds, the vicious schemes of sexuality). They fail to recognise even their friends like the man on the edge of death.’

Thus, we should remain always alert from the evils of wealth. As it has been said—

मिथ्यामाहात्म्यगर्वनिर्भराश्च न प्रणमन्ति देवताभ्य:, नाभिवादयन्त्यभिवादनाहर्ान्, नाभ्युत्तिष्ठन्ति गुरून्। जरावैक्लव्यप्रलपितमिति पश्यन्ति वृद्धजनोपदेशम्। आत्मप्रज्ञापरिभव इत्यसूयन्ति सचिवोपदेशाय, कुप्यन्ति हितवादिने। सर्वथा तमभिनन्दन्ति तमालपन्ति, तं पार्श्वे कुर्वन्ति तस्मै ददति, तस्य वचनं शृण्वन्ति, तं बहु मन्यन्ते, योऽहर्निशमुपरचिताञ्जलिरधिदैवतमिव विगतान्यकर्तव्य: स्तौति यो वा माहात्म्यमुद्भावयति।

Means—‘The evil minded rich persons of vicious mentality don’t pay obeisance to the gods even in the egotism of superiority complex.’

They don’t bow down in salutation to deserving elders and don’t stand up in their honour to see them.’

They take the sermons of the learned old man as the gabbling due to the weakness of old age.

They are displeased on teachings of the minister and consider it the defeat of their intelligence.

They are so proud of their wealth that they are in anger even on the adviser of their welfare.

They give honour, keep in their company and listen to them only who are always day and night remain busy in their flattery with folded hands and leaving their duty praise them just like their deity-God or who declare of their greatness.’

By remaining absorbed in all the above mentioned evils the mother Lakshmiji is insulted. We should keep ourselves always away from all these demerits and vices. We should not do any such evil deed that insults the mother Lakshmi with our wealth.

Lakshmiji dwells in these places

का त्वं केन च कार्येण सम्प्राप्ता चारुहासिनि।

कुतश्चागम्यते सुभ्रु गन्तव्यं क्व च ते शुभे॥

Lord Indra asked Lakshmi—‘O the charming lady! Who are you? Why and where do you come from and where will you go?

साहं वै पङ्कजे जाता सूर्यरश्मिविबोधिते।

भूत्यर्थं सर्वभूतानां पद्मा श्री: पद्ममालिनी॥

अहं लक्ष्मीरहं भूति: श्रीश्चाहं बलसूदन।

अहं श्रद्धा च मेधा च सन्नतिर्विजिति: स्थिति:॥

अहं धृतिरहं सिद्धिरहं तद‍्भूतिरेव च।

अहं स्वाहा स्वधा चैव सन्मतिर्नियति: स्मृति:॥

‘In the lotus flourished by the lustre of the sun I appeared I have appeared for the welfare of all beings, I am called by the name of ‘Padma, Padmalini, Lakshmi, Bhuti, Shree’ also. It is I who am reverence, sagacity, modesty, dignity, patience and accomplishment (Anima etc.), ‘Swaha’, ‘Swadha’ and ‘Smriti’ also.’

राज्ञां विजयमानानां सेनाग्रेषु ध्वजेषु च।

निवासे धर्मशीलानां विषयेषु परेषु च॥

जितकाशिनि शूरे च संग्रामेष्वनिवर्त्तिनि।

निवसामि मनुष्येन्द्रे सदैव बलसूदन॥

धर्मनित्ये महाबुद्धौ ब्रह्मण्ये सत्यवादिनि।

प्रश्चिते दानशीले च सदैव निवसाम्यहम्॥

‘I dwell always on the banners of the victorious kings and ahead the armies and at the place of moral persons, in the countries and cities and in the valorous victorious persons not to give in the wars and always virtuous saints, great wisdom, Brahmanhood and in the truthful, modest persons and in the charity donators.’

 

The wealth earned by righteous conduct is conducive to prosperity

Today, the price-rise is at a high pitch of voice. In every department demand to increase the income and salary to the employees is being made. We blame the time and charge the government responsible for the dearness. We consider the outer reasons the cause of our financial problems but we should realise that in most of the cases, we are responsible ourselves for the financial troubles.

The cinema owners are earning fearlessly a lot. In the market the shops of betels and cigarretes are opening daily and they are earning a good income; the English wine shops are flourishing abundantly; the spicy and fast food and cut fruits are at a large sale. The sale of fashionable objects has increased very fast. There is a bumper sale of cosmetics in the market. Thus, including them the sellers of other luxurious objects also are increasing their income by leaps and bounds.

Then, what is dearness! If really it had been the problem of price-rise, who would have purchased the above mentioned objects?

We complain of the dearness due to the expenses increased in the purchase of the objects of our fashionable attitude in the name of the price-rise. We feel difficulty in maintaining the outer pomp and show and the fashionable life. We don’t fail in the outward show. Then, we want to meet the increased unfair expenses with the unfair and without exertion earning. Really, it is we only to be blamed for our artificial needs.

The solution of the economic problems in the Vedas

In the Vedas churning of the Shastras butter is available. Our preceptors and thinkers have given the solution of our all the financial problems in a few words. In the modern context these thoughts may prove to be a good supporter for us. Just see what is written in the Vedas—

अग्निनारयिमश्नवत् पोषमेव दिवेदिवे।

यशसं वीरवत्तमम्॥

(Rigved 1/1/3)

Means—‘For the true and lasting prosperity it is necessary that we should earn our livelihood following the rules of God honestly and with self effort. It is better to let that money earned dishonesty remain far away from us. In any case, we should not possess the money earned by immoral means (as bribe, deceit, dishonesty, cheating, theft, black-marketting, adulteration or any other immoral means). To remain everlong rich you should earn your livelihood only by moral means and whatever you get, spend it in moral works (with full restraint and frugality.’

प्राता रत्नं प्रातारित्वा दधाति तं चिकित्वान् प्रतिगृह्यानि धत्ते।

तेन प्रजां वर्धयमान आयू रायस्पोषण सचते सुवीर:॥

(Rigved 1/125/1)

Means—(This is the experience proved matter that)—‘The man of moral character, who earns money with the moral conduct without laziness, protects it and enjoys it and spends it in the interest of others, the same way, lives in this world always happy.’

The mind remains always contented and peaceful with the honestly earned money. No one suffers from fears that he will be complained or the case will be lodged against him etc. Each and every paisa earned by hard labour, gives satisfaction. The money earned by immoral means causes tension to the mind—

अग्ने नय सुपथा राये अस्मान् विश्वानि देव वयुनानि विद्वान्।

युयोध्यस्मज्जुहुराणमेनो भूयिष्ठां ते नम उक्तिं विधेम॥

(Rigved 1/189/1)

Means—‘May we (living the modern clvilized life) be blessed with holy money by following the moral path having given up the crooked, wickedness forever!’

ये त्वां देवोस्रिकं मन्यमाना: पापा भद्रमुपजीवन्ति पज्रा:।

न ढूढ्ये अनु ददासि वामं बृहस्पते चयस इत्पियारुम्॥

(Rigved 1/190/5)

Means—‘Those men who don’t pray to God and perform the auspicious deeds, are empty of wit by nature. So, they remain deprived of wealth in natural way.’

पर ऋणा साबीरध मत्् कृतानि,

माहं राजन्नन्यकृतेन भोजम्।

अव्युष्टा इन्नु भूयसीरुषास,

आ नो जीवान् वरुण तासु शाधि॥

(Rigved 2/28/9)

Means—‘O the Supreme Lord! Bless me with strengths that I may get rid of the ‘Father-debt’ and the ‘Seer-debt’. (By chance, due to the adverse circumstances, if I am indebted any how, may I be able to pay it off as soon as possible with self-efforts and self-restraint!) O Lord! May I not depend on other’s earning! May I depend only on the self-earned livelihood with own labour; because it is a kind of sin! It is an untruthful behaviour I may never live on the earning of others as it is a sin. It is an untruthful behaviour. May I remain alive depending on own moral earning! May my life be strictly controlled in all respects by righteousness!’

शतहस्त समाहर सहस्रहस्त सं किर।

कृतस्य कार्यस्य चेह स्फातिं समावह॥

(Atharvaved 3/24/5)

Means—‘May the mankind earn his livelihood by the means of knowledge, wisdom, morality, ability etc., moral conduct and the materialistic means with courage and zeal!’ (He should not accept a single paisa at all by adopting the immoral means of fraud and dishonesty) and then spend this holy money in the works of social welfare (as in the construction of public inns, wells, in getting the trees planted, in the charity donation to the poors, in uplifting the backwards, in purchasing the religious literature, in providing the medicines to the poors in the hospitals and in the help of the blinds, lepers, lames, crippled and the distressed persons). That money is auspicious which is not spent in the luxuries but which is spent in the works of social welfare.

It is mentioned at a place—

यदिन्द्र यावतस्त्वमेतावदहमीशीय। स्तोतार मिद् दिधिषेय रदावसो न पापत्वाय रासीय।

(Rigved 7/32/18)

Means—‘The wealth earned by proper means in the proper way provides the man happiness and contentment in life, inner peace and balance of mind and salvation after death if it is invested in virtuous deeds. The man who spends the wealth in the sinful and vicious deeds (as in the luxurious enjoyments, fashion, drinking wine, self-interest, fulfilling the sensuous desires and in addiction of vices) insults the mother, Lakshmi. He is ruined.

Here, in our religion the immoral means have always been considered worth shunning and they have been condemned openly. None is regarded honourable and dignified on the basis of the excess of money. Even the thieves, robbers, murderers, plunderers and prostitutes have a lot of wealth. The people have become very rich with bribery and the embezzlement of government money. Hundreds of cases of deceit, fraud and embazzlement have been filed. Such immortal money is not only worthless but disastrous also. From the Hindu religious point of view, it is mean and worth abandoning.

This is the opinion of the Hindu thinkers—

न दुष्टुती मत्र्यो विन्दते वसु न स्रेधन्तं रयिर्नशत््।

सुशक्रिरिन्मधवन् तुभ्य मावते देष्णं यत् पार्ये दिवि॥

(Rigved 7/32/21)

Means—‘Money, post, property and prosperity are gained by the just conduct. The money earned by immoral means is disastrous for the prestige, honour, repute and dignity of the man who earns it.’

मोषु वरुण मृण्मयं गृहं राजन्नहं गमम्।

मृळा सुक्षम मृळय॥

(Rigved 7/89/1)

‘Man should make his financial condition strong only by hard and true labour and constant efforts so that the society as a whole may progress and proceed ahead towards the honesty and labour.

 

Let the tradition of charity continue through your hands

The Indian culture gives immense importance to the munificence and absolute truth. When our needs combining purity with simplicity are fulfilled, we should donate in charity for the welfare and progress of others. In the ancient time they were the sages, hermits, priests, Brahmans, saints and monks who were selfless and devoted to public welfare and surrendered their entire life for the welfare of human beings. They used to support and help others always. There were some who passed their entire life in imparting knowledge and study. They used to make efforts for the enhancement of the knowledge, health, efforts, co-operation, joy, comforts, wisdom, morality etc., virtues of the people through their sermons. They passed most of their time in the development of the spiritual truth in human nature. These learned and liberal saints were the institutions of living benevolence in themselves and the form of Yagya. When they were so much dedicated to the public service, the public also managed for their food, residence, clothes, bringing up their children, considering their moral duty. As today in the present time the public welfare institutions are running with the public contribution, similarily the saints and Sadhus, Brahmans also lived their life depending on the charity donation, auspicious contributions and alms etc. The character and mentality of the ancient saints and their personality used to be so higher and dignified, so sacred and holy and so pure combined with simplicity that there was no room for any doubt even in the imagination about them; because the public used to remain confident of the right use of their donations after donating them. The public did not think the need of the audit of the account. Thus, our priests, the Brahmans imparting knowledge, the Munis, sages used to manage for the all-round development of the public with the money got in the charity donation. The system of fulfilling the needs of their life by the charity donation was justified, he who has dedicated his whole life and absorbed so much in the public service, in the munificence and absolute truth that he may not even think of his individual gain, deserves to be looked after by the public.

Thus, the tradition of charity donation started. In the due course of time, the charity donation for the blinds, crippled, lame, leper, incapable of making any earning—all types of helpless persons who were not capable of earning for their livelihood, came in practice. They deserve also to accept the alms because there remains no other means for them to continue their life. In this way, the system of charity donation has been prevalent in two ways—

1. The financial aid to the saints, Brahmans, priests, preceptors, hermits was given the name of ‘Charity donation’, 2. The name ‘alms’ was given to the crippled persons, lame, disabled person, unable to do any earning. The charity donation and alms, both meant to help others. These both should be used for the enhancement of ability, benevolence, virtuous deeds, public welfare, joy and peace and purity combined with simplicity.

What does to give to others mean? The Indian tradition of charity donation is nothing but the scientific system of lending. Whatever we give to others is deposited like our secured capital. The better in charity donation is that which is given to one who suffer from scarcity. To dontate to the person who is not in need, has no importance. The money donated to the non-deserving is useless. If more food is fed to the person whose stomach is full, he will fall ill and he will drag the donator also along with him towards the downfall. According to the Indian culture the charity donation is a very noble work. He who eats his loaf of bread with distributing it to others also, never goes in the scarcity of anything. How will the hard-hearted persons, who dig their money in the earth adding to more and more, come to realise what is the mental contentment and self-satisfaction in charity donation? The self gets exhilarated. The death is the most unpleasant but to see any other one in sorrow and finding himself helpless not to help him by any way is more unpleasasnt than death even. This is unanimous opinion of all the Hindu Shastras that the total sum of human life is benevolence. We should remain devoted in the human welfare to the best of our capacity. But this donation should not be for the arrogancy, egotism, repute but for the self-redemption. It is not proper to think that I have done good to others. Charity donation does good to the donator himself. It gives us the lesson of self-control. If you don’t even donate, even then, the world will go as usual. The Lord is so generous in squandering His abundant store that even without our least support the public work will not suffer. If you don’t give, any begger will not die of hunger. Any how his food will be managed; but you will lose an opportunity of benevolence. Your liberal tendency of benevolence will be damaged and blunted. The mental evolution and the spiritual power achieved by the charity donation is not beneficial to the receiver but to the donator. To do good to others is a kind of means of our own redemption. What a big benefit we may give to anyone by supporting him with a little amount? But in comparison we do our benefit thousand times. It develops our liberal mentality. The source of joy opens.

Charity is the divine quality of spirit. The Sattvic sentiment of benevolence in whose innersense it is aroused, it turns him to be liberal and a cluster of radiance. The charity is not confined to money or food and clothes only, but labour can also be donated in charity. The true donator gives priority to the public welfare. He donates even his bones like Dadhichi for the general welfare of the mankind. Like Vyasji, he spends his entire life in the creation of virtuous books. He preaches the knowledge of weapons like Dronacharya. He originates the grammar like Panini, preaches the sermon of love and religion like Buddha. Thus, a true charity donator donates his talent, wit, ability, art, intelligence and energy according to the time and necessity of the country.

This is the discussion of the donatior’s side. Now see the next side of the receivers side who accepts the charity donation. To accept begging and charity donation is an act of a very heavy responsibility and to bear this burden is found among a very few courageous men. The scholars of Shastras have compared the alms with fire. Just as the fire should be used very carefully otherwise it can create a great havoc and loss; similarily a well consideration and better thinking is needed before accepting the alms or charity. You should remain always ready to give just double of the accepted alms or charity in return to the donator. Your needs be very limited. The effort should be made for the service, support and solving the problems of hardships of the donator or remain giving lofty sermons in the form of well wishes and blessings.

There are two purposes of charity or alms—The first purpose is that by the act of charity the donator gets self-satisfaction of sacrifice and benevolence. The second purpose is that the sages, seers and Brahmans get the opportunity to remain moderating and purifying their pride and egotism. In the ancient time, the public servants, benevolents and the saints adopted the bare position of a begger to remain free from egotism. In donating charity or alms to such beggars, the donators felt their honour and the beggars became free from egotism. This increased a strong feeling of mutual brotherhood and affection. The donator usually remained in gain more than the beggar. To give spiritual help to the strivers seeking God-realization, this system of begging had been made. In fact, this begging was proper and according to treaties of the Shastras too:

Nowadays, several lazy and idle persons, fraudulenters, wicked beggars and cheaters, taking the advantage of this profession, are in practice of cheating the people. As regards themselves, they don’t want to do any work and want to enjoy the money got without any effort. Last year, the number of beggars had gone high as fiftysix lakh. The number of real sufferers of the distress is only nominal, but mostly they are those who take the disadvantage of others labour; and in the name of morality and righteousness are engaged in the profession of begging by several types of ostentations, mean deceptive conduct and untruthful behaviour. It creates the poisonous and disasterous atmosphere in the society. By doings so there is the spread of untruthfulness, hypocrisy, false show, deceit and intoxication in the society. So, it is our duty to remain alert from such cheaters who are grabbing free money without any work in the name of morality and religion.

Its has been said in our religion—

‘दानशूरो विशिष्यते’

Means—‘That is the munificent person who is foremost among the mankind. In other words the munificent person holds the dignified position among the men in the society.’

 

Move towards divinity

Mental struggle between god and devil—In our mind there continues usually the conflict of the two contradictory feelings constantly the conflict between good and bad, truth and untruth, the struggle of gods and demons. In the Purans the description of the battles of gods and demons has been made from step to step. In every Puran on any pretext, the wars between some gods and some demons have been described again and again. What is this?

Actually, this is a kind of symbol. In the symbolic way, the effort has been made to show that the struggle between the virtuous and vicious mentalities of mankind, this struggle of gods and demons has been continuing from eternity and will continue till eternity. None is spared from it. The problem of truth and untruth is perpetual.

In the Gita, whatever the description of the holy battlefield of Kurukshetra and in the Mahabharat the description of the Kauravas and the Pandavas representing the immoral side and moral side respectively, has been made that is not limited only to the battle of arms but that is the symbolic description of the constant conflict of our innerself regarding two contradictory tendencies of truth and untruth, the virtues and vices, god and devil.

The scholars of Shastras were proved expert enough in conveying the divine knowledge to the reach of the common public. They have a hidden meaning also behind all the fables of the Purans. A wise man can easily understand this hidden meaning and can take the broad sense, hidden in it to his heart. There are two contradictory sides in all the moral fables—One is immoral and uncontrolled and the second is fully moral and restrained, one is righteous and the second is vicious, one is of the gods, the second is of devils, means the demons. The struggle of these two opposite characters have been described in the Mahabharat and the Ramayan. Both the feelings are worth reflection.

As described in the Ramayan, the army of monkeys and bears, of Rama and the army of demons consisting demons like Ravan, Kumbhkarna and Meghnad, their regular war between them and ultimately the victory of Rama, is the symbolic description of our internal mental condition. In the Mahabharat the side of the Pandavas respresents the truth, justice, ethics, honesty and theism and the Kaurava side represents falsehood, deceit, violence, injustice and dishonesty. After a long struggle between the both we find the success of the divine side.

In the ‘Adhyatma Ramayan’, the representation of God-devil war has been made more clearly. All the incarnations of the Lord are with the purpose to destroy the collected sins in the society and to establish the morality and divinity, to protect the gods and annihilate the demons. Such incarnation can be felt in innersenses of several amongst us also being incarnated from time to time.

This struggle of sin and virtue

In the innerself of the mankind both the tendencies of virtue and vice are hidden in the form of seed. When we bend towards evil, vices, untruthfulness, deceit, jealousy and violence and torture the weak and helpless or exploit others, our demoniac or devil character dominates. On the next side, when we become restrained to love, justice, truth and wisdom, our divinity gets flourished. The demoniac and divine are the two mighty forces of our mind, brain and character. These are the two tendencies—Sin and virtue of our mind are the two sides, the two aspects. Out of them one is the intoxicating black side and the second is bright snow-white pure mixed with simplicity like winter moon light.

In everyone some evil sacraments of ruthlessness and sin are present. In some persons these demonic characters are strong for a long time, and later on they are subsided and become well cultured. In the duration of passing lacs of years through the highly mean classes of births in the animal and demon classes, these demonic elements remain clinged to our soul. In the proportionate of our collected noble deeds slowly and slowly these demonic characters go on decreasing. Yet even throughout the human life they remain dominating and strong in some persons. The struggle between demon and god goes on continuing. The brutish tendencies of sin and untruth remain creating conflict and disturbing the peace of man’s mind.

In some of the men the devil mind and demoniac mentality are very strong. When the brutish mentality grows up very strong, they come to commit such vicious acts such sinful acts, intoxicating and violent deeds which remind us of the demons like Ravan and it becomes fresh in our memory. Those mean mentalities overpower them and they commit unrestrained evil deeds in their influence.

The fury of demoniac wit is mostly in two forms—1. The unrestrained dance of sexual passion, 2. The fierce blast of wrath. In addition to it, the naked demonstration of the mental agitation, intoxication, jealousy, passion and emotional fury are seen in the demons. In the momentry demoniac frenzy or mental agitation, the men of demoniac mentality happen to do such unwise deeds which result is unexpected dreadful.

The men of demonic mind spread poison in the society because by its imitation the other men are also stimulated to do evil and it awakens the vice mentality of others and the whole society is affected. The immortality starts growing, the entire atmosphere is polluted with disorder, rowdyism and unrestrained behaviour and its demonstration is seen at a broad level.

Whatever the mean mentality of rift, non-cooperation, breach, separation, narrow mind, exploitation, selfishness, violence, barbarism, plundererism, kidnapping etc., vices are seen in the society is the blackness of demonism.

Demon is very mighty

The demon and god, both are of the same appearance, of mankind. They are distinguished on demon and god on the basis of their different opposite mentality of innerself. Those elements creating wrath, hostility, clash and disturbance are called demonic elements. Those men who diffuse such vice elements of selfishness, clash, violence and disaster in the society or in the world; support deceit, hypocrisy, fraud, arrogance and tyranny; pollute the atmosphere with jealousy, hostility and hatred—really they are demons in the form of human beings. Their feature, hands,legs, mouths and head face look like man’s external appearance basically but basically they are demons. Their mind remains always running towards the brutish and demonic mentality of sexual and sensuous passion. Their speech and behaviour is always bitter.

The demonic food

The demons meal is Tamasika and Rajasika. There is no consideration of edible and non-edible in their meal. They daily use meat, wine, eggs, intoxicating objects, onion, garlic etc. By this vicious meal their brutish instincts remain overpowering them always.

One of the causes of wicked nature is the Rajasika, food also. The excess use of pickle, sauce, sour, heavy, the sweets of different types, red chillies, the drug prepared from hemp leaves and buds, hemp, Hashish, opium, wine, intoxicating drug made of opium, crude cigarette, cigarette, tobacco, soda, lemon etc., all the stimulating food objects are Rajasika. It stimulates the sexual feelings and agitation of man.

The Tamasika meal is worse than this also. There is the excess use of stale—polluted, tasteless, foul smelt, rotten, oil and the objects prepared from ghee, meat, wine and intoxicating objects in it. By eating all these types of objects man becomes wrathful, sensuous and sexual, immoral, violent, greedy, lazy and vicious. By the use of such demonic food the mind lives in the condition of greed, passion, lust, wrath and agitation.

The demonic tendencies

The mean mentality of man is called demonic feeling. It remains present secretly hidden inactive in his mind and comes out in the different repulsive, nasty mean despicable form.

Today we are observing different types of vulgarity, intoxication, dishonesty and evils in the society. The people become agitated, violent, disturbed and turbulent on the triffling matters. They feel proud of on the triffling matters. They feel proud of on the matters of no importance. They use slanderous words and quarrel. Being emotionally mad and agitated they come to clash. The suicides are generally committed in such a perturbed condition. There are the dreadful reactions of demonical frenzy. Now-a-days, daily we go through the tragic news of suicide, clash and litigations, the triffling matters are taking the giant shape. The politics has became the battlefield of groupism.

Today, the diseases, sorrow and worries have affected the society in excess. The people are dying of heart-attack even in their young age. One of the chief reasons of heart attack is the constant worry of a man. The mental evils are more in the cities than that of in the villagers. The useless thinking and tension is mostly the cause of madness. The insanity of anger and jealousy has badly covered the society.

This increasing mentality of clash and struggle is demonic instinct. This is the disasterous and mostly mentality hidden secretly in our inner mind, it is very difficult to get pleasure, peace and balance. It is this wicked character of our mind which is the root cause of all the domestic clashes, long sickness, ill-behaviour, illegal abortion, social stigma, insult, poverty, retaliation, demonic frenzy, like all the tragic diseases. Ill thoughts is almost the wickedness. Passion of sensuousness is apparently poison.

Let us proceed towards divinity

All the creatures in the form of human-beings in the world can be divided into three classes according to their virtues, action and nature—1. God, 2. man and 3. demon. All these three are similar in colour, shape, figure, like a man but their virtues, action and nature differ from one another. They are the demons who are fallen down with the point of view of thought, life, goal and food. They eat meat, keep the ill-thoughts of agitation, passion and desires in their minds. The demon remains always alert for his own selfish interest. I should grab everything, I should remain always in gain, my passions and desires should always remain fulfilled, there is no concern to others—such thoughts are there only in the men of demonic mentality. That outlook is absolutely impure.

In real sense he is the man who looks both the sides—gain-loss, liberal-miser, self and others, own and the rests, whereas he brings up the feelings of love and genrosity in his mind on one side, on the next side, he feels jealousy, hostility and hatred etc., also in his mind. Man is the bundle of weakness. He considers gain and loss and in the influence of present gain he comes to commit errors. His self-interest goads him to do otherwise. Due to impure outlook, man’s thoughts and actions turn to disaster. He remains wandering about on the lowest surface of materalism. He spoils the invaluable divine blessing like human life among the domestic, worldly and economic problems.

The feeling of divinity is great

The state of divinity is the Supreme State. By assuming the divine sentiment man becomes blessed. In this world whatever the condition has been imagined to be the source of immortality, that is included in the divine character.

In the feeling of Divinity there is the purity of Godliness. In our concept of our ideal, the Supreme Lord is the mass of Supreme higher powers. All the noble qualities of man—love, mercy, pity, friendliness compassion, courage, patience, generosity—emerge from the Supreme Lord, god is His part. Divinity is the lustre of spiritual power and holiest particle of Divine majesty.

The feeling of Divinity is the feeling of immortality. The gods don’t give any importance to this transitory body of bones and flesh. This earthly body is to be perished in a very short time. The body is born, grows up, but very soon it is perished also, but the soul is undecaying, immortal, eternal. Soul is the part of the Supreme God. The feeling of Divinity is the feeling of the spiritual supremecy. By realizing ourself the eternal spirit, by self-realization, the body does not feel the pains of death. The man considering himself god always observes with spiritual sight. He always considers that he is the soul. My real eternal form is indivisible impregnable, imperishable, endless. My soul can never decay at any cost.

The man dwelling in the higher mental sphere of divinity, thinks that he is pious, pure internally and externally both. No vicious demonic attack on him is possible.

The morality of divinity

The worshipper of divinity discarding the peity worldly outlook always watches everything with spiritual eyes. He adopts pure Sattvika nature combined with in mind, speech and action. He has no interest at all in the transitory pleasures, worldly attractions and materialistic allurements. He assumes and develops those noble and higher qualities in himself day by day which are beneficial for the public in general.

The centre of all virtues

The sentiment of Divinity only is the central point of all the spiritual and divine powers and that is the emerging point of the entire spiritual divine energy. The inner ambition of the soul is to merge into the Supreme Almighty at last by self-evolution. Our soul is nothing but verily God itself. We can plan for our spiritual evolution by developing the virtues of the soul, which is the compact of truth, consciousness and bliss.

In fact, as much as we meditate and ponder over the divine properties of the soul so much we are benefitted with the noble company of divine bodies who have reached the highest position due to their spiritual evolution, so much we reach close to the absolute truth. The ultimate goal of man’s life is to be developed in the form of Supreme Lord. Our auspicious instincts are to develop the divine virtues.

Divinity is hidden in you

Know it granted that the shadow of the divinity is present in your this body unobtainable even to the gods. You have obtained this class of birth after wandering about through numberless classes of births and rebirths. There is need of only one leap for the embodied being in this body. By this effort he can be able to bear the responsibility of absolute truth.

Such numberless great persons of divine merits have been born who are yet even today the pillars of illumination. Shivi, Dadhichi, Harishchandra, Moradhvaj, Prahlad, Buddha, etc., were gods despite their human bodies. They are immortal. These immortal persons will be always counted in the category of gods. They will always remain the source of the message of the highest knowledge, devotion, service, sacrifice, generosity to the humanity.

The theistic faith

The indomitable faith in God, reverence and faith in the eternal existence of God is the strong base like the boat to cross this ocean of the world. The Divine sentiment is the spiritual process based on theism. In the world it is he who has faith in the existence of God and spiritual support also in addition to the materialistic bases, becomes victorious. The feeling of theism is a base. By the support of theistic feeling and spiritual powers even the great miseries go away.

In the words of a great learned scholar, ‘Generally, in all the religions the existence of All-pervading and All-powerful God has been made the base of faith and devotion. When the man finds himself attached to the existence of All-pervading mighty, Divine Reality, his energy becomes so powerful that he moves ahead being balanced in spite of his mental conflicts, worldly pains, materialistic problems.

‘Firm faith in God and indomitable conviction provides mental balance and strength to the mankind.’

‘To unite ourselves to the Divine entity, seeking shelter, self-surrender and hymns have been considered the constructive form of religion. The processes of contemplations, pondering, conviction, concentration, meditation etc., have been managed for the union with the Divine entity, to gets the inspiration of strength and mental balance.’

The above mentioned words clear the significance of theistic feelings and view. By developing the theistic emotions and feelings, man gets union with the supreme powers of the spiritual world. He becomes introvert sparing himself from the mean worldly ups and downs.

Our Sanatan Dharma is based on this concept. By the means of prayer, we take advantage of establishing our close contact to this power storage. We feel excessively contented and peace in our mind after the worship of God. We become free from all mental tensions. All the great thinkers of the world have emphasized to adopt theistic view. You should also adopt it in your life and take the advantage of Divine feelings.

The feeling of devotion

There are different forms of God. There are several different idols and paintings in the form of gods; there are numberless temples of God. By awakening the devotional feeling in these idols, these temples and these paintings, the dwelling of God becomes possible. The existence of God lies in the higher feelings of devotion. The God presents Himself in the mental attitude. We get the sight of God, where we instal His idol with devotion. To centralise around the faith is devotion.

In the words of a famous thinker—‘For the faith in God, devotion is very important. In the worldly life and in the physical sphere love has its limit, when the same love becomes active in the inner sphere of self, it becomes devotion.’

The realization of that Supreme God is possible only through devotion. Devotion handsover the entire oar of this life boat to the hands of God.

What fear has he whose life is in the hands of God? He, who holds the hands of God, becomes fearless. The God illuminates his whole life.

Devotion fills our life with such a firm conviction which always follows us and supports us like armour. It is only devotion that can unite us with the spiritual truth (God). By the faith in God we unfold our divine traits and rise above the mean demonic and brutish mentality.

Develop in yourself the virtuous merits of Gods Sense of Truthfulness

Truth has the first and foremost place to awaken the divine feelings. Truth is the form of God, the untruth is demonic property. The men of Godliness always search out truth and adopt it. They always speak the truth; they make truth the base of their life, they keep false and untruth at an arm’s length.

The seer Vedvyas has given the topmost place to the truth among the divine merits. He writes that—all lofty divine propensities are included in Truth. ‘There is included non-violence and non-theiving etc., in truth. Mahatma Gandhi was such a votary of truth that he used to say that after knowing truth nothing is left to know. Well! Who needs to be guided the light of sun?’ The truth is itself illumination and itself evident. Man’s deliverance is possible only then when he comes to know the different forms of truth well and try his best to practise it in his daily life. This is the best means to proceed towards divinity.

Truth is the part of divine feelings. ‘Just while pronouncing ‘Truth’ the tongue gets a great satisfaction and peace, just while thinking the mind becomes cool; and by installing truth in heart, the heart feels cold. By being entangled with the illusory creation, this man, the immortal prince of God has become beast having fallen down from the humanity—he is suffering from the imprecation of ignoring the truth. In the whole frolicsome activities of God there is everywhere truth. Every particle of life is thirsty of ‘truth’ only. This life only means moving in the element of absolute truth we should drink nectar.

The ‘Shruti’ says—‘असतो मा सद‍्गमय’ ‘Let us move towards truth from untruth.’ All the programes of our life, the entire success, the ultimate goal is hidden in one word—that is ‘Truth’.

Brothers! Move towards truth giving up untruth, false, deceit, all these forms of evil conduct.

Just as the calf of a cow milking the udder of the mother cow, gets only milk, similarily, by the study of Vedas, nothing purer than the milk of truth is available anywhere. Truth is the ladder to heaven, just like the ship to cross the sea. There is the presentation of truth only in the Vedas. It is only truth that has been mentioned as the absolute fruit. Penance, morality and restraint—all these are included in truth.

The sense of justice

Due to the hidden wickedness and barbarism in human being different kinds of injustice are created. A man tortures another one only due to his demonic attitude.

The inner darkness creates injustice. The animals have no sense of just and unjust. Due to this downfall in our society, the injustice is spread over in the houses, families, castes, institutions and groups. The foolish men of strength are doing injustice to the wise weak. The fools are ruling the wise. This barbarism can be subsided only when we assume the divine mentality of justice in all respects.

Injustice is created by sin and immorality. The weakness invites others to do the acts of injustice. The big wild violent animals are present in the world. But they fail to dominate us due to our more strength. So, being, powerful, we should try to prevent injustice. To prevent injustice, develop your mental, physical and financial strength. Always keep it in your mind that God has to incarnate again and again to remove sin, immortality, injustice from the world.

If others oppress you, if they are unjust to you then, begin atonce to become strong. Don’t think that you are alone and bereft of means. It is better to go on following the path of justice by your noble conduct than to become stronger capitalist by adopting the sinful and immoral means. Attention! Let not your unjust hands rise on anyone.

Ultimately justice wins sentiment of generosity. It is justice which is morality.

Sentiment of generosity is a divine quality. The gods are always generous by nature. They support and co-operate everyone with the same sentiment without any discrimination of caste, creed, condition or good or bad. The narrowness cannot approach them.

Miserliness is not our spiritual quality. The spirit is generous. There is no limit of its bound. Whenever we see with the spiritual eyes, all the creatures appear verily our own and own. When we see ourself with the angle of spirit, due to considering everyone the part of God, we find our own friend, well-wisher, member of our family and brother. In everyone there is the existence of the same single spirit. With the point of view, internal unity, love and co-operation all are found included in the great quality of generosity. He who assumes generosity with broad outlook, the entire world is our own, the loss of one is the loss of all, the gain of one is the gain of all. By the mentality of generosity we remain active in the collective uplift.

The unity means by divine mentality that you should not consider yourself, body but spirit and assume the qualities of truth, justice, love, wisdom, generosity etc., which are your real endowment.

Read your innerself and findout such mean works which are not favourable to your pure, righteous element like spirit.

Do only what suits your spirit. Start giving up the works from just today which are against the dignity of your soul.

Your soul is the divine touch stone of the discriminate truth-untruth, righte-wrong, good-bad. At the time of confusion, that discriminates milk and water. Don’t make the least delay at all in growing that work or thought that creates the feeling of internal joy, happiness or self-elation even if you might be presuming any worldly loss of present either directly or indirectly—This is the straight way of self-realization.

‘In our life and actions, the divine element will certainly be visible. I am shaping my life and thus, approaching God.’ Root this thought firmly in your mind—

Our soul is the reflection of God. Basically, there is such a divine power, that inspires a divine intelligence by its influence. To realize this spirit, to develop its qualities, to obey its command should be our ultimate goal.

 

Learn the genuine use of compassion, forgiveness and punishment

There are several means of human welfare in Indian culture. The seers and sages of Hindu religion have decided the traditions of Shastras after the serious consideration of each and every aspect of human life. Our culture is full of the wish of the highest good and deliverance of even the meanest and downfallen. In the Hindu Dharma, the exhilarating messages of new hope and zeal have been given to everyone, how much lower to any extent he may be and the society has accepted him fallen down to any extent. It becomes possible only by the genuine use of these three—Compassion, forgiveness and punishment. So, its real significance should be understood well.

Kindness is justified moral of the human being. He who is in distress, crying for your support deserves your mercy. Those, who are weaker than you, who are younger than you in age, who are in pitiable condition deserve your mercy and you should be certainly kind to them. Mercy is your duty. To serve others means—You serve yourself. The complete humanity is not possible only by courage and vigour, it needs to be combined with the tender feeling of mercy also.

It is the mercy, that divine quality which is expected by God from you to support his brethren. Mercy is a very important virtue for the protection of humanity and to remove the patient’s diseases, to free the poors from poverty and to remove the distress of grieved ones. Effort should be made to hold on to it. The sphere of your mercy should continue to be extending. It should not be only for the mankind but it should include birds, animals and small insects, moths also.

But mercy also has its limit. The man who does not prosper or progress by your kindness once or twice is not a man and he is a stone. What we see in the society that a number of beggars have made begging as their profession in the pretext of mercy. This is misuse of mercy. Many other such examples will be there, which ought to be avoided.

Forgiveness is an other part of our mercy. He who misbehaves with us, or causes harm to us and becomes the cause of our trouble and loss, should be forgiven if he repents with true mind. Usually, several wicked persons become aggressive towards the path of progress after forgiveness. Human life is invaluable. So, once or twice even the guilty should be forgiven and the means of progress should be provided to him. Today in our society many neglected castes, distressed, backward persons are there who deserve our mercy and sympathy.

Society is the association of men. It consists of advanced ones and backwards both. It is only the mutual treatment of love and kindness that can run the society in right order. Co-operation is the religion of human spirit. Forgiveness provides a new opportunity to a man to improve himself.

Punishment is the last limit of our culture. The wickeds must be suppressed. In the public interest, if a wicked is punished even breaking the general rules to some extent, it is not worth abandoning. Maryada Purushottam Shri Ramchandraji had to kill Bali by hiding himself.
